# math.SP [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Patterson-Sullivan distributions of finite regular graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09779)
*Christian Arends,Guendalina Palmirotta*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 该论文在有限正则图（finite regular graphs）上构造了与离散拉普拉斯算子（discrete Laplace operator）本征函数相关的Patterson-Sullivan分布，通过其在相空间（phase space）上的边界值定义。这些分布与图上的伪微分演算（pseudo-differential calculus）定义的Wigner分布密切相关，并建立了与移位空间（shift space）上测地流（geodesic flow）的转移算子（transfer operator）产生的不变Ruelle分布之间的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在建立有限正则图上量子混沌（quantum chaos）相关分布的离散类比。具体动机是通过边界值方法构造Patterson-Sullivan分布，并探索其与Wigner分布和不变Ruelle分布之间的关系，从而为紧双曲曲面（compact hyperbolic surfaces）上的已知结果提供离散对应。

Method: 方法包括：1）在有限正则图上通过离散拉普拉斯算子本征函数的相空间边界值构造Patterson-Sullivan分布；2）利用配对公式（pairing formula）建立这些分布与不变Ruelle分布之间的关系；3）通过图上的伪微分演算定义Wigner分布，并分析其与Patterson-Sullivan分布的关联。

Result: 主要结果证明了Patterson-Sullivan分布与Wigner分布密切相关，后者在量子混沌研究中自然出现。通过配对公式，进一步建立了Patterson-Sullivan分布与由移位空间上测地流转移算子产生的不变Ruelle分布之间的关系。这些关系为Anantharaman-Zelditch和Guillarmou-Hilgert-Weich在紧双曲曲面上获得的结果提供了离散类比。

Conclusion: 该研究成功地在有限正则图上构造了Patterson-Sullivan分布，并建立了其与Wigner分布和不变Ruelle分布的明确关系。这些结果为连续双曲几何背景下的量子混沌理论提供了离散图论框架下的对应物，扩展了相关数学工具的应用范围。

Abstract: On finite regular graphs, we construct Patterson-Sullivan distributions associated with eigenfunctions of the discrete Laplace operator via their boundary values on the phase space. These distributions are closely related to Wigner distributions defined via a pseudo-differential calculus on graphs, which appear naturally in the study of quantum chaos. Using a pairing formula, we prove that Patterson-Sullivan distributions are also related to invariant Ruelle distributions arising from the transfer operator of the geodesic flow on the shift space. Both relationships provide discrete analogues of results for compact hyperbolic surfaces obtained by Anantharaman-Zelditch and by Guillarmou-Hilgert-Weich.

</details>

# nlin.AO [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Simple mathematical model for a pairing-induced motion of active and passive particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2501.00411)
*Hiroaki Ishikawa,Yuki Koyano,Hiroaki Ito,Yutaka Sumino,Hiroyuki Kitahata*

Main category: nlin.AO

TL;DR: 本文提出一个描述二维系统中主动与被动粒子配对诱导运动的简单数学模型，通过数值模拟观察到直线、圆周和蛇形运动，理论分析再现了基于自推进强度变化的运动分岔现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于作者先前的工作[Ishikawa et al., Phys. Rev. E 106 (2022) 024604]，旨在建立描述主动和被动粒子配对诱导运动的数学模型。

Method: 方法基于以下假设：主动与被动粒子通过线性弹簧连接，主动粒子沿当前速度方向自推进，被动粒子受到主动粒子的排斥作用；采用数值模拟和理论分析相结合的研究方法。

Result: 数值模拟观察到三种运动模式：直线运动（straight motion）、圆周运动（circular motion）和蛇形运动（slalom motion）；理论分析成功再现了直线与圆周运动之间的分岔现象，该分岔取决于自推进强度的大小。

Conclusion: 该简单数学模型能够描述主动-被动粒子对的复杂运动模式，特别是揭示了自推进强度对运动模式分岔的关键影响，为理解此类系统的动力学行为提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We propose a simple mathematical model that describes a pairing-induced motion of active and passive particles in a two-dimensional system, which is motivated by our previous paper [Ishikawa et al., Phys. Rev. E \textbf{106} (2022) 024604]. We assume the following features; the active and passive particles are connected with a linear spring, the active particle is driven in the direction of the current velocity, and the passive particle is repelled from the active particle. A straight motion, a circular motion, and a slalom motion were observed by numerical simulation. Theoretical analysis reproduces the bifurcation between the straight and circular motions depending on the magnitude of self-propulsion.

</details>

# math-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Spectral transitions in some Rabi models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08834)
*Grzegorz Świderski,Lech Zieliński*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了量子拉比模型（quantum Rabi models）中离散谱向连续谱的转变，运用从属理论（subordinacy theory）检测并定位了三种模型的本质谱（essential spectrum），证明了这些模型在参数全范围内不存在奇异谱（singular spectrum）且本质谱内部不存在本征值（eigenvalues）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探讨量子拉比模型中离散谱向连续谱的转变现象，特别是针对强度依赖拉比模型（intensity-dependent Rabi model）、各向异性双光子拉比模型（anisotropic two-photon Rabi model）以及双光子拉比-斯塔克模型（two-photon Rabi-Stark model）的谱结构分析。

Method: 采用从属理论（subordinacy theory）作为主要分析方法，用于检测和定位三种量子拉比模型的本质谱（essential spectrum），该方法适用于参数的全范围分析。

Result: 研究成功确定了所有考虑模型的本质谱（essential spectrum），并证明了两个关键结果：这些模型不存在奇异谱（singular spectrum），且本质谱内部不存在本征值（eigenvalues）。

Conclusion: 该研究系统分析了三种量子拉比模型的谱特性，通过从属理论（subordinacy theory）完整刻画了它们的本质谱结构，证实了在这些模型中离散谱向连续谱转变的特定性质，为理解量子拉比模型的谱行为提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We consider the transition from discrete to continuous spectrum which occurs in some quantum Rabi models. The subordinacy theory is used to detect and locate the essential spectrum of the intensity-dependent Rabi model, the anisotropic two-photon Rabi model, and the two-photon Rabi-Stark model for the whole range of parameters. The absence of a singular spectrum and the absence of eigenvalues in the interior of the essential spectrum are proved for all models considered.

</details>


### [4] [State integral models and the tetrahedron equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09230)
*Junya Yagi*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证明了一类状态积分模型（包括Teichmüller TQFT的边缘表述）中，分配给四面体的玻尔兹曼权重满足四面体方程（tetrahedron equation），其中四面体的二面角（dihedral angles）充当谱参数（spectral parameters）的角色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在研究形状化伪3-流形（shaped pseudo 3-manifolds）上状态积分模型（state integral models）的代数结构，特别是探讨这些模型中四面体权重与四面体方程之间的关系。

Method: 研究聚焦于一类状态积分模型，包括Teichmüller拓扑量子场论（Teichmüller TQFT）的边缘表述（edge formulation），分析分配给四面体的玻尔兹曼权重（Boltzmann weight）的数学性质。

Result: 证明了该类模型中四面体的玻尔兹曼权重满足四面体方程，并揭示了四面体的二面角在方程中作为谱参数发挥关键作用。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了形状化伪3-流形上状态积分模型的四面体权重与四面体方程之间的深刻联系，为理解这类拓扑量子场论的代数结构提供了新的视角。

Abstract: It is shown that for a class of state integral models on shaped pseudo 3-manifolds, including the edge formulation of Teichmüller TQFT, the Boltzmann weight assigned to a tetrahedron solves the tetrahedron equation. The dihedral angles of the tetrahedron play the role of spectral parameters.

</details>


### [5] [On Fermi's model for the scattering of a slow neutron from a bound proton](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09372)
*Domenico Finco,Raffaele Scandone,Alessandro Teta*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了费米于1936年提出的一个两粒子系统模型，证明了极限吸收原理，建立了定态散射理论，并在玻恩近似下推导了费米的散射截面公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在分析费米（Fermi）在1936年提出的一个特定两粒子系统模型，该系统由中子（neutron）和束缚在谐振势中的质子（proton）组成，中子-质子相互作用采用δ-势（δ-potential）形式。

Method: 针对该模型哈密顿量（model Hamiltonian），研究者证明了极限吸收原理（Limiting Absorption Principle），并建立了定态散射理论（stationary scattering theory）。

Result: 研究成功证明了该系统的极限吸收原理，描述了其定态散射理论框架，并最终在玻恩近似（Born approximation）下推导出了费米的散射截面公式（Fermi's formula for the scattering cross-section）。

Conclusion: 该工作为费米原始模型提供了严格的数学基础，包括极限吸收原理的证明和散射理论的完整描述，并在玻恩近似下恢复了费米的散射截面公式，从而完善了对该历史模型的理论理解。

Abstract: We consider a model Hamiltonian, introduced by Fermi in 1936, describing a two-particle system made of a neutron and a harmonically bound proton, where the neutron-proton interaction has the form of a $δ$-potential. For such Hamiltonian we prove the Limiting Absorption Principle and describe the stationary scattering theory. Finally, we derive Fermi's formula for the scattering cross-section valid in the Born approximation.

</details>


### [6] [Weak-Coupling Limit of the Lattice Nonlinear Schrödinger Integral Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09522)
*Felipe Taha Sant'Ana*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了量子晶格非线性薛定谔模型（等价于各向同性XXX海森堡自旋链）在弱耦合极限下的基态积分方程。通过匹配渐近展开方法，揭示了晶格方程的双重奇异性，并建立了与玻色-爱因斯坦分布的对偶关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解量子晶格非线性薛定谔模型在弱耦合极限下的行为。与连续Lieb-Liniger方程不同，晶格方程具有双重奇异性：驱动项和积分核在κ→0时都退化为δ函数，这需要新的分析方法。

Method: 采用匹配渐近展开（matched asymptotic expansion）方法，将问题划分为三个区域：内部区（inner）、外部区（outer）和边界层（edge）。通过Wiener-Hopf分解分析边界层，并利用与圆形盘电容器Love积分方程的精确对偶性。

Result: 重标度内部解的傅里叶变换精确对应于玻色-爱因斯坦分布（Bose-Einstein distribution），峰值密度以对数方式发散且常数C可通过解析和数值方法确定。从边界层分析中识别了瞬子作用（instanton action），并预测了复现超越级数结构（resurgent transseries structure）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功解析了量子晶格模型在弱耦合极限下的基态性质，建立了晶格方程与统计物理分布的对偶关系，并为理解量子系统的超越级数结构提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study the ground-state integral equation of the quantum lattice nonlinear Schrödinger model -- equivalently the isotropic Heisenberg XXX spin chain with spin $s = -1$ -- in the weak-coupling limit. Unlike the continuous Lieb--Liniger equation, whose driving term is a constant, the lattice equation is doubly singular: both the driving term and the integral kernel degenerate into $δ$-functions as $κ\to 0$. We develop a matched asymptotic expansion with three regions -- inner, outer, and edge. The Fourier transform of the rescaled inner solution is exactly the Bose--Einstein distribution, and the peak density diverges logarithmically with a constant $C$, which we determine analytically via two independent routes and confirm numerically. An exact duality with the Love integral equation for the circular disc capacitor yields the total density expansion. We prove an identity for the inner energy, allowing us to obtain the ground-state energy per site. From the Wiener--Hopf factorisation of the edge boundary layer, we identify the instanton action and predict a resurgent transseries structure.

</details>


### [7] [Pseudo-Riemmanian Lie algebras with coisotropic ideals and integrating the Laplace-Beltrami equation on Lie groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09535)
*A. A. Magazev,I. V. Shirokov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文识别了一类李群上的左不变伪黎曼度量，使得拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米方程可降阶为一阶偏微分方程并获得精确解。方法基于非交换积分技术和轨道方法，通过广义傅里叶变换将方程简化，并揭示非局部对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于寻找一类特殊的左不变伪黎曼度量，使得拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米方程能够显著简化。这类度量由李代数中满足特定正交关系的交换理想定义，旨在超越传统变量分离方法的限制。

Method: 采用基于轨道方法和广义傅里叶变换的非交换积分方法。通过将拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米方程简化为可显式积分的一阶线性偏微分方程，并利用逆变换揭示原始方程的非局部对称算子。

Result: 成功识别了满足正交条件 $\mathfrak{h}^\perp\subseteq\mathfrak{h}$ 的度量类别，并获得了精确解。在四维非幺模群的 $(2,2)$ 签名度量示例中，传统变量分离法不适用，但非交换方法仍能获得显式解并揭示预测的非局部对称性。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一种处理特殊伪黎曼度量的系统方法，将拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米方程降阶为一阶方程。所得对称算子通常是积分-微分型的，与先前研究中出现的多项式对称性形成对比，扩展了可解方程类的范围。

Abstract: We identify a class of left-invariant pseudo-Riemannian metrics on Lie groups for which the Laplace-Beltrami equation reduces to a first-order PDE and admits exact solutions. The defining condition is the existence of a commutative ideal $\mathfrak{h}$ in the Lie algebra $\mathfrak{g}$ whose orthogonal complement satisfies $\mathfrak{h}^\perp\subseteq\mathfrak{h}$. Using the noncommutative integration method based on the orbit method and generalized Fourier transforms, we reduce the Laplace--Beltrami equation to a first-order linear PDE, which can then be integrated explicitly. The symmetry of the reduced equation gives rise, via the inverse transform, to nonlocal symmetry operators for the original equation. These operators are generically integro-differential, contrasting with the polynomial symmetries appearing in previously studied classes. The method is illustrated by two examples: the Heisenberg group $\mathrm{H}_3(\mathbb{R})$ with a Lorentzian metric and a four-dimensional non-unimodular group with a metric of signature $(2,2)$. In the latter, classical separation of variables is not directly applicable, yet the noncommutative approach yields explicit solutions and reveals the predicted nonlocal symmetry.

</details>


### [8] [Intertwining Markov Processes via Matrix Product Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09928)
*Rouven Frassek,Jan de Gier,Jimin Li,Frank Verstraete*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究将矩阵乘积算符（matrix product operators）推广到非平衡态，用于实现一维边界驱动马尔可夫过程的对偶变换，并在对称简单排他过程（symmetric simple exclusion process）中精确构造了对偶算符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对偶变换（duality transformations）能揭示看似不同模型之间的等价性，但传统方法主要关注平衡态系统。本研究旨在将矩阵乘积算符推广到非平衡态，以处理边界驱动的马尔可夫过程。

Method: 引入非平衡态的矩阵乘积算符（matrix product operators）推广，通过广义交换关系（generalised exchange relations）实现两个马尔可夫过程的交织。在具有不同非平衡边界的对称简单排他过程（symmetric simple exclusion process）中精确构造了这些算符。

Result: 发现非平衡边界与满足Liggett条件的平衡边界对偶，表明当利用对偶算符时，吉布斯-玻尔兹曼测度（Gibbs-Boltzmann measure）能够捕捉非平衡物理。这一原理通过物理应用进行了说明。

Conclusion: 该研究成功实现了非平衡态下的全局对偶变换，为理解边界驱动系统的非平衡物理提供了新工具，并展示了平衡态测度在特定对偶变换下对非平衡现象的刻画能力。

Abstract: Duality transformations reveal unexpected equivalences between seemingly distinct models. We introduce an out-of-equilibrium generalisation of matrix product operators to implement duality transformations in one-dimensional boundary-driven Markov processes on lattices. In contrast to local dualities associated with generalised symmetries, here the duality operator intertwines two Markov processes via generalised exchange relations and realises the out-of-equilibrium duality globally. We construct these operators exactly for the symmetric simple exclusion process with distinct out-of-equilibrium boundaries. In this case, out-of-equilibrium boundaries are dual to equilibrium boundaries satisfying Liggett's condition, implying that the Gibbs-Boltzmann measure captures out-of-equilibrium physics when leveraging the duality operator. We illustrate this principle through physical applications.

</details>


### [9] [A complete classification of 2d symmetry protected states with symmetric entanglers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09959)
*Alex Bols,Wojciech De Roeck,Michiel De Wilde,Bruno de O. Carvalho*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证明了对于可由对称纠缠器从直积态制备的二维量子自旋系统对称保护拓扑态，其分类由上同调群H³(G,U(1))完全描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维量子自旋系统的对称保护拓扑态（symmetry protected topological states）分类问题尚未完全解决。虽然已有猜想认为这类态由上同调群H³(G,U(1))分类，但该分类的完备性仍是一个开放问题。

Method: 研究限制于可通过对称纠缠器（symmetric entangler）从直积态（product state）制备的对称保护拓扑态。在此约束条件下，采用数学证明方法验证分类的完备性。

Result: 证明了对于所研究的态类别，由上同调群H³(G,U(1))进行的分类是完备的。这一结果支持了先前关于对称保护拓扑态分类的猜想。

Conclusion: 在有限对称群G和特定制备约束条件下，二维量子自旋系统的对称保护拓扑态分类可由上同调群H³(G,U(1))完全描述，解决了该分类问题的完备性疑问。

Abstract: We consider symmetry protected topological states of 2d quantum spin systems, with a finite symmetry group $G$. It has been conjectured that such states are classified by the cohomology group $H^3(G,U(1))$, but the completeness of this classfication is an open problem. We restrict ourselves to symmetry protected topological states that can be prepared from a product state by a symmetric entangler. For this class of states, we prove that the classification by $H^3(G,U(1))$ is complete.

</details>

# physics.hist-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [10] [Does Quantum Cosmology Predict the Age of the Universe?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09699)
*Álvaro Mozota Frauca*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 本文论证量子宇宙学中的时间问题使其方法存在缺陷，无法保留经典宇宙学中宇宙年龄等物理预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子引力中的时间问题使正则方法（canonical approaches）存在缺陷，本文旨在研究该问题如何影响量子宇宙学，并得出相似结论。通过研究宇宙学案例，其简单性能使讨论更清晰且技术性更低。

Method: 研究经典宇宙学模型，该模型描述两个自由度——尺度因子（scale factor）和标量场（scalar field）相对于时间变量的演化。在量子化模型后，分析时间变量消失的问题。同时分析量子引力和量子宇宙学文献中否认时间变量物理意义的关系性立场（relational positions）。

Result: 量子化后时间变量消失，导致经典模型中"宇宙年龄为138亿年"等物理上有意义的预测在量子宇宙学中丢失。作者论证了这些时间变量在经典宇宙学中具有物理意义，并反对否认其物理意义的关系性立场。

Conclusion: 宇宙年龄是经典宇宙学模型的物理预测，但在量子宇宙学中缺失，这表明此类方法存在问题。量子宇宙学未能保留经典模型中具有物理意义的时间预测，使其方法存在根本性缺陷。

Abstract: The problem of time of quantum gravity has been argued to make canonical approaches unsatisfactory. In this article I study how it affects quantum cosmology and reach the same conclusion. The advantage of studying the cosmological case is that its simplicity makes the discussion much clearer and less technical. The classical models I will be concerned with describe how two degrees of freedom, the scale factor and a scalar field, evolve with respect to a time variable. After quantizing the model, this time variable just disappears, and I argue that this is problematic. Indeed, this variable in the classical model allowed us to make claims like `the universe is 13.8 billion years old' and I will argue that these claims are physically meaningful predictions that are lost in quantum cosmology. I will analyze some of the relational positions in the quantum gravity and quantum cosmology literature that tend to deny the physical meaning of time variables and I will argue against them for the case of classical cosmology. I conclude that the age of the universe is a physical prediction of classical cosmological models, that it is missing from quantum cosmology, and that this should make us suspect that there is something wrong with this sort of approach.

</details>

# hep-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [11] [Quark-diquark effective mass formalism for heavy baryon spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.01037)
*Binesh Mohan,Rohit Dhir*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在夸克-双夸克有效质量形式下，对重味重子进行了全面研究，预测了两种互补场景下的重子质量，结果与实验和格点QCD数据高度一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过夸克-双夸克有效质量形式（quark-diquark effective mass formalism）系统研究重味重子（heavy flavor baryons），以理解其质量谱并验证理论框架的有效性。

Method: 采用夸克-双夸克有效质量形式，在两种互补场景下预测重子质量：夸克-夸克相互作用图像（Scenario I）考虑所有可能的夸克-夸克关联；夸克-双夸克相互作用图像（Scenario II）采用固定自旋-味道双夸克构型，将重子视为有效夸克-双夸克系统。方法包括估算组分夸克质量、双夸克质量和超精细相互作用，并引入质量依赖的结合能项以考虑短程色电效应。

Result: 分析表明结合能在描述重-重双夸克（heavy-heavy diquarks）中起关键作用。预测的重子质量在粲夸克和底夸克领域均与实验数据和格点QCD（lattice QCD）结果表现出极好的一致性。

Conclusion: 夸克-双夸克有效质量形式能够有效描述重味重子质量谱，结合能项对重-重双夸克系统的描述至关重要，理论预测与现有实验和格点QCD结果高度吻合。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive study of heavy flavor baryons within a quark-diquark effective mass formalism, formulated using the effective masses of quarks and diquarks inside baryons. We predict the masses of $J^P=\frac{1}{2}^+$ and $J^P=\frac{3}{2}^+$ states under two complementary scenarios: the quark-quark interaction picture (Scenario I) and the quark-diquark interaction picture (Scenario II). Scenario I considers all possible quark-quark correlations, while Scenario II employs fixed spin-flavor diquark configurations, treating the baryon as an effective quark-diquark system. Using current experimental data, we estimate constituent quark masses, diquark masses, and hyperfine interactions, and include a mass-dependent binding energy term to account for short-range chromoelectric effects. The analysis shows that the binding energy plays a crucial role in describing heavy-heavy diquarks. The predicted baryon masses show excellent agreement with experimental and lattice QCD results across the charm and bottom sectors.

</details>


### [12] [Exotic hadrons associated with $b$-quark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09315)
*Xinchen Dai,Sen Jia,Alexey Nefediev,Juan Nieves,Chengping Shen,Liming Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文综述了底夸克（b-quark）相关奇异强子态的研究优势，重点分析了Belle/Belle II和LHCb实验在探索Z_b、X_b、Y_b态及粲偶素类似态方面的贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相较于粲偶素类似态（charmonium-like states），底夸克相关的奇异强子态（exotic hadrons）在研究多夸克现象本质和强相互作用动力学方面具有独特优势。底夸克质量较重使得理论计算（特别是基于有效场论和势模型的方法）在底偶素（bottomonium）领域更为可靠且可控。

Method: 研究主要基于两大实验平台：Belle和Belle II实验利用清洁的e⁺e⁻对撞环境和高亮度探索底夸克相关奇异强子态；LHCb实验则利用大型质子-质子对撞数据集，通过B介子和Λ_b重子衰变道广泛研究重味多夸克态。

Result: 实验研究覆盖了Z_b、X_b和Y_b态等底夸克相关奇异强子态，以及B衰变中的粲偶素类似态。相关现象学解释（phenomenological interpretations）也在文中得到综述。

Conclusion: Belle/Belle II和LHCb实验为探索底夸克相关奇异强子态提供了理想平台，这些研究有助于深入理解多夸克现象和强相互作用动力学，理论计算的可靠性在底偶素领域得到增强。

Abstract: Compared to charmonium-like states, exotic hadrons associated with $b$-quark offer distinct advantages for exploring the nature of multiquark phenomena and the dynamics of the strong interaction. Due to the heavier bottom quark mass, theoretical calculations, particularly those based on effective field theories and potential models, tend to be more reliable and under better control in the bottomonium sector. With its clean $e^+e^-$ collision environment and high luminosity, the Belle and Belle II experiments are ideally suited to explore these exotic hadrons associated with $b$-quark, including $Z_b$, $X_b$, and $Y_b$ states, and charmonium-like states in $B$ decays. Utilizing the large proton--proton collision dataset, the LHCb experiment has conducted extensive investigations of heavy-flavor multiquark states through $B$ and $Λ_b$ decay channels. The relevant phenomenological interpretations are also reviewed.

</details>


### [13] [Extracting freeze-out conditions in beam energy scan via functional QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09336)
*Yi Lu,Christian S. Fischer,Fei Gao,Yu-xin Liu,Jan M. Pawlowski*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过比较功能量子色动力学（functional QCD）理论计算的守恒荷涨落与重离子碰撞实验提取的质子数累积量，自洽地确定了化学冻结点参数，并预测了冻结线上的峰度，在约5 GeV碰撞能量处发现了可能指示QCD临界终点的峰结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 守恒荷涨落为高质量理论结果与重离子碰撞精密测量之间提供了重要联系。研究旨在通过比较功能量子色动力学（functional QCD）理论计算的守恒荷涨落与实验提取的质子数累积量，自洽地确定化学冻结点参数。

Method: 采用功能量子色动力学（functional QCD）方法计算最低阶重子数敏感度（baryon number susceptibilities）的比值，并与重离子碰撞实验中提取的质子数累积量（proton number cumulants）进行比较。

Result: 理论结果与实验数据在每个碰撞能量下的特定温度和化学势处交汇，这指示了相应的冻结点（freeze-out point）。从这些自洽确定的冻结点参数中，研究提取了冻结线上峰度（kurtosis）的预测，并与现有实验数据达成定量一致。

Conclusion: 在约5 GeV碰撞能量处，研究发现的峰度峰结构可能指示量子色动力学（QCD）的临界终点（critical end point）。尽管比较的是重子与质子这两种不同粒子，但仍获得了定量一致的结果。

Abstract: Fluctuations of conserved charges provide a link between high quality theoretical results and precision measurements of heavy ion collisions. We compare results for ratios of the lowest order baryon number susceptibilities from functional QCD approaches to proton number cumulants extracted from experiments. We find that they meet at a specific temperature and chemical potential for each collision energy. This is indicative of the respective freeze-out point. From this self-consistent determination of the freeze-out parameters we extract a prediction for the kurtosis on the freeze-out line. We find quantitative agreement with experimental data where available, despite comparing apples (baryons) with oranges (protons). At a collision energy around 5 GeV, our kurtosis exhibits a peak structure indicative of the critical end point of QCD.

</details>


### [14] [JLab and J-PARC for the J/{\ensuremathψ} Production at the Threshold](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09622)
*Igor I. Strakovsky,Jung Keun Ahn,William J. Briscoe,Misha G. Ryskin,Axel Schmid*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究利用007、CLAS12和GlueX实验的J/ψ阈值测量数据，扩展了J/ψ-质子散射长度（α_{J/ψp}）的现象学确定，并验证了不同实验方法的一致性。研究还支持重矢量介子-核子散射长度的微扰QCD预测，并期待J-PARC实验解决矢量介子-核子散射长度趋势的谜题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是利用新的实验数据（007和CLAS12的阈值测量）扩展先前基于GlueX数据的J/ψ-质子散射长度现象学确定。同时验证不同实验方法之间是否存在系统性差异，并为理解矢量介子-核子散射长度趋势提供实验支持。

Method: 方法基于三个实验数据集的阈值测量：007实验的$γ~p\to p~J/ψ\to p~(μ^+μ^-)$过程、CLAS12实验的$γ^\ast~p\to p~J/ψ\to p~(e^+e^-)$过程，以及先前GlueX实验的$γ~p\to p~J/ψ\to p~(e^+e^-)$数据。通过现象学分析确定J/ψ-质子散射长度（α_{J/ψp}），并比较不同方法的一致性。

Result: 结果显示所有三个J/ψ数据集之间具有良好一致性，未发现不同方法之间存在系统性差异。微扰QCD（perturbative QCD）预测支持重矢量介子-核子散射长度的现象学确定。矢量介子-核子散射长度趋势$|α_{Υp}| \ll |α_{J/ψp}| \ll |α_{φp}| \ll |α_{ωp}|$与"年轻矢量介子"假设（"young vector meson" hypothesis）一致。

Conclusion: 结论表明新实验数据成功扩展了J/ψ-质子散射长度的现象学确定，验证了不同实验方法的一致性。即将到来的J-PARC阈值测量$π^-~p\to n~J/ψ\to n~(l^+l^-)$将有助于解决矢量介子-核子散射长度趋势的谜题，进一步验证理论假设。

Abstract: New threshold measurements for $γ~p\to p~J/ψ\to p~(μ^+μ^-)$ by 007 and $γ^\ast~p\to p~J/ψ\to p~(e^+e^-)$ by CLAS12 allow us to extend the previous phenomenological determination of the J/\ensuremathψ-proton scattering length, $α_{J/ψp}$, using GlueX threshold data for $γ~p\to p~J/ψ\to p~(e^+e^-)$. The agreement between all three J/\ensuremathψ data sets shows no indication of systematic differences between methodologies. Furthermore, perturbative QCD predictions support the phenomenological determination of heavy vector meson-nucleon scattering lengths. Upcoming J-PARC threshold measurements of the reaction $π^-~p\to n~J/ψ\to n~(l^+l^-)$ will help resolve a puzzle regarding the trend of the vector meson-nucleon scattering lengths, $|α_{Υp}| \ll |α_{J/ψp}| \ll |α_{φp}| \ll |α_{ωp}|$, which is consistent with the ``young vector meson'' hypothesis.

</details>


### [15] [Extracting the speed of sound of QCD from transverse momentum fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09647)
*Mubarak Alqahtani,Tribhuban Parida,Jean-Yves Ollitrault*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究从ATLAS实验数据中提取夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）的声速，通过分析超中心铅-铅碰撞中横向动量分布，并校正探测器低动量粒子损失和强子化噪声的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在从重离子碰撞实验数据中直接提取夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma, QGP）的声速（speed of sound），这是表征QGP热力学性质的关键参数。传统方法受限于探测器对低横向动量（low-$p_T$）粒子的探测效率以及强子化（hadronization）过程的噪声干扰。

Method: 通过分析ATLAS实验的超中心（ultra-central）Pb+Pb碰撞数据，利用粒子平均横向动量（mean $[p_T]$）随碰撞多重数（collision multiplicity）的变化来推断声速。为校正低动量粒子探测损失，引入了$[p_T]$的方差（variance）数据和最近测量的$v_0(p_T)$信息。同时开发了系统性的去模糊（deblurring）方法来消除强子化过程的噪声影响。

Result: 在假设零碰撞参数（zero impact parameter）下夸克-胶子等离子体尺寸与强子多重数无关的前提下，该研究获得声速值$c_s/c=0.496\pm 0.008$，对应温度$T=221\pm 13$ MeV。该结果与格点QCD（lattice QCD）的第一性原理计算完美吻合。

Conclusion: 研究成功建立了从实验数据提取夸克-胶子等离子体声速的可靠方法，校正了探测器偏差和强子化噪声。获得的声速值与理论预测高度一致，验证了该方法在重离子碰撞物理研究中的有效性。

Abstract: We extract the speed of sound ($c_s$) in the quark-gluon plasma from ATLAS data on the probability distribution of the transverse momentum per particle, $[p_T]$, in ultra-central Pb+Pb collisions. With an ideal detector, $c_s$ can be inferred from the rise of the mean $[p_T]$ with the collision multiplicity. In practice, however, low-$p_T$ particles escape detection, which biases the analysis. We show how to correct for this bias by using data on the variance of $[p_T]$, as well as information from the recently-measured $v_0(p_T)$. We also introduce a systematic method for deblurring the noise from the hadronization process. Assuming that the size of the quark-gluon plasma is independent of the hadron multiplicity in collisions at zero impact parameter, which is the scenario preferred both by high-energy QCD and heavy-ion data, we obtain $c_s/c=0.496\pm 0.008$ at temperature $T=221\pm 13$ MeV, in perfect agreement with first-principles calculations from lattice QCD.

</details>


### [16] [First Estimation of Model Parameters for Neutrino-Induced Nucleon Knockout Using Simulation-Based Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09778)
*Karla Tame-Narvaez,Steven Gardiner,Aleksandra Ćiprijanović,Giuseppe Cerati*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨基于模拟的推理（SBI）在微调中微子相互作用模型中的应用，通过重新分析MicroBooNE合作组开发的GENIE事件生成器配置，发现SBI算法能获得与实验数据更好拟合的参数值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 加速器中微子实验需要精确的GeV能区核相互作用模拟以确定振荡参数。当前模拟存在不足，迫使实验合作组依赖经验性调参，而机器学习技术可能为未来中微子相互作用模型调优提供强大工具。

Method: 研究基于模拟的推理（simulation-based inference, SBI）在此物理应用中的适用性，重新分析MicroBooNE合作组开发的GENIE中微子事件生成器调优配置。将训练后的SBI算法应用于原始实验数据集进行推理。

Result: 尽管SBI算法在输入调优截面预测时能紧密复现四个物理参数的采用值，但算法倾向于略微不同的参数值（在MicroBooNE指定不确定度范围内），并在原始实验数据集上获得稍好的拟合优度。训练算法还能近似模拟另一种中微子散射模拟NuWro。

Conclusion: 基于模拟的推理技术在中微子相互作用模型调优中具有应用潜力，能够处理未来模型调优复杂性的增长，为高精度中微子实验提供更有效的参数优化方法。

Abstract: To enable an accurate determination of oscillation parameters, accelerator-based neutrino experiments require detailed simulations of nuclear interaction physics in the GeV regime. While substantial effort from both theory and experiment is currently being invested to improve the fidelity of these simulations, their present deficiencies typically oblige experimental collaborations to resort to empirical tuning of simulation model parameters. As the precision requirements of the field continue to become more stringent, machine learning techniques may provide a powerful means of handling corresponding growth in the complexity of future neutrino interaction model tuning exercises. To study the suitability of simulation-based inference (SBI) for this physics application, in this paper we revisit a tuned configuration of the GENIE neutrino event generator that was originally developed by the MicroBooNE collaboration. Despite closely reproducing the adopted values of four physics parameters when confronted with the tuned cross-section predictions as input, we find that our trained SBI algorithm prefers modestly different values (within MicroBooNE's assigned uncertainties) and achieves slightly better goodness-of-fit when inference is run on the experimental data set originally used by MicroBooNE. We also find that our trained algorithm can create a fair approximation of an alternative neutrino scattering simulation, NuWro, that shares only a subset of its physics model parameters with GENIE.

</details>


### [17] [Polarization transfer in $ψ'\toψππ$: a complete spin density matrix analysis framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09858)
*Jiabao Gong,Guanyu Wang,Dongyu Yuan,Libo Liao,Yilun Wang,Jiarong Li,Xiaoshen Kang,Lei Zhang,Jin Zhang,Gang Li*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文基于自旋密度矩阵（Spin Density Matrix）形式体系，建立了描述衰变链 $e^+e^- \rightarrow ψ^\prime \rightarrow ψππ$ 中极化转移的理论框架，为在无连续背景环境下提取 $ψ$ 极化和分析其后续衰变振幅提供了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要建立一个理论框架来描述粲偶素衰变链中的极化转移，特别是 $e^+e^- \rightarrow ψ^\prime \rightarrow ψππ$ 过程，以提供在无连续背景环境下提取 $ψ$ 极化和分析其后续衰变振幅的一致基础。

Method: 发展了基于自旋密度矩阵（Spin Density Matrix, SDM）形式体系的理论框架，推导了连接 $ψ^\prime$ 和 $ψ$ 的 SDM 的显式关系，将 Cahn 的分析推广为完整的 SDM 处理。

Result: 对于主导的 $S$-波 $ππ$ 发射，SDM 被证明是完美保持的（$ρ_ψ= ρ_{ψ^\prime}$），使 $ψ$ 成为初始极化状态的理想探针；量化了 $D$-波贡献引起的偏差，并提出了同时验证框架和约束分波振幅的自洽性实验检验。

Conclusion: 该框架为提取 $ψ$ 极化和在无连续背景环境下分析后续 $ψ$ 衰变振幅提供了一致基础，并可扩展到其他强子跃迁（如粲偶素中的 $ψ' \to h_cπ^0$ 和底偶素中的 $Υ(nS) \to Υ(mS)ππ$）以及电弱过程（如 $e^+e^- \to Z^\ast \to ZH$），为从粲偶素到希格斯扇区的动力学提供了统一的极化探针。

Abstract: A theoretical framework based on the Spin Density Matrix (SDM) formalism is developed to describe polarization transfer in the decay chain $e^+e^- \rightarrow ψ^\prime \rightarrow ψππ$. Explicit relations connecting the SDMs of $ψ^\prime$ and $ψ$ are derived, generalizing Cahn's analysis into a complete SDM treatment. For the dominant $S$-wave $ππ$ emission, the SDM is shown to be perfectly preserved, $ρ_ψ= ρ_{ψ^\prime}$, rendering the $ψ$ an ideal probe of the initial polarization state. Deviations arising from $D$-wave contributions are quantified, and a self-consistency experimental test is proposed that simultaneously validates the framework and constrains partial wave amplitudes. This formalism provides a consistent basis for extracting $ψ$ polarization and for amplitude analyses of subsequent $ψ$ decays in a continuum-background-free environment. The framework extends to other hadronic transitions, including $ψ' \to h_cπ^0$ in charmonium and $Υ(nS) \to Υ(mS)ππ$ in bottomonium, as well as to electroweak processes such as $e^+e^- \to Z^\ast \to ZH$, where the same angular-momentum structure governs polarization transfer -- offering a unified probe of dynamics from charmonium to the Higgs sector.

</details>


### [18] [Jet energy loss in anisotropic plasmas meets limiting attractors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09912)
*Kirill Boguslavski,Lucas Hörl,Florian Lindenbauer*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了重离子碰撞早期各向异性等离子体中高能部分子的能量损失，计算了各向异性背景下发射胶子的平均能量变化，并与各向同性介质进行比较，发现各向异性影响通常较小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解重离子碰撞早期各向异性等离子体中高能部分子的能量损失机制，特别是各向异性背景对喷注淬火（jet quenching）过程的影响。

Method: 采用谐波近似（harmonic approximation）方法，计算了在具有各向异性喷注淬火参数$\hat q_{x}\neq \hat q_{y}$的背景中发射胶子的平均能量变化，并通过数值积分评估结果。

Result: 研究发现各向异性对平均发射胶子能量的影响通常较小，并推导了简单的经验公式来估计这种影响。结合QCD动力学理论模拟提取的喷注淬火参数，发现介质长度依赖性表现出极限吸引子（limiting attractors）的特征。

Conclusion: 该研究将喷注部分子的能量损失与各向异性等离子体的普适动力学联系起来，表明可以通过外推到零耦合和无限耦合来获得极限吸引子特征。

Abstract: We consider the energy loss of a high-energy parton in the early anisotropic plasma in heavy-ion collisions. Working in the harmonic approximation, we compute the change in the mean energy of an emitted gluon in the presence of an anisotropic background, characterized by anisotropic jet quenching parameters $\hat q_{x}\neq \hat q_{y}$. Evaluating the resulting integrals numerically, we compare with isotropic media, and obtain a simple pocket formula to estimate the impact of anisotropy on the mean emitted gluon energy, which is generally small. We then combine our results with the values of the jet quenching parameter extracted from QCD kinetic theory simulations and show that the medium length dependence of this mean energy loss exhibits the characteristics of limiting attractors, which can be obtained by extrapolating to zero and infinite coupling. Our study thus relates energy loss of jet partons to universal dynamics of anisotropic plasmas.

</details>


### [19] [Sensitivity of Jet Observables to Molière Scattering Off Quasiparticles in Quark-Gluon Plasma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08776)
*Zachary Hulcher,Arjun Srinivasan Kudinoor,Daniel Pablos,Krishna Rajagopal*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究在混合模型（Hybrid Model）中完整计算了喷注部分子与夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）准粒子间的莫里哀散射（Molière scattering），分析了这种硬散射对喷注形状、碎裂函数及子喷注分布的影响，发现光子标记喷注（photon-tagged jets）对探测QGP微观结构具有特殊敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma, QGP）在长尺度表现为强耦合液体，但在短尺度下存在类夸克和胶子准粒子（quasiparticles）。喷注部分子（jet partons）与QGP准粒子间的莫里哀散射（Molière scattering）可作为探测QGP微观结构的重要探针，但此前混合模型中仅考虑了软动量交换和喷注激发的尾迹（wakes），缺乏对硬散射过程的完整计算。

Method: 在混合模型（Hybrid Model）中实现了喷注部分子与QGP准粒子间莫里哀散射的完整计算，包括喷注偏转和被踢出的反冲部分子（recoil parton）激发。散射后的喷注和反冲部分子继续在QGP中传播，经历能量损失、动量转移、激发尾迹，并可能发生进一步再散射。

Result: 莫里哀散射会加宽软降角（Soft Drop angle）R_g和喷注宽度（jet girth）g的分布，特别是当包含显著软于光子的喷注时。光子标记喷注（photon-tagged jets）通过光子能量选择事件，减轻了包容性喷注测量的选择偏差（selection bias），增强了对罕见大角度散射的敏感性。

Conclusion: 该研究为喷注部分子与QGP准粒子间的硬散射提供了独特的模型无关实验特征（model-independent experimental signatures），为探测QGP微观结构开辟了新途径。光子标记喷注成为特别敏感的探针，有助于揭示QGP中准粒子的存在和性质。

Abstract: Quark-gluon plasma (QGP) is a strongly coupled liquid when viewed at length scales of order the inverse of its temperature and longer. However, when it is probed at short enough length scales, asymptotic freedom mandates the presence of quark- and gluon-like quasiparticles. Partons in jets can trigger perturbative, high momentum-exchange $2\rightarrow2$ Molière scatterings off quasiparticles in the medium, making jets useful probes of the microscopic structure of QGP. Prior to this work, soft strongly coupled momentum-exchanges between jet partons and the QGP droplet produced in a heavy-ion collision, as well as the wakes that jets excite in the droplet, had been accounted for in the Hybrid Model of jet quenching. Here, we present a full calculation of Molière scattering off a QGP quasiparticle which results in the deflection of the jet parton and the excitation of a parton from the thermal medium that recoils after being kicked, and describe how it is implemented in the Hybrid Model. The scattered jet and recoil partons continue to propagate through the QGP, lose energy and momentum, excite wakes, and may further re-scatter. Using the Hybrid Model, we study how Molière scatterings impact jet shapes and fragmentation functions, the Soft Drop angle $R_g$, jet girth $g$, and observables that focus on the number and angular distribution of subjets within jets. We demonstrate that photon-tagged jets provide a particularly sensitive probe: selecting events by the photon energy mitigates the selection bias inherent in inclusive jet measurements and enhances sensitivity to rare large-angle scatterings. We find that Molière scatterings broaden both the $R_g$ and $g$ distributions when jets significantly softer than the photon are included. Our results point the way towards distinctive model-independent experimental signatures of hard scattering of jet partons off quasiparticles in QGP.

</details>

### [20] [Quotient Quiver Subtraction -- Classical Groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08774)
*Sam Bennett,Amihay Hanany,Guhesh Kumaran*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文扩展了商箭图减法（quotient quiver subtraction）方法，利用含O5平面的IIB型膜构造，实现了对具有酉规范群（unitary gauge groups）的箭图中Sp(n)、SO(n)及耦合半超多重态（half-hypermultiplet）的Coulomb分支等距子群的规范化（gauging）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 商箭图减法原是一种简单的组合学方法，用于对3维N=4超对称箭图规范理论（3d N=4 quiver gauge theories）的Coulomb分支等距子群（Coulomb branch isometry subgroups）进行规范（gauging）。本文旨在将该方法扩展到更广泛的规范群类型。

Method: 采用含O5平面（O5 planes）的IIB型膜构造（Type IIB brane constructions），将商箭图减法扩展至规范Sp(n)、SO(n)以及耦合半超多重态的Coulomb分支等距子群。该规范化过程不再仅仅是减法操作，还需额外步骤改变图类型（graph type）。

Result: 该方法成功应用于为某些高维SCFT（superconformal field theories）的Higgs分支（Higgs branch）提供替代构造（alternative constructions），展示了扩展后商箭图减法的实际应用价值。

Conclusion: 通过引入含O5平面的IIB型膜构造，商箭图减法得以扩展至更广泛的规范群类型，为高维超共形场理论的Higgs分支研究提供了新的构造工具。

Abstract: Quotient quiver subtraction is a simple combinatorial prescription for gauging Coulomb branch isometry subgroups of 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ quiver gauge theories. This paper uses Type IIB brane constructions with $\mathrm{O5}$ planes to extend the prescription to gauge $\mathrm{Sp}(n),\;\mathrm{SO}(n)$, and $\mathrm{Sp}(n)$ coupled to a half-hypermultiplet Coulomb branch isometry subgroups of quivers with unitary gauge groups. The gauging procedure is no longer solely a subtraction -- additional steps change the graph type. The method is applied to provide alternative constructions of the Higgs branch of certain SCFTs in higher dimensions.

</details>


### [21] [A domain wall bound on anti-de Sitter vacua](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08779)
*Niccolò Cribiori,Antonia Paraskevopoulou,Thomas Van Riet*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了反德西特（anti-de Sitter）通量真空（flux vacua）中通量变化畴壁（domain wall）的张力约束，推导出反德西特半径的上限（畴壁边界），这转化为引力子质量（gravitino mass）的下限，从而实现了沼泽地（swampland）纲领中的引力子猜想和反德西特距离猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于通过通量变化畴壁来约束反德西特通量真空，建立畴壁张力与有效描述紫外截断（ultraviolet cutoff）之间的关系，从而验证沼泽地纲领中的相关猜想。

Method: 方法要求畴壁张力高于有效描述的紫外截断，由此推导出反德西特半径的上限（畴壁边界），并将其转化为引力子质量的下限。该方法在具有候选尺度层级（hierarchy of scales）的多个例子中进行测试。

Result: 结果表明，经典通量真空（classical flux vacua）和大体积情景（LVS）与畴壁边界兼容。对于赛道模型（racetrack models）和KKLT类反德西特真空（KKLT-like anti-de Sitter vacua），该边界对实现大尺度层级提出了非平凡约束。

Conclusion: 畴壁边界实现了引力子猜想和反德西特距离猜想，为反德西特通量真空的尺度层级提供了重要约束，特别是在赛道模型和KKLT类真空的构建中需要满足该边界条件。

Abstract: We consider anti-de Sitter flux vacua interpolated by flux-changing domain walls. Demanding that the tension of such a domain wall be above the ultraviolet cutoff of the effective description, we derive an upper bound on the anti-de Sitter radius, which we term domain wall bound. It translates into a lower bound on the gravitino mass, thus realizing the gravitino conjecture and the anti-de Sitter distance conjecture of the swampland program. We test the domain wall bound on several examples with a candidate hierarchy of scales: classical flux vacua, racetrack models, LVS and KKLT-like anti-de Sitter vacua. The classical flux vacua and LVS are found to be compatible with the bound. For racetrack and KKLT-like anti-de Sitter vacua, the bound poses a non-trivial constraint on achieving large hierarchies of scales.

Result: 实现了所有介子算符（meson operators）球面关联函数的精确全息匹配，成功将最小模型全息（Minimal Model Holography）嵌入到弦理论框架中。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of 2d fermions coupled to 3d Chern-Simons gauge fields. We give an holographic description of the interfaces within the A-model Topological String Theory. The model has exotic integrability properties, which allow us to propose an exact holographic match of all sphere correlation functions of meson operators. This construction embeds Minimal Model Holography in String Theory.

### [23] [A Covariant Formulation of Logarithmic Supertranslations at Spatial Infinity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08784)
*Florian Girelli,Simon Langenscheidt,Giulio Neri,Christopher Pollack,Celine Zwikel*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了渐近平坦时空在空间无限远处的渐近对称性，提出了新的辛结构和保守边界条件，扩展了BMS代数，发现了包含对数超平移的新对称性及其中心扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究渐近平坦时空在空间无限远处的渐近对称性，旨在揭示该区域未被发现的新物理信息，为在零无限远和类时无限远处考虑新可观测量开辟道路。

Method: 采用多齐次Beig-Schmidt展开，提出新的辛结构和保守边界条件，分析渐近对称性代数及其扩展，计算相关荷及其代数结构。

Result: 渐近对称性扩展了BMS代数，包含阿贝尔扇区，特别是正则对数平移和对数超平移；相关荷有限且守恒，其代数在超平移与对数超平移之间、奇异平移与正则对数平移之间允许中心扩展。

Conclusion: 新识别的空间无限远对称性编码了渐近平坦时空其他区域未揭示的新物理信息，为在零无限远和类时无限远处考虑新可观测量打开了大门，同时兼容并扩展了arXiv:1106.4045和arXiv:2211.10941的工作。

Abstract: We investigate the asymptotic symmetries of asymptotically flat spacetimes at spatial infinity. We propose a new symplectic structure and conservative boundary conditions in a polyhomogeneous Beig-Schmidt expansion. The asymptotic symmetries extend the BMS algebra by abelian sectors, notably incorporating regular log-translations and log-supertranslations. The associated charges are finite and conserved, and we show that their algebra admits a central extension between supertranslations and log-supertranslations, and between the singular translations and regular log-translations. Our analysis is compatible with, and extends, both the work of arXiv:1106.4045 and arXiv:2211.10941 : it extends the former by incorporating log-supertranslations, and the latter by allowing both parities of the log-supertranslations in the same phase space. These newly identified symmetries at spatial infinity encode novel physical information that has not been revealed in other regions of asymptotically flat spacetimes, thereby opening the door to new observables to consider at null and timelike infinity.

### [24] [All-Loop Renormalization and the Phase of the de Sitter Wavefunction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08794)
*Alexander Farren,Ciaran McCulloch,Enrico Pajer,Xi Tong*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了在德西特（de Sitter）时空中，具有平移对称性的标量场原初波函数在重整化过程中会出现量子反常，导致树图级应为纯实数的波函数产生虚部，且该虚部完全由重整化标度依赖性决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多暴胀模型的近似描述涉及德西特时空中的平移对称标量场，其树图级波函数应为纯实数。然而重整化过程中的量子反常会破坏这一性质，需要系统研究该反常对波函数虚部的影响。

Method: 基于幺正性（unitarity）、局域性（locality）、膨胀等距（dilation isometry）和邦奇-戴维斯态（Bunch-Davies state）等基本原理，在微扰理论的所有圈图阶次上分析波函数虚部与重整化标度的关系。

Result: 发现波函数虚部完全由其重整化标度依赖性决定，这一紧凑关系意味着无质量场及其共轭动量关联函数之间存在无限组关系，并在单圈阶次给出了具体示例。

Conclusion: 重整化过程中的量子反常固定了德西特时空中平移对称标量场波函数的虚部，这一发现建立了波函数虚部与重整化标度之间的基本联系，并为原初宇宙学可观测量提供了新的理论约束。

Abstract: Cosmological observables of the primordial universe are encoded in the late-time field-theoretic wavefunction. For shift-symmetric scalars in de Sitter, a good approximation for many inflationary models, the wavefunction must be purely real at tree-level. This property is violated by a quantum anomaly in the process of renormalization. As a result, we show that the imaginary part of the wavefunction is fixed by its dependence on the renormalization scale to all loop orders in perturbation theory. This follows from unitarity, locality, dilation isometry and a Bunch-Davies state. The compact relation we uncover for the wavefunction implies an infinite set of relations among correlators of massless fields and their conjugate momenta, which we exemplify at one-loop order.

</details>


### [25] [Introduction to Generalized Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08798)
*Justin Kaidi*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用渐进式教学方法，首先回顾高形式对称性（higher-form symmetries）、反常（anomalies）和离散规范理论（discrete gauge theories），然后引入(1+1)维系统中的非可逆对称性。接着讨论融合范畴（fusion categories）的基本结构，包括离散规范化和表示理论的范畴类比，最后转向(3+1)维理论中的物理应用。

Result: 讲义构建了从基础对称性概念到非可逆对称性理论的完整教学框架，涵盖了(1+1)维和(3+1)维系统中的具体应用。通过系统性的讲解，使读者能够理解融合范畴等抽象数学结构在物理理论中的具体实现。

Conclusion: 该讲义成功提供了关于非可逆对称性的自包含教学材料，系统连接了高形式对称性、反常理论、离散规范理论和融合范畴等概念，为理解现代量子场论中的对称性结构奠定了坚实基础。

Abstract: These notes were prepared for a series of intensive lectures delivered at Hokkaido University, Nagoya University, Kyoto University, and Kyushu University.
  We begin with a brief review of higher-form symmetries, anomalies, and discrete gauge theories, before introducing non-invertible symmetries in $(1+1)$-dimensional systems. The basic structure of fusion categories is then discussed, including a discussion of categorical analogs of discrete gauging and representation theory. We subsequently turn to $(3+1)$-dimensional theories, where several physical applications of non-invertible symmetries are discussed. These notes are intended to be largely self-contained, and require no prior familiarity with subjects such as conformal field theory or lattice models.

</details>

Abstract: We extend the study of the recently introduced crystal melting models associated to toric Calabi-Yau 4-folds in several directions. To this end, we develop an efficient algorithm for constructing crystals based on periodic quivers. A central goal of this work is to understand the behavior of crystals and their partition functions under triality. We analyze the evolution of crystals along periodic triality cascades and generate detailed data for these systems, including Hasse diagrams, partition functions, and the multiplicities of melting configurations. We introduce the notion of stable variables and show that they lead to the stabilization of the partition functions along cascades. Finally, we define the profile of the crystal partition function and observe that, when expressed in terms of stable variables, it displays interesting behavior. A further motivation for this work is to generate empirical data that may guide the search for a physically motivated generalization of cluster algebras associated with $2d$ (0,2) quiver theories and their triality transformations.

### [27] [Universal Planar Abelian Duals for 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ Unitary CS-SQCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08842)
*Sergio Benvenuti,Riccardo Comi,Gabriel Pedde Ungureanu,Simone Rota,Anant Shri*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有手征-平面对偶（chiral-planar dualities）仅限于参数空间中的特定轨迹$F = 2|k| + 2N$，这限制了其应用范围。需要发展更通用的对偶框架来覆盖整个参数空间，以系统分析三维规范理论的动力学。

Method: 通过开发系统算法追踪对偶理论在一般质量形变（generic mass deformations）下的流（flow），将平面阿贝尔四元图（planar Abelian quiver）构建为通用分析工具，而非仅限于特定对偶描述。

Result: 成功构建了覆盖整个$(N, F, k)$参数空间的显式平面阿贝尔对偶，统一了三维$\mathcal{N}=2$ $U(N)_k$ SQCD理论的红外物理描述。该结果推广了先前仅限于$F = 2|k| + 2N$轨迹的手征-平面对偶类。

Conclusion: 平面阿贝尔四元图不仅是特定对偶描述，更是分析三维规范动力学（3d gauge dynamics）的通用工具。该框架为$\mathcal{N}=4$镜像对称（mirror symmetry）的质量形变提供了系统处理方法，扩展了对偶性在更广泛参数空间的应用。

Abstract: We provide an explicit planar Abelian dual for three-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=2$ $U(N)_k$ SQCD with $F$ fundamental chiral multiplets. This construction covers the entire $(N, F, k)$ parameter space (provided supersymmetry is unbroken), offering a unified framework for the infrared physics of these theories. Our results generalize a recently discovered class of chiral-planar dualities, which were previously limited to the locus $F = 2|k| + 2N$, which is a mass deformation of $\mathcal{N}=4$ mirror symmetry plus a restricted set of additional mass deformations. By developing a systematic algorithm to track the flow of the dual theory under generic mass deformations, we establish the planar Abelian quiver not merely as a specific dual description, but as a universal tool for analyzing 3d gauge dynamics.

</details>


### [28] [New Construction of Black Hole Solution in Non-Commutative Geometry and their Thermodynamic Properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08971)
*Abdellah Touati*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种在非对易规范理论中构建黑洞解的新方法，通过Seiberg-Witten映射获得牛顿势的非对易修正，求解爱因斯坦方程得到精确黑洞解，并分析了其热力学性质、相变行为及量子隧穿效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非对易规范理论（non-commutative gauge theory）中的引力研究方法通常较为繁琐，需要一种更简洁有效的方法来构建非对易时空中的黑洞解，并系统研究其物理性质。

Method: 首先通过Seiberg-Witten映射获得牛顿势的非对易修正，然后在非对易参数一阶近似下求解包含非对易物质密度的爱因斯坦方程；该方法也应用于构建具有非对易U(1)对称性的带电解。

Result: 该方法在指定阶数下得到了非对易规范理论中的精确黑洞解，比现有方法更简洁；热力学分析显示非对易性消除了蒸发末期的温度发散并诱导二阶相变，在压力存在时恢复了类Hawking-Page相变。

Conclusion: 非对易性显著影响黑洞物理：小黑洞对非对易参数变化高度敏感，非对易形变抑制了粒子数密度并减弱了连续发射间的关联，相当于为粒子逃逸设置了势垒。

Abstract: We present a new method to construct black hole solutions in non-commutative (NC) gauge theory. First we obtain the NC correction to the Newton potential via the Seiberg-Witten (SW) map, and then solve the Einstein equations in the presence of the resulting NC matter density at first order in the NC parameter. The same procedure is applied to construct a charged solution with NC \(U(1)\) symmetry. This method yields an exact black hole solution in NC gauge theory at the stated order and is considerably less cumbersome than other NC gauge theory approaches to gravity. As an application, we analyze the thermodynamic properties of the new solutions: we compute the ADM mass, Hawking temperature, entropy, heat capacity and free energy, both in the absence and in the presence of pressure. Our results show that non-commutativity removes the temperature divergence at the final stage of evaporation and induces a second-order phase transition; in the presence of pressure we recover a Hawking-Page-like phase transition. We then investigate the susceptibility and linear response of the black hole to changes in the NC parameter. Our results show high sensitivity to small changes in the NC parameter for small black holes, while the sensitivity becomes weaker for larger ones. Finally, we study quantum tunneling in this geometry for both thermal and non-thermal radiation, and we investigate the particle-number density and statistical correlations of successive emissions. We find that the NC deformation suppresses the particle-number density and weakens correlations between successive emissions, effectively acting as a barrier to particle escape.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流体动力学基于守恒流（conserved currents）的守恒定律，最近扩展到包含高阶形式对称性（higher-form symmetries）。需要建立微观理论与流体动力学理论之间的数学联系框架。

Result: 提出流体动力学近似可以表示为微分分级流形的余跨度结构，其中X_micro和X_hydro分别描述微观和流体动力学理论，X_BF描述守恒流的BF理论。

Conclusion: 该框架为理解流体动力学近似提供了新的数学视角，通过BF理论和微分分级流形的余跨度结构统一描述微观理论与流体动力学理论之间的关系。

Abstract: Hydrodynamics is based on conservation laws of currents: one starts from the conserved currents of the theory describing the microscopic dynamics, and provides an alternative parameterisation of these currents in terms of hydrodynamic variables (density, pressure, velocity, etc.). This paradigm has recently been extended to incorporate higher-form symmetries. The conservation law of the $p$-form conserved currents can be regarded as the equations of motion of a $BF$ theory that treats the currents as fundamental fields. We argue that the hydrodynamic approximation to a microscopic theory can be regarded as a cospan of differential graded manifolds $X_\mathrm{micro}\to X_{BF}\leftarrow X_\mathrm{hydro}$, where $X_\mathrm{micro}$ and $X_\mathrm{hydro}$ describe the microscopic and hydrodynamic theories, respectively, and $X_{BF}$ describes the $BF$ theory of conserved currents.

In particular, in $d=3$ the extremal surfaces are geodesics with two ends in the boundary. In the Schwarzschild-AdS black hole the space-like geodesics can connect timelike-separated points by winding around the horizon multiple times. This result can be extended to other asymptotically AdS spacetimes. Moreover, for geodesics joining time-like separated points, if there is a photon ring then the timelike entanglement entropy in the $AdS_3/CFT_2$ will not have an imaginary part. We present an exhaustive analysis about the existence of geodesics anchored in the boundary of the three dimensional quantum BTZ (quBTZ) black hole and its charged counterpart. We found conditions for the existence of geodesics with two ends in the boundary in all branches of the quBTZ and determine the type of distance between the points in the boundary. We use a criteria for the existence of light rings to shed some light over the conjecture for spacetimes that are spherically symmetric and have a photon sphere: there are always points with time-like separation that can be connected by space-like or null geodesics.

Abstract: For light and massless scalar fields, cosmological correlation functions suffer from infrared divergences and secular logarithms. Abstract: We review and elaborate on the issue of the dilaton transformation under the usual $r \rightarrow α'/r$ target space duality and its non-static generalization (or $σ$-model duality). ### [36] [Kaluza-Klein mode mixing in braneworlds: constraints on scalar absorption and physical degrees of freedom](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09656)
*Wen-Xuan Ma,Chun-E Fu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了膜世界模型中体U(1)规范场的Kaluza-Klein模式混合，发现向量-标量和标量-标量混合对余维d(d>1)背景的翘曲因子施加严格约束，并揭示了混合如何改变标量模式的吸收机制，导致向量KK模式物理质量偏移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过要求Kaluza-Klein基函数的正交归一性和完备性，分析混合扇区的解耦条件，特别关注余维d(d>1)背景中翘曲因子所受约束，并在(4+2)维模型中研究两个不同标量扇区的混合动力学。

Result: 向量-标量混合对余维d(d>1)背景的翘曲因子施加严格约束；四维有效作用量的规范不变性在混合下得以保持；混合改变了标量模式的吸收机制，使向量KK模式的物理质量偏离未扰动本征值；(4+2)维模型中两个标量扇区导致丰富混合动力学，仅特定线性组合被吸收，剩余标量KK模式作为物理自由度持续存在。

Abstract: We investigate the mixing between Kaluza-Klein (KK) modes for a bulk U(1) gauge field within braneworld models. By demanding orthonormality and completeness for the KK basis functions, we demonstrate that the decoupling of mixed sectors, specifically of the vector-scalar and scalar-scalar types, imposes stringent constraints on the warp factors of codimension-d (d>1) backgrounds. We show that the gauge invariance of the four-dimensional effective action is preserved despite such mixing, manifesting as an intrinsic property of the massive vector KK sector. However, the generic presence of vector-scalar mixing fundamentally alters the absorption mechanism of the scalar modes, dynamically shifting the physical masses of the vector KK modes away from their unperturbed eigenvalues. In (4+2)-dimensional models, the existence of two distinct scalar sectors significantly enriches the mixing dynamics. As the massive vectors absorb only specific linear combinations of these scalars, a residual set of massive scalar KK modes persists as physical degrees of freedom.

</details>


### [37] [Capacity of Entanglement and Replica Backreaction in RST Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09763)
*Raúl Arias,Daniel Fondevila*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究计算了二维膨胀子引力（dilaton gravity）中纠缠容量（capacity of entanglement）的解析解，重点关注RST模型中的永恒黑洞（eternal black hole）与N个共形物质场（conformal matter fields）耦合的情况。通过求解轨道折叠（orbifold）上的复制形变（replica deformation），获得了单区间的时间无关广义容量和双区间的时间依赖容量，揭示了Page转变（Page transition）附近容量尖锐特征的微观机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 主要技术步骤是在轨道折叠（orbifold）上全局求解n=1附近的复制形变（replica deformation），包括由单值性（single valuedness）和固定微正则态（fixed microcanonical state）要求确定的齐次部分。研究聚焦于Russo-Susskind-Thorlacius模型（RST model）中的永恒黑洞（eternal black hole）与N个共形物质场（conformal matter fields）耦合的系统。

Result: 对于单区间，获得了与广义熵（generalized entropy）类似的时间无关广义容量（time independent generalized capacity）。对于双区间，即使在晚期因子化区域（late time factorization regime），全局解在复制固定点（replica fixed points）之间产生相互作用项；经过洛伦兹延拓（Lorentzian continuation）后，这导致在两个量子极值曲面鞍点（two QES saddle）上产生时间依赖的容量（time dependent capacity），尽管相应的熵处于平台期（entropy plateau）。

Conclusion: 双区间容量的大尺寸意味着在n=1附近存在高度非均匀的鞍点竞争（non uniform saddle competition），这为Page转变（Page transition）处容量的尖锐特征提供了具体机制。研究讨论了所得表达式的有效范围，阐明了容量动态行为背后的微观物理机制。

Abstract: We compute the capacity of entanglement in two dimensional dilaton gravity in a setting where Hawking radiation, backreaction, and islands can be treated analytically. Our focus is the eternal black hole of the Russo Susskind Thorlacius model coupled to N conformal matter fields. Unlike previous gravitational computations, which were mostly carried out in JT gravity, the RST model forces one to deal with a genuinely dynamical conformal factor and with the global constraints of the replica construction. The main technical step is therefore to solve the replica deformation on the orbifold globally at first order near n=1, including the homogeneous sector fixed by single valuedness and by the requirement of a fixed microcanonical state. For a single interval we obtain a time independent generalized capacity, parallel to the generalized entropy. For two intervals, even in the late time factorization regime, the global solution generates an interaction term between replica fixed points; after Lorentzian continuation this produces a time dependent capacity on the two QES saddle, despite the corresponding entropy plateau. We discuss the regime of validity of the resulting expressions and explain how the large size of the two QES capacity implies a highly non uniform saddle competition near n=1, providing a concrete mechanism for sharp features of the capacity at the Page transition.

### [38] [The scheme independent 3-sphere free energy is not a monotone F-function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09799)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索从三维量子场论的三球配分函数中构造的自然方案无关量是否可以作为单调F函数。这关系到理解重整化群流中信息量的单调性行为，特别是与F定理相关的物理量。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）从(2+1)维量子场论的三球配分函数中去除所有局域反项模糊性，构造方案无关量；2）在共形固定点处验证该量等于标准F定理不变量；3）通过共形微扰理论分析相关标量形变下的行为；4）对自由质量标量场在S³上进行精确分析。

Result: 研究结果显示：1）在共形固定点处，该方案无关量等于标准F定理不变量；2）共形微扰理论表明，在三维CFT的任何相关标量形变下，该量在O(g²)阶局部减小；3）然而，对自由质量标量场的精确分析表明，该球面自由能插值函数在完整重整化群流上并非单调：它会低于其红外值，然后回升至该值。

Conclusion: 结论指出，从球面热力学构建的自然反项扣除量本身并非单调F函数。该障碍源于消除局域模糊性所需的二阶微分算符，这阻碍了该量在完整重整化群流上保持单调性。

Abstract: We study the natural scheme-independent quantity obtained from the three-sphere partition function of a $(2+1)$-dimensional quantum field theory by removing all local counterterm ambiguities. At conformal fixed points this quantity equals the standard $F$-theorem invariant. Conformal perturbation theory shows that it locally decreases at $O(g^2)$ under any relevant scalar deformation of a three-dimensional CFT. However, an exact analysis of the free massive scalar on $S^3$ shows that this sphere-free-energy interpolant is not monotone along the full renormalization-group flow: it dips below its infrared value and then returns to it. Thus the natural counterterm-subtracted quantity built from sphere thermodynamics is not, by itself, a monotone $F$-function. We trace the obstruction to the second-order differential operator required to eliminate the local ambiguities.

  The validity of Hod's conjecture, which relates quasinormal frequencies to the black hole temperature, is tested throughout the physically allowed parameter space. Our results show that both the effective potential and the decay rate of perturbations depend on the values of $α$ and $λ$, leading to either enhancement or suppression of the conditions required to satisfy Hod's bound.
  Furthermore, we discuss how these parameters modify the black hole shadow and the corresponding energy emission rate, revealing correlations with observable signatures. Finally, we establish a connection with the Swampland Distance Conjecture by expressing the Hawking temperature in terms of the scalar field excursion.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In Kaluza-Klein (KK) compactification of gravitational theories, moduli fields, which are scalar fields associated to the deformations of the compact manifold, are typically lighter than the KK gravitons. However, a universal limit on their mass does not seem to exist. We provide numerical evidence that a light scalar particle, with mass ratio to the first KK graviton $(m_{\rm sc}/m_{1KK})^2 \leq {4/3}$, is necessary for the consistency of the $4d$ effective theory of KK gravitons. This can be interpreted as a limit on how rigidly the compact manifold can be stabilized.

### [41] [Dynamics and interaction of solitons in the BPS limit and their internal modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09887)
*S. Navarro-Obregón*

TL;DR: 该博士论文详细分析了孤子动力学（soliton dynamics），特别关注了与这些构型相关的内部模式（internal modes）的作用。通过构建有效模型和使用集体坐标方法（collective coordinate method），论文在一维和二维模型中建立了坚实基础，为三维理论研究奠定基础。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文采用集体坐标方法（collective coordinate method）构建有效模型，保留捕捉完整理论数值模拟现象学所需的基本自由度。同时使用了微扰技术（perturbative techniques）等补充数学工具，并特别关注扭结（kinks）、振荡子（oscillons）、涡旋（vortices）和瞬子（sphalerons）的研究。

Result: 主要成果包括：首次在集体坐标框架内引入真正的辐射模式（radiation modes）；通过纳入振动自由度，推广了阿贝尔-希格斯模型（Abelian-Higgs model）中局部涡旋的Samols模空间度量（Samols' moduli space metric）；识别并分析了一类新的瞬子，称为半BPS瞬子（semi-BPS sphalerons）；详细研究了振荡内部模式在瞬子衰变过程中的作用。

Conclusion: 论文提出了动态稳定机制（dynamic stabilisation mechanism），该机制在更一般模型中得到进一步解释和扩展，证明了这一现象对物理相关理论的鲁棒性和潜在适用性。研究为一维和二维模型建立了坚实基础，为扩展到三维理论研究提供了框架。

Abstract: The main objective of this thesis has been to analyse soliton dynamics in detail, with special attention paid to the role of the internal modes associated with these configurations. Specifically, the thesis has focused on the study of one- and two-dimensional models, with the aim of developing a solid basis that can then be extended to the study in three-dimensional theories. This thesis concentrates on the study of kinks, oscillons, vortices, and sphalerons. Nevertheless, field theories constitute systems with an infinite number of degrees of freedom, which poses challenges both for obtaining analytical results and for predictive modeling. To address these challenges, this thesis employs the construction of effective models that retain the essential degrees of freedom required to capture the phenomenology observed in numerical simulations of the full theory, using the well-known collective coordinate method. In addition, other complementary mathematical tools, such as perturbative techniques, have also been employed. Among the main achievements of this doctoral thesis, it is worth highlighting the introduction, for the first time, of genuine radiation modes within the collective coordinate framework. Furthermore, a generalisation of Samols' moduli space metric for local vortices in the Abelian-Higgs model has been developed through the incorporation of vibrational degrees of freedom. Additionally, a new class of sphalerons that we have coined semi-BPS sphalerons has been identified and analysed. Finally, the role of oscillatory internal modes in the decay process of sphalerons has been studied in detail, leading to the proposal of a dynamic stabilisation mechanism. This mechanism has been further explained and extended to more general models, demonstrating the robustness and potential applicability of this phenomenon to physically relevant theories.

### [42] [Equilibrium Partition Function of Non-Relativistic CFTs in Harmonic Trap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09856)
*Eunwoo Lee*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究分析了非相对论共形场论（non-relativistic conformal field theories）在谐振子量子化（harmonic quantization）下的平衡配分函数（equilibrium partition function）。研究揭示了配分函数在流体力学区域（hydrodynamic regime）和角动量极限（large-angular-momentum limit）下的普遍结构，特别关注了谐振频率（harmonic trapping frequency）与角速度（angular velocities）的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索非相对论共形场论在谐振子量子化下的平衡配分函数特性。特别关注流体力学区域和角动量极限下的普遍结构，这对于理解冷原子实验（cold-atom experiments）中可实现的超流系统（superfluid systems）具有重要意义。

Method: 研究方法首先分析流体力学区域，研究配分函数的主导阶行为。然后研究大角动量极限（Ω_a→ω），此时离心效应（centrifugal effects）几乎抵消了囚禁势（trapping potential）。最后以冷原子实验中可实现的系统，特别是谐振子囚禁中的幺正费米子（fermions at unitarity）作为具体实例进行分析。

Result: 研究结果显示，在流体力学区域，配分函数的对数在ω²-Ω_a²处表现出简单极点（simple poles），其残差由μ/T的单变量函数决定。在大角动量极限下，配分函数的对数同样在ω²-Ω_a²处表现出简单极点，但残差分别依赖于μ/T和ω/T，普遍性较低。

Conclusion: 研究表明，非相对论共形场论在谐振子量子化下的平衡配分函数具有特定的极点结构。在流体力学区域，这种结构由状态方程（equation of state）决定，表现出较高的普遍性；而在大角动量极限下，结构虽然相似但普遍性降低。这些发现对于理解冷原子系统中的超流行为具有重要意义。

Abstract: We investigate the equilibrium partition function of non-relativistic conformal field theories in harmonic quantization. We first analyze the hydrodynamic regime and show that, at leading order, the partition function exhibits a universal structure determined by the equation of state: the logarithm of the partition function develops simple poles in $ω^2-Ω_a^2$, where $ω$ is the harmonic trapping frequency and $Ω_a$ are angular velocities acting as chemical potentials for angular momentum. The corresponding residue is determined by a single-variable function of $μ/T$, with $μ$ the particle-number chemical potential and $T$ the temperature.
  We then study the large-angular-momentum limit $Ω_a\toω$. In this regime centrifugal effects nearly cancel the trapping potential, and the logarithm of the partition function again exhibits simple poles in $ω^2-Ω_a^2$, but with a less universal residue depending separately on $μ/T$ and $ω/T$. As explicit examples we analyze superfluid systems realizable in cold-atom experiments, in particular fermions at unitarity confined in a harmonic trap.

Abstract: The free string spectrum is highly degenerate, with a degeneracy that grows exponentially with the mass. Turning on a non-vanishing string coupling $g_s$ introduces interactions, rendering massive string states unstable and allowing them to decay into lower-mass states, with mixing constrained by Lorentz invariance. This behavior is expected already at one-loop level. The imaginary part of the one-loop mass correction is related to the width of the decay into two lower-mass states at tree level, whereas the real part is generally IR-divergent and needs regularization and renormalization. The analysis simplifies for states in the first Regge trajectory. In particular, we consider the one-loop mass corrections for these states in the NS-NS sector of Type-II string theories. We explicitly construct the related vertex operators and exploit the properties of elliptic functions in order to obtain a closed form expression for the integral over the insertion point. We further regularize the divergences of the integral over the modular parameter of the torus by means of the $i\varepsilon$-prescription in string theory. Finally we extract numerical results for the mass correction up to level $N=4$.

We call this property the ordered single cluster condition, and provide its physical interpretation. This condition is stronger than the usual cluster adjacency obeyed by neighbouring letters, and imposes stronger constraints for the symbol bootstrap. We also show how any tree graph satisfies a cluster-like structure in terms of tubes and tubings on the underlying graph, which allows for a similar bootstrap approach.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期格点证据表明，对于N_f≥2无质量味夸克，QCD的手征相变（chiral phase transition）是二阶的。这促使研究者探索在温度T和虚重子化学势θ_B构成的临界线上可能的共形场论（conformal field theory, CFT）描述。

Method: 通过分析在一般θ_B值下的't Hooft异常（'t Hooft anomaly）来约束相变行为，即使是在θ_B=0的情况下。该方法利用异常匹配条件限制可能的临界理论。

Result: 't Hooft异常对θ_B=0处的相变施加了强约束，仅留下三种最小化情景。对于N_f≥3（可能也包括N_f=2）的最佳动机情景超越了Ginzburg-Landau理论，其特征是一个依赖于θ_B的普适类（universality classes）构成的共形流形（conformal manifold），其中包含一个与重子密度相关的精确边际算子（exactly marginal operator）。

Conclusion: 研究确定了QCD手征相变临界行为的可能理论框架，揭示了超越传统Ginzburg-Landau描述的新物理情景，特别是存在一个依赖于虚重子化学势的共形流形，这为理解QCD相图提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: Recent lattice evidence suggests the chiral phase transition in QCD is second-order for $N_f \ge 2$ massless flavors. We constrain CFT descriptions of a critical line in temperature $T$ and imaginary baryon chemical potential $θ_B = iμ_B/T$. An 't Hooft anomaly at general $θ_B$ constrains the transition even at $θ_B = 0$, leaving only three minimal scenarios. The best-motivated scenario for $N_f\ge3$, and perhaps also $N_f = 2$, is beyond Ginzburg-Landau, featuring a conformal manifold of $θ_B$-dependent universality classes with an exactly marginal operator related to baryon density.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文研究了稀释Curie-Weiss模型，该模型通过Erdős-Rényi图（而非完全图）编码自旋间依赖关系。在高温外磁场条件下，证明了磁化强度的尖锐累积量界限，导出了中心极限定理、中偏差原理、集中不等式、带Cramér修正的正态近似界限和模高斯收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Curie-Weiss模型使用完全图编码自旋间依赖关系，而本文考虑更一般的稀释Curie-Weiss模型，其中依赖结构通过Erdős-Rényi随机图实现，每个边以概率p(N)独立出现。这种推广旨在研究稀疏连接对统计力学系统行为的影响。

Method: 研究在高温外磁场条件（0<β<1, h∈ℝ）下进行，要求p³N²→∞。主要方法是通过对退火Gibbs测度（annealed Gibbs measure）建立磁化强度的尖锐累积量界限（sharp cumulant bounds）。

Conclusion: 稀释Curie-Weiss模型在高温外磁场条件下，当p³N²→∞时，磁化强度展现出丰富的概率极限行为，包括中心极限定理、偏差原理和集中性质，这些结果通过尖锐的累积量界限得以统一证明。

Abstract: We consider the dilute Curie-Weiss model of size $N$, which is a generalization of the classical Curie-Weiss model where the dependency structure between the spins is not encoded by the complete graph but via the (directed) Erdős-Rényi graph on $N$ vertices in which every edge appears independently with probability $p(N)$. In the high temperature with external magnetic field regime ($0<β<1,h\in\mathbb{R}$) we prove for $p^{3}N^{2}\to\infty$ sharp cumulant bounds for the magnetization for the annealed Gibbs measure implying a central limit theorem with rate, a moderate deviation principle, a concentration inequality, a normal approximation bound with Cramér correction and mod-Gaussian convergence.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过迭代取完全非负部分（totally nonnegative part）的解析边界来研究$V(3,n)$及其诱导子簇。利用Gelfand-MacPherson对应将这些子簇解释为$\mathbb{P}^2$上的点配置，并在$V(3,n)$上构造了一个最高次亚纯形式（top-degree meromorphic form）。

Conclusion: 本文通过组合与代数几何方法系统研究了ABCT簇$V(3,n)$及其子簇，证明了其为正几何，解决了Lam猜想，为相关物理理论中的几何结构提供了严格的数学基础。

Abstract: The ABCT variety $V(3,n)$ is the image closure of the rational Veronese map from the Grassmannian $\operatorname{Gr}(2,n)$ to the Grassmannian $\operatorname{Gr}(3,n)$. It was studied by Arkani-Hamed--Bourjaily--Cachazo--Trnka in the context of tree-level scattering amplitudes arising in planar $\mathcal N=4$ supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory and Witten's twistor string theory. From this perspective, $V(3,n)$ is conjectured to be a positive geometry by Lam.
  In this paper, we study the combinatorial and algebraic geometry aspects of $V(3,n)$ and its subvarieties induced by iteratively taking analytic boundaries of the totally nonnegative part. We interpret these subvarieties as point configurations on $\mathbb{P}^2$ by the Gelfand-MacPherson correspondence. We construct a top-degree meromorphic form on $V(3,n)$ and show that it is a positive geometry, proving Lam's conjecture.

Abstract: In theories where the Lorentz symmetry of gravity is spontaneously broken, a non-minimally coupled bumblebee vector field acquires a nonzero vacuum expectation value, leading to modifications of standard General Relativity (GR). In this work, we investigate exact solutions describing static and spherically symmetric charged black holes surrounded by a cloud of strings within the framework of bumblebee gravity. We begin by analyzing the thermodynamic properties of these black hole solutions, including their mass, temperature, and entropy, highlighting how Lorentz-violating effects alter standard results. Next, we examine the optical properties of the spacetime, focusing on the photon sphere, the resulting black hole shadow, and the deflection of light, thereby providing potential observational signatures of Lorentz violation. Finally, we explore the impact of Lorentz-violating parameters on classical gravitational tests within the Solar System, such as advance of perihelion precession, in order to set observational constraints. Our analysis provides a comprehensive investigation of the interplay between Lorentz violation, black hole physics, and cloud of strings, offering a framework to probe new physics beyond GR.

Abstract: The new tetrads introduced previously for non-null electromagnetic fields in Einstein- Maxwell spacetimes enable a direct link to the local electromagnetic gauge group of transformations. Due to the peculiar elements in the construction of these new tetrads a direct connection can be established between the local group of electromagnetic gauge transformations and local groups of tetrad transformations on two different local and orthogonal planes of eigenvectors of the Einstein-Maxwell stress-energy tensor. These tetrad vectors are gauge dependent. It is an interesting and relevant problem to study if there are local gauge transformations that can map on the timelike-spacelike plane, the timelike and the spacelike vectors into the intersection of the local light cone and the plane itself. How many of these local gauge transformations exist and how the mathematics and the geometry of these particular transformations play out. These local gauge transformations would be singular and it is important to identify them.

### [51] [Spin Induced Geometry: Emergence of Metric and Torsional Sectors from Spinor Source](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08769)
*Elisa Varani*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种几何框架，其中度量和扭率自由度从旋量流中动态涌现，而非作为仿射连接的基本属性。基本动力学变量是一个带局部洛伦兹指标的三阶场，由费米子自旋流源驱动。该框架导致传播的扭率，并使无自旋测试粒子通过涌现的几何结构间接感知自旋流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在构建一个几何框架，其中度量和扭率（torsion）自由度从更基本的旋量（spinor）流中动态涌现，而非作为仿射连接（affine connection）的基本预设属性。这区别于爱因斯坦-嘉当理论（Einstein-Cartan theory）中扭率被代数约束的情况。

Method: 采用几何框架，基本动力学变量是携带局部洛伦兹指标的三阶场，由费米子自旋流（spin currents）源驱动的有质量克莱因-戈登方程（massive Klein-Gordon equation）控制。该场在时空指标上的投影产生无确定对称性的二阶张量，其对称和反对称部分分别定义了有效的自旋诱导度量和扭率自由度。

Result: 度量和扭率自由度均有质量且受汤川抑制（Yukawa-suppressed），确保与长程引力动力学解耦。扭率在此框架中是传播的而非代数约束的。无自旋测试粒子遵循有效度量的测地线，从而通过涌现的几何结构间接感知自旋流。在Majorana费米子极限下，几何变为纯轴扭率（axial-torsional），允许拓扑非平凡构型如涡旋（vortices）和类斯格明子结构（Skyrmion-like structures）从旋量源中动态涌现。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种机制，使度量和扭率从旋量流中涌现，为引力几何与量子物质场之间的相互作用提供了新视角。特别地，它揭示了无自旋测试粒子如何通过涌现几何间接感知自旋流，这一机制在标准广义相对论和爱因斯坦-嘉当理论中均不存在。不同旋量结构（Dirac、Weyl、Majorana）产生不同的几何相，其中Majorana极限导致纯轴扭率几何和拓扑非平凡构型的涌现。

Abstract: We present a geometric framework in which both metric and torsional degrees of freedom emerge dynamically from spinor currents, without being postulated as fundamental properties of the affine connection. The fundamental dynamical variable is a rank-three field carrying local Lorentz indices, governed by a massive Klein--Gordon equation sourced by fermionic spin currents. Its projection onto spacetime indices yields a rank-two tensor with no definite symmetry; the symmetric and antisymmetric sectors define, respectively, an effective spin-induced metric and the torsional degrees of freedom. Both sectors are massive and Yukawa-suppressed, ensuring decoupling from long-range gravitational dynamics. Unlike Einstein--Cartan theory, torsion here is propagating rather than algebraically constrained. A key consequence is that spinless test particles follow geodesics of the effective metric and are therefore indirectly sensitive to spin currents through the emergent geometric structure~ -- ~a mechanism absent in both standard General Relativity and Einstein--Cartan theory. The spinorial structure of the source is analyzed across three regimes: general Dirac, Weyl, and Majorana fermions, each giving rise to a distinct geometric phase. In the Majorana limit, the geometry becomes purely axial-torsional, admitting topologically non-trivial configurations such as vortices and Skyrmion-like structures, which emerge dynamically from the spinorial source.

Result: 研究结果建立了曲率标量之间的实用层次结构，明确了高阶不变量受低阶不变量代数控制的程度。具体包括：建立了不同Petrov和Segre类型时空曲率不变量之间的逐点不等式；确定了Zakhary-McIntosh不变量受Kretschmann标量控制的条件。

Abstract: We establish a new set of pointwise inequalities that order curvature invariants across various Petrov and Segre types of spacetimes. In arbitrary spacetime dimension, we systematically analyze inequalities among contractions of the Ricci tensor. We further explore the conditions under which all Zakhary--McIntosh invariants in $(1+3)$-dimensional spacetimes are bounded above (up to appropriate powers) by the Kretschmann scalar. ### [53] [Strong-deflection expansion of the deflection angle near a degenerate photon sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08778)
*Takahisa Igata,Tadashi Sasaki,Naoki Tsukamoto*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种在渐近平坦、静态、球对称时空中，针对光线在退化光子球附近散射的强偏折展开方法，能够分离发散项并得到唯一的领先幂律项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究光线在退化光子球（degenerate photon sphere）附近散射时的偏折角计算问题，传统方法在边际轨道（marginal orbit）处存在发散困难，需要建立一种在边际性处仍保持良好定义的展开方法。

Method: 采用强偏折展开（strong-deflection expansion）方法，通过分离光线经过边际轨道时产生的发散贡献，得到在边际性处唯一确定的领先幂律项。该方法将偏折角积分中的发散部分与局部因子分离。

Result: 在强偏折极限下，以最接近半径（radius of closest approach）表示的领先系数可分解为通用分支常数（universal branch constant）和由退化光子球处有效势（effective potential）三阶导数决定的局部因子。当转换为以碰撞参数（impact parameter）展开时，系数仅需乘以额外的局部转换因子。

Conclusion: 该展开方法提供了处理退化光子球附近光线偏折问题的系统框架，局部因子可通过韦尔张量（Weyl tensor）电部分构造的无量纲潮汐度量的面积半径导数进行不变表示，在广义相对论中进一步与加权零能量密度剖面的面积半径导数相关联。

Abstract: We present a strong-deflection expansion for the deflection angle of light rays scattered near a degenerate photon sphere in asymptotically flat, static, and spherically symmetric spacetimes. Our prescription isolates the divergent contribution to the deflection-angle integral arising from the ray's passage near the marginal orbit in a way that remains well defined at marginality, thereby yielding a unique leading power-law term. When expressed in terms of the radius of closest approach, the leading coefficient in the strong deflection limit factorizes into a universal branch constant and a local factor determined by the third derivative of the effective potential at the degenerate photon sphere. Passing to the expansion in terms of the impact parameter then only multiplies the coefficient by an additional local conversion factor. We show that the local factor in the closest-approach expansion admits an invariant representation through the areal-radius derivative of a dimensionless tidal measure constructed from the electric part of the Weyl tensor. In general relativity, we further relate this quantity to the areal-radius derivative of a weighted null-energy density profile. Analytic examples validate this factorization and yield closed-form expressions for the leading divergent coefficients in representative marginal configurations.

</details>


### [54] [Scalar shortcut to beyond-Kerr ringdown tests and their complementarity with black-hole shadow observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08782)
*Paolo Pani,Andrea P. Sanna*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种通过计算测试标量场的准正则模式（quasinormal modes）来近似估计引力准正则模式修正的补充方法。对于Kerr-Newman和Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet黑洞，该方法能以数十个百分点精度重现精确修正，其精度通常与或优于eikonal近似。研究首次计算了引力测试中常用现象学度规的标量准正则模式，发现当前环降（ringdown）约束与黑洞阴影观测相当甚至更严格。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于寻找一种在超越广义相对论（general relativity）的复杂理论或缺乏基础理论的唯象度规（phenomenological metrics）中，近似计算黑洞准正则模式（quasinormal modes）的有效方法。传统eikonal近似（eikonal approximation）常被外推至低角动量区域，但需要更准确且互补的近似策略。

Method: 研究方法采用一种互补的近似策略：精确计算在黑洞背景下传播的测试标量场（test scalar field）的准正则模式，并将其与广义相对论预测的偏差（deviations）作为引力准正则模式相应修正的代理（proxy）。该方法首次应用于引力测试中常用的大类唯象度规。

Result: 对于Kerr-Newman和Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet黑洞，该方法能在数十个百分点精度内重现精确修正，包括不同自由度间的耦合（coupling among different degrees of freedom）。该方法精度通常与或优于eikonal近似，且在环降测量保持百分比水平时足够准确。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的标量场准正则模式方法为估计引力准正则模式修正提供了有效的近似策略。通过首次计算唯象度规的标量准正则模式，发现当前环降约束与黑洞阴影（BH shadow）观测相当甚至更严格，并为原本无法探测的领域提供了互补约束。

Abstract: The quasinormal modes of black holes (BHs) in the large-angular-momentum limit can be computed within the eikonal approximation. This approximation is often extrapolated to low angular momentum to obtain a rough estimate of the dominant ringdown modes. Although approximate, this approach is particularly convenient in theories beyond general relativity with intricate dynamics, or for phenomenological metrics that lack an underlying fundamental theory. Here we explore a complementary approximate strategy: we compute exactly the quasinormal modes of a test scalar field propagating on the BH background and use their \emph{deviations} from the general-relativity predictions as a proxy for the corresponding corrections to the gravitational quasinormal modes. For Kerr-Newman and Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet BHs, we show that this method reproduces the exact corrections (including the coupling among different degrees of freedom) within tens of percent, an accuracy that is adequate as long as ringdown measurements remain at the percent level. Furthermore, this method is typically comparable to, or more accurate than, the eikonal approximation. We then apply the same strategy to phenomenological metrics commonly employed in tests of gravity using BH imaging. By computing scalar quasinormal modes in a large family of these metrics for the first time, we find that current ringdown constraints are comparable to, and in some cases more stringent than, those derived from BH shadow observations, while also providing complementary bounds on sectors that would otherwise be inaccessible.

### [55] [Chaos and fractals of the black hole photon ring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08790)
