<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 克尔黑洞的光子环具有自相似的分层结构，本文旨在探究这种自相似结构在相空间中的持续性，并分析近束缚光子轨道（bound photon orbit）的动力学特性，特别是李雅普诺夫指数在其中的作用。

Method: 通过计算近不稳定束缚轨道（unstably bound orbit）光线的首次返回映射（first-return map），分析李雅普诺夫指数对动力学的影响，并研究背景时空偏离克尔几何时混沌的出现机制。

Result: 尽管近束缚光线对初始条件具有指数敏感性，但并未表现出混沌行为；然而当背景时空偏离克尔几何时，混沌开始出现，特别是在光子壳层（photon shell）中强共振束缚轨道附近最为明显，导致相空间出现分形结构（fractal phase-space structure）。

Conclusion: 克尔黑洞光子环的自相似结构在相空间中持续存在，李雅普诺夫指数控制着近束缚轨道的动力学；时空几何的微小偏离会引发混沌行为，这种混沌、分形、自相似的结构特征在首次返回映射中得到编码。

Abstract: The photon ring of a Kerr black hole decomposes into a self-similar hierarchy of subrings. Here, we show that this self-similar structure persists in phase space. Moreover, near the photon shell of bound photon orbits, dynamics are controlled by a Lyapunov exponent $γ$, whose role we highlight by computing the first-return map for light rays close to an unstably bound orbit. Despite an exponential $e^γ$ sensitivity to initial conditions, nearly bound rays do not exhibit chaotic behavior. However, as the background spacetime is deformed away from the Kerr geometry, chaos sets in, with its first onset most visible near strongly resonant bound orbits in the photon shell. We display two animations: one illustrating the emergence of chaos near the photon shell, which results in a fractal phase-space structure, and another exhibiting how this chaotic, fractal, self-similar structure is encoded in the first-return map.

### [56] [Inspirals into bosonic dark matter stars and chirp mimickers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08795)

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究使用完全相对论性微扰方法分析了极端质量比旋进系统，其中恒星质量致密天体围绕超大质量玻色子暗物质星（玻色星）运行。研究发现标量物质耗散可产生类似黑洞双星的啁啾引力波信号，使玻色星成为引力波啁啾模拟体，未来空间探测器可通过相位差区分这些信号。

Method: 采用完全相对论性微扰方法（fully relativistic perturbative methods）研究恒星质量致密天体围绕超大质量玻色子暗物质星的轨道运动。为支持波形建模，推导了在深度相对论区域仍保持精确的引力与标量能量通量（gravitational and scalar energy fluxes）的半解析公式。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，未来空间探测器如LISA可通过标量耗散引起的可测量相位差（measurable phase dephasings）区分这些模拟体信号与真实黑洞旋进。玻色星即使非超致密（ultracompact）也能模拟引力波啁啾信号，这对引力波天文学中的天体识别具有重要意义。

Abstract: We investigate extreme-mass-ratio inspirals in which a stellar-mass compact object orbits a supermassive bosonic dark matter star, modeled as a boson star, using fully relativistic perturbative methods. Unlike inspirals around electro-vacuum black holes, these systems can shed scalar matter through dynamical friction which significantly alters the inspiral dynamics. We show that this additional dissipation can induce a chirp-like gravitational-wave signal closely resembling that of black hole binaries, allowing boson stars to act as gravitational-wave chirp mimickers even when they are not ultracompact. The inspiral evolution and resulting waveform depend sensitively on the compactness of the central boson star: highly compact configurations trigger dipolar scalar radiation, leading to a rapid plunge, whereas less compact stars yield smoother inspirals dominated by gravitational and quadrupolar scalar waves. To support waveform modeling, we derive semi-analytical prescriptions for the gravitational and scalar energy fluxes that remain accurate deep into the relativistic regime. Our findings indicate that future space-based detectors such as LISA could distinguish these mimicker signals from true black hole inspirals through measurable phase dephasings induced by scalar dissipation.

### [57] [Images of the Thin Accretion Disk Around Kerr Black Holes coupled to time periodic scalar fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08796)

Conclusion: 结论表明几何薄吸积盘可以为同步标量发提供稳健的观测诊断，并为通过未来视界尺度黑洞成像观测测试张量-多标量引力提供了有前景的途径。即使在较弱标量化接近克尔几何的情况下，逆行盘对标量发的存在仍保持高度敏感性。

Abstract: We investigate the orbital structure and observable appearance of rotating Kerr black holes endowed with synchronized scalar hair described by two time-periodic scalar fields with a flat target-space geometry. The presence of scalar hair enriches the geodesic structure of the spacetime relative to the Kerr case and significantly modifies the emission properties of geometrically thin Novikov-Thorne accretion disks. Combining an analysis of timelike circular orbits with backward ray tracing, we show that the normalized scalar charge governs the morphology and luminosity of both prograde and counter-rotating disks. In the strongly scalarized regime, additional light rings and modified circular-orbit regions produce multiple inner emitting zones and strongly enhanced redshift patterns that depart markedly from the Kerr prediction. The most pronounced deviations occur in the counter-rotating sector, where scalar hair generates inner retrograde radiative rings with substantially enhanced luminosity and distinctive frequency-shift signatures. Even when the spacetime approaches the Kerr geometry at weaker scalarization, the retrograde disk remains highly sensitive to the presence of scalar hair. Our results demonstrate that geometrically thin accretion disks can provide robust observational diagnostics of synchronized scalar hair and may offer a promising avenue for testing tensor-multi-scalar gravity with future horizon-scale black-hole imaging observations.

### [58] [Extreme mass ratio head-on collisions of black holes in Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08839)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用光线追踪（ray-tracing）技术，在无限质量比假设下研究单个黑洞时空。分析了三种耦合函数家族：线性、二次型和特定指数形式，分别对应具有平移对称性（shift symmetry）的标量毛黑洞和自发标量化（spontaneously scalarized）黑洞。

Abstract: The evolution of the event horizon when two black holes merge can be determined by resorting to ray-tracing techniques on a single black hole spacetime, under the assumption that the binary's mass ratio is infinite and the underlying gravity theory respects the equivalence principle. We extend this analysis to the head-on collision of non-spinning hairy black holes in Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity. In such theories the scalar field is coupled to a higher curvature operator, leading to possible modifications of the background geometry and consequently of photon propagation. We study three families of coupling functions: linear, quadratic, and a particular exponential form. The first choice enjoys a shift symmetry and forces the presence of scalar hair in the spectrum of black hole solutions. The latter two couplings break the shift symmetry and allow for spontaneously scalarized hairy black holes, which coexist with the Schwarzschild black hole. For all three classes of theories studied, we find a merger duration that is longer than the corresponding time in general relativity, when keeping the size of the small black hole fixed, and for viably small values of the coupling constant. However, the case of the exponential coupling yields a non-monotonic merger duration, which can become shorter than the general relativity value for a sufficiently large coupling constant. We observe that the merger duration and the area increment generically track the behavior of the small black hole's photon ring. Finally, we also compare our results with recent numerical simulations by other groups, despite the dissimilar mass ratios considered.

### [61] [Dual Cutler-Vallisneri Corrections: Mitigating PSD Drift in Zero-Latency Gravitational-Wave Searches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09132)
*James Kennington*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究开发了针对最小相位白化（minimum-phase whitening）中谱漂移（spectral drift）的微扰修正框架，显著减少了引力波探测中的定时、相位和信噪比偏差，对提升早期预警精度至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最大化引力波搜索的合并前预警时间需要最小化算法延迟。虽然最小相位白化（minimum-phase whitening）提供了零延迟替代方案，但这种方法使分析暴露于谱漂移（spectral drift）问题，导致白化算子与静态模板库（template bank）产生偏差，从而影响匹配滤波度量（matched-filter metric）的准确性。

Method: 研究开发了一个微扰框架（perturbative framework），将Cutler-Vallisneri形式体系推广以处理度量误差，推导了定时、相位和信噪比（SNR）偏差的解析表达式。该框架通过精确的平稳相位模型（stationary-phase models）和数值注入（numerical injections）进行验证。

Result: 修正实现了小于1%的误差。应用于GWTC-4.0事件时发现，未修正的漂移会导致严重系统误差：探测器对定时偏差超过200微秒，相位偏移达0.2弧度，天空定位误差为5-10度。此外，信噪比（SNR）中位数损失为3-5%，异常值超过8%。

Conclusion: 虽然最小相位白化（minimum-phase whitening）能最大化早期预警窗口，但解析漂移修正对于维持未来观测运行中的探测体积和指向精度至关重要。该框架为引力波实时探测提供了重要的误差校正方法。

Abstract: Maximizing pre-merger warning times in gravitational-wave searches requires minimizing algorithmic latency. While current pipelines typically rely on truncated linear-phase filters, minimum-phase whitening offers a zero-latency alternative that eliminates the acausal look-ahead buffer. However, this causal approach exposes the analysis to spectral drift, where the whitening operator applied to live data diverges from the static template bank, creating a functional perturbation of the matched-filter metric. We develop a perturbative framework generalizing the Cutler-Vallisneri formalism to address these metric errors, deriving analytic expressions for the resulting timing, phase, and SNR biases. Validated against exact stationary-phase models and numerical injections, these corrections achieve $<1\%$ error. Applying this framework to GWTC-4.0 events with realistic 1-week power spectral density (PSD) lags, we find that uncorrected drift induces severe systematics: detector-pair timing biases exceeding $200 μ$s, phase shifts up to 0.2 rad, and sky-localization errors of $5^{\circ}-10^{\circ}$. Additionally, we observe a median signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) loss of $3-5\%$, with outliers exceeding $8\%$. These results demonstrate that while minimum-phase whitening maximizes the early-warning window, analytic drift corrections are essential to maintain detection volume and pointing accuracy in future observing runs.

</details>


### [62] [Gravitational waveforms and accretion characteristics in a quantum-corrected black hole without Cauchy horizons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09140)
*Shilong Huang,Jiawei Chen,Jinsong Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了无柯西视界量子修正黑洞的动力学与辐射特性，包括周期轨道、引力波和吸积盘辐射，揭示了量子参数对轨道稳定性、引力波相位和吸积盘辐射效率的影响。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强场区物理现象已成为探测量子修正引力（quantum-corrected gravity）的主要方法。本文旨在通过研究无柯西视界（Cauchy horizons）量子修正黑洞的多种观测特征，为未来区分量子修正几何与经典黑洞提供潜在的现象学支持。

Method: 首先分析赤道面内大质量粒子的轨迹方程，研究量子参数ζ对圆轨道稳定性的影响。进一步研究粒子的周期轨道特性，并计算极端质量比旋近（extreme mass-ratio inspirals）的引力波形。最后基于Novikov-Thorne薄吸积盘模型，评估该量子修正黑洞周围吸积盘的辐射特性。

Result: 量子参数ζ的增加导致最内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbit）和边际束缚轨道（marginally bound orbit）向外迁移，且粒子在这些轨道运动所需比角动量增加。量子修正引起引力波信号的累积相移，导致与经典史瓦西（Schwarzschild）情形相比显著失相。量子参数的引入抑制了吸积盘的辐射能流、有效温度和整体辐射效率。

Conclusion: 这些独特的动力学和辐射偏差为未来利用多种观测手段区分量子修正几何与经典黑洞提供了潜在的现象学支持。量子修正对轨道稳定性、引力波相位和吸积盘辐射效率的系统性影响构成了可观测的特征信号。

Abstract: The use of physical phenomena in the strong-field regime has become a primarily methodology for probing quantum-corrected gravity. This paper investigates periodic orbits, gravitational waves, and accretion disk radiation for a quantum-corrected black hole without Cauchy horizons. First, by analyzing the trajectory equations of massive particles in the equatorial plane, we study the influence of the quantum parameter $ζ$ on the stability of circular orbits. The results show that an increase in $ζ$ leads to an outward migration of both the innermost stable circular orbit and the marginally bound orbit, accompanied by an increase in the required specific angular momentum for particle motion on these two orbits. Then, we further investigate the periodic orbit characteristics of particles and compute the associated gravitational waveforms for extreme mass-ratio inspirals. It is demonstrated that quantum corrections induce a cumulative phase shift in the gravitational wave signal, leading to significant dephasing compared to the classical Schwarzschild case. Furthermore, based on the Novikov-Thorne thin accretion disk model, we evaluate the radiation characteristics of the accretion disk around this quantum-corrected black hole. The results indicate that the introduction of the quantum parameter suppresses the radiant energy flux, effective temperature, and overall radiative efficiency of the disk. These distinctive dynamical and radiative deviations provide potential phenomenological support for distinguishing quantum-corrected geometries from classical black holes using multiple observational means in the future.

### [63] [Binary Black Hole inspirals cannot hide their eccentricity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09150)
*Johann Fernandes,Praveer Tiwari,Archana Pai*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种改进的唯象学方法，用于从引力波数据中快速约束致密双星并合系统的轨道偏心率（eccentricity）。该方法在时频域中使用有效啁啾质量模型，结合改进的像素收集方法和基于似然函数的采样技术，能够在5分钟内提供合理的偏心率估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LIGO Virgo KAGRA合作组在过去10年探测到的致密双星并合事件均未显示出明确的偏心率特征。随着现有探测网络的升级和下一代引力波探测器的发展，探测偏心率系统的可能性将增加，因此需要开发快速有效的偏心率约束方法。

Method: 研究改进了在时频域中使用有效啁啾质量模型（effective chirp mass model）提供偏心率约束的唯象学方法。引入了改进的像素收集方法（pixel collection method）以及受贝叶斯参数估计启发的基于似然函数的采样方法，通过时频表示中不同偏心率谐波（eccentric harmonics）收集能量的乘积构建似然函数。

Result: 在500个无自旋等质量偏心率系统上的测试表明，该方法能够将偏心率约束在真实值±0.2范围内。在50核机器上仅需5分钟即可提供这些约束，证明了该方法的快速性和合理准确性。

Conclusion: 该唯象学方法能够提供快速且合理的偏心率估计，使其成为快速引力波数据分析的有前景工具。该方法还通过整合偏心率谐波间的能量比信息进一步优化了偏心率估计。

Abstract: The events detected by the LIGO Virgo KAGRA collaboration over a period of 10 years have yielded a treasure trove of signals from compact binary coalescences. None of these events have shown a confident signature of eccentricity. With upgrades to the existing network and potential next generation gravitational wave detectors, we will be able to see much further into the universe increasing the likelihood of detecting eccentric systems. We improve upon the phenomenological approach of providing eccentricity constraints using an effective chirp mass model in the time frequency domain. We introduce an improved pixel collection method along with a likelihood based sampling approach inspired by Bayesian parameter estimation. Our approach constructs a likelihood from the product of energies collected across different eccentric harmonics in the time frequency representation. This formulation enables coarse but meaningful constraints on orbital eccentricity. Additionally, we incorporate information from the energy ratios between eccentric harmonics, further refining the eccentricity estimates. We test our approach on 500 non spinning equal mass eccentric systems and demonstrate that we can constrain the eccentricity within 0.2 around the true value. Moreover, our approach can deliver these constraints in 5 minutes on a machine with 50 cores. These results demonstrate that our phenomenological approach provides fast and reasonably accurate eccentricity estimates, making it a promising tool for rapid gravitational wave data analysis.

### [64] [Shadows of quintessence black holes: spherical accretion, photon trajectories, and geodesic observers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09159)
*Ji-Wen Li,Zi-Liang Wang,Tao-Tao Sui*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了quintessence-like场对黑洞阴影的影响，重点分析了观测者运动状态对阴影角尺寸测量的影响，并应用于M87*的观测数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: quintessence-like场通过吸积流动力学、光子轨迹和观测者运动三种机制影响黑洞阴影。由于quintessence修正时空的非渐近平坦性质，需要研究自由下落（测地线）观测者，而非传统静态观测者假设。

Method: 采用微扰方法推导事件视界位置、光子球半径、最内稳定圆轨道和临界撞击参数的解析表达式。计算静态和下落球对称吸积流的观测强度剖面，分析不同运动状态观测者的测量差异。

Result: 光子球半径和临界撞击参数是时空的不变性质，但阴影的视角尺寸强烈依赖于观测者的运动和位置。自由下落观测者测量的角半径系统性地小于同半径处的静态观测者，而自由出射观测者测量值更大，符合相对论像差效应。

Conclusion: 在非渐近平坦时空中，仅凭撞击参数不足以表征观测到的角结构。应用于事件视界望远镜对M87*的观测，更负的状态方程导致对quintessence参数更强的约束，且基本独立于观测者设定。研究强调了在非渐近平坦黑洞时空的阴影研究中明确定义观测者的重要性。

Abstract: The presence of a quintessence-like field can influence the black hole shadow through three primary mechanisms: the dynamics of accretion flows, the trajectories of photons, and the motion of observers. Unlike standard shadow analyses that assume a static observer at spatial infinity, the non-asymptotically flat nature of quintessence-corrected spacetimes motivates the consideration of freely falling (geodesic) observers. Using a perturbative approach, we derive analytical expressions for the event-horizon location, photon-sphere radius, innermost stable circular orbit, and critical impact parameter. We compute the observed intensity profiles for both static and infalling spherical accretion flows. We find that, although the photon-sphere radius and the critical impact parameter are invariant properties of the spacetime, the apparent angular size of the shadow depends sensitively on the observer's motion and location. Freely infalling observers systematically measure smaller angular radii than static observers at the same radius, whereas freely outgoing observers measure larger ones, in agreement with relativistic aberration. In contrast to the Schwarzschild case, the impact parameter alone is insufficient to characterize the observed angular structure in non-asymptotically flat spacetimes. Applying our results to the Event Horizon Telescope observation of M87$^\ast$, we show that more negative equations of state lead to stronger constraints on the quintessence parameter, largely independent of the observer prescription. Our analysis highlights the importance of carefully specifying the observer in shadow studies of non-asymptotically flat black-hole spacetimes.

We find that the results obtained through the asymptotic iteration method (AIM) are in good agreement with those obtained by the WKB method. Importantly, the Bernstein spectral method is employed as a rigorous cross-check for QNFs in the $l=0$ scalar perturbation sector, where the WKB approximation is often unreliable.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用了一种混合方法，将匹配滤波概念与卷积神经网络（Convolutional Neural Networks）相结合，无需依赖传统的χ²拒绝检验（χ² rejection test）。该方法使用包含高斯噪声、瞬态噪声以及模板库未包含的物理效应（如轨道偏心率、进动和高阶模式）的模拟数据集进行验证。

Conclusion: 深度学习辅助搜索能够支持未来探测器时代的可持续引力波数据分析。该混合方法为应对下一代干涉仪带来的计算挑战提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Gravitational wave searches rely on a combination of methods, including matched filtering, coherent analyses, and more recent machine learning based pipelines. For compact binary coalescences, where signals originate from the relativistic dynamics of compact objects, matched filtering remains a central element, but its computational cost will increase substantially with the data volumes and parameter-space coverage required by next-generation interferometers such as the Einstein Telescope. Developing complementary strategies that reduce computational load while preserving detection performance is therefore essential. We investigate a hybrid approach that combines matched-filtering concepts with Convolutional Neural Networks, enabling efficient signal searches without relying on the usual $χ^2$ rejection test. Using simulated data sets that include injected signals in Gaussian noise, transient noise, and physical effects not represented in template bank, such as eccentricity, precession and higher-order modes, we show that the method achieves a detection efficiency comparable to a standard matched-filtering search while offering a more resource efficient pipeline. These results indicate that deep learning assisted searches can support sustainable gravitational-wave data analysis in future detector eras.

### [67] [Relativistic Corrections to the Formation Rate of Extreme Mass-Ratio Inspirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09547)

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究构建了一个相对论自洽的解析框架来估计极端质量比旋进（EMRI）事件率，发现相对于牛顿处理，纳入相对论效应可将预测的EMRI率提高约8倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）是长时引力波源，其形成机制涉及两体弛豫驱动的随机角动量扩散与引力波辐射引起的耗散演化之间的相互作用。现有牛顿处理可能低估EMRI率，需要建立相对论自洽框架为空间引力波探测器（如LISA和Taiji）提供更准确的事件率估计。

Method: 在史瓦西时空（Schwarzschild spacetime）中，将标准损失锥角动量推广为能量依赖量，并使用广义相对论推导的最小稳定半径修正了坠入近心点（plunge pericenter）。构建了一个相对论自洽的解析框架来估计EMRI事件率。

Result: 相对于牛顿处理，纳入相对论效应使预测的EMRI率提高约8倍。这种增强效应在较浅的恒星密度分布中更为显著，且对中心大质量黑洞的质量不敏感，表明相对论效应对于EMRI率估计至关重要。

Conclusion: 相对论效应对于空间引力波探测器（如LISA和Taiji）相关的EMRI率估计至关重要，建立的相对论自洽框架显著提高了事件率预测的准确性，强调了在引力波天体物理研究中必须考虑广义相对论效应。

Abstract: Extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) are long-duration gravitational-wave sources in which a compact object gradually spirals into a massive black hole. Their formation is governed by the interplay between stochastic angular-momentum diffusion driven by two-body relaxation and the dissipative evolution caused by gravitational-wave emission, with the loss-cone boundary deciding whether an object undergoes an inspiral or a direct plunge. Building on this physical picture, we construct a relativistically self-consistent analytic framework for estimating EMRI event rates. In Schwarzschild spacetime, we generalize the standard loss-cone angular momentum to an energy-dependent quantity and revise the plunge pericenter by using the minimum stable radius derived from general relativity. Relative to the Newtonian treatment, we show that incorporating these relativistic effects increases the predicted EMRI rates by roughly a factor of 8. This enhancement becomes more pronounced for shallower stellar density profiles and is insensitive to the mass of the central massive black hole, which emphasizes that relativistic effects are essential for EMRI rate estimations that are relevant for space-based gravitational-wave detectors, such as LISA and Taiji.

### [68] [Dynamics of quadratic f(R) cosmology with a perfect fluid: Jordan and Einstein frames](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09667)
*Artur Alho,Margarida Lima,Filipe C. Mena*

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了广义爱因斯坦理论的纯二次引力理论在平坦均匀各向同性宇宙模型中的全局动力学，分别在Jordan框架和Einstein框架中建立了三维动力系统，并通过单调性分析、轨道结构表征和奇点去奇异化等方法获得了全局流描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索广义爱因斯坦理论的纯二次引力理论（pure quadratic theories of gravity）在宇宙学背景下的全局动力学行为，特别是在平坦均匀各向同性（spatially flat homogeneous and isotropic）宇宙模型中，使用完美流体（perfect fluid）作为物质源。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）在Jordan框架和共形相关的Einstein框架中引入全局且规则的三维动力系统（global and regular 3-dimensional dynamical systems' formulations）；2）在Jordan框架中分析内部流的单调性（monotonicity properties），表征二维不变边界上的轨道结构，并对非双曲不动点进行去奇异化（desingularisation）；3）在Einstein框架中利用状态空间的斜积结构（skew-product structure）分析轨道结构。

Result: 研究结果获得了两种框架下动力系统的全局流描述及其极限集（limit sets），通过渐近展开（asymptotic expansions）识别了可以从Jordan框架全局共形映射到Einstein框架的解，以及那些不能全局映射的解。

Conclusion: 该研究为纯二次引力理论在宇宙学模型中的动力学行为提供了完整的全局分析框架，揭示了Jordan框架和Einstein框架之间的共形映射关系及其局限性，深化了对广义引力理论动力学特性的理解。

Abstract: We investigate the global dynamics of the field equations of (pure) quadratic theories of gravity which generalise Einstein's theory in spatially flat homogeneous and isotropic cosmological models with a perfect fluid. We introduce global and regular 3-dimensional dynamical systems' formulations, on both the Jordan frame and the conformally related Einstein frame. The analysis in the Jordan frame explores the monotonicity properties of the interior flow which, together with the characterisation of the orbit structure on the 2-dimensional invariant boundaries and the desingularisation of non-hyperbolic fixed points, provides a global description of the flow and its limit sets. In the Einstein frame, the analysis uses the skew-product structure of the Einstein state space and the characterisation of the orbit structure on the 2-dimensional invariant boundaries. Furthermore, by obtaining asymptotic expansions we identify the solutions that are global conformally mapped from the Jordan frame to the Einstein frame and those that are not.

### [69] [Cosmological Spacetimes with Sign-Changing Spatial Curvature and Topological Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09812)
*Gerardo García-Moreno,Bert Janssen,Alejandro Jiménez Cano,Marc Mars,Miguel Sánchez,Raül Vera*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了在FLRW宇宙学模型中，通过将空间曲率k推广为时间依赖函数k(t)，允许宇宙从闭合到开放的拓扑转变，从而避免大爆炸后物质能量无限的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于FLRW度规的宇宙学模型支持欧几里得空间扇区，但这意味着大爆炸后物质和能量的总量必须是无限的。避免这一含义的唯一途径是宇宙从闭合到开放的转变，而这在标准FLRW模型中被禁止。

Method: 通过将FLRW时空中的空间曲率k推广为时间依赖函数k→k(t)，允许其改变符号，从而允许常数t切片的拓扑发生变化。作者构建了三种不同的几何结构，使用不同的常曲率空间表示，并分析其全局性质。

Result: 研究表明，当共动时间（comoving time）与柯西时间（Cauchy time）不同时，这种拓扑转变与全局双曲性（global hyperbolicity）一致。作者识别了保持全局双曲性的温和条件，并表征了它们的基灵向量（Killing vectors），证明了球对称时空的一般结果。

Conclusion: 通过允许空间曲率随时间变化，可以构造出允许宇宙拓扑转变的几何结构，这些结构在特定条件下保持全局双曲性，为解决标准FLRW模型中的无限物质能量问题提供了理论可能性。

Abstract: Observational evidence, together with practical computations and modeling, supports a Euclidean spatial sector in the current cosmological model based on the FLRW metric. This, however, would imply that the total amount of matter and energy immediately after the Big Bang must have been infinite, an implication that could only be avoided through a transition from a closed to an open universe, a process forbidden in standard FLRW models. In this article, we investigate the spacetimes resulting from promoting the spatial curvature $k$ in FLRW spacetimes to a time-dependent function, $k \to k(t)$, allowing it to change sign and thereby allowing changes in the topology of the constant-$t$ slices. Although previously dismissed due to a classical theorem by Geroch, such transitions are shown to be consistent with global hyperbolicity when the comoving time is distinct from a Cauchy time, as recent work by one of the authors demonstrates. We construct three distinct geometries exhibiting this behavior using different representations of constant-curvature spaces. We analyze their global properties and identify mild conditions under which they remain globally hyperbolic. Furthermore, we characterize their Killing vectors, proving a general result for spherically symmetric spacetimes and compare them with known geometries in the literature.

</details>


### [70] [An asymptotic proof of the classical log soft graviton theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09844)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究经典对数软引力子定理在渐近框架内的推导，特别关注时间反演协变性和入射软辐射的贡献，旨在理解软因子中未来与过去硬分量不对称性的渐近起源。

Result: 在无入射记忆（incoming memory）的情况下，恢复了标准的对数软因子（log soft factor），该因子显示出未来与过去硬分量之间的不对称性。从渐近视角看，这种不对称性源于引力场在空间无穷远处的长期已知的不连续性。

Conclusion: 该推导完全具有时间反演协变性并包含了入射软辐射的贡献，揭示了软引力子定理中不对称性的渐近起源与引力场在空间无穷远的不连续性直接相关。

Abstract: We present a derivation of the classical log soft graviton theorem within the asymptotic framework of Compère, Gralla, and Wei. The approach is fully covariant under time reversal and incorporates contributions from incoming soft radiation. In the absence of incoming memory one recovers the standard log soft factor, which features an asymmetry between future and past hard components. ### [71] [Globally stable, ghost-free hyperbolic square-root deformation of the Starobinsky model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09944)
*Andrei Galiautdinov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种精确解析的Starobinsky模型变形，通过双曲平方根函数消除二次f(R)引力中的强耦合奇点，同时保持低曲率下的广义相对论和暴胀平台，预测了与观测一致的宇宙学参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决二次f(R)引力中当f'(R)=0时出现的强耦合奇点问题，同时保持Starobinsky模型的成功特征，如低曲率下的广义相对论恢复和暴胀平台。

Method: 采用几何双曲平方根函数$f'(R) = αR + \sqrt{α^2 R^2 + 1}$作为拉格朗日导数，确保f'(R)严格为正，从而消除奇点。在爱因斯坦框架中，标量子动力学由全局定义的势函数$V(φ)$描述。

Result: 该模型成功消除了强耦合奇点，保证了全局无鬼粒子（ghost-free）和无快子（tachyon-free）的宇宙演化。对于N=60的暴胀e-折叠数，预测标量谱指数$n_s \simeq 0.967$和张量标量比$r \simeq 0.00083$，与Planck和BICEP/Keck观测约束一致。

Conclusion: 提出的双曲平方根变形为Starobinsky模型提供了一个全局稳定、无奇点的理论框架，既能消除二次f(R)引力的病理分支，又能保持观测上成功的暴胀预测，为非奇异反弹宇宙学提供了稳健机制。

Abstract: We propose an exact, analytic deformation of the Starobinsky model governed by the strictly positive derivative of its Lagrangian, $f'(R) = αR + \sqrt{α^2 R^2 + 1}$, with $α> 0$. This geometric hyperbolic square-root ansatz is designed to eliminate the well-known strong-coupling singularity that arises in quadratic $f(R)$ gravity when $f'(R)=0$. The construction seamlessly recovers general relativity at low curvatures and preserves the successful slow-roll inflationary plateau at extreme positive curvatures. In the limit $R \to -\infty$, the derivative $f'(R)$ asymptotes to zero strictly from above, removing the pathological branch associated with the vanishing of $f'(R)$. This guarantees that the only admissible constant-curvature ($R=A$) solutions correspond to standard Einstein spaces with an effective cosmological constant $Λ_{\text{eff}} \equiv A/4$. The first and second derivatives of the action, as well as the scalaron mass squared, remain strictly positive globally, ensuring a perfectly ghost-free and tachyon-free cosmological evolution across the entire spacetime manifold. In the Einstein frame, the dynamics of the scalaron is governed by the globally defined potential $V(φ) = \frac{1}{8α} [ 1 - (1 + 2\sqrt{2/3}φ) \exp(-2\sqrt{2/3}φ) ] + Λ\exp(-2\sqrt{2/3}φ)$, which naturally establishes an impenetrable energetic wall as $φ\to -\infty$, offering a robust, globally stable mechanism for non-singular bouncing cosmologies. For $N = 60$ inflationary e-folds, the model predicts a scalar spectral index of $n_s \simeq 0.967$ and a strongly suppressed tensor-to-scalar ratio of $r \simeq 0.00083$, which position the proposed theory within the observationally favored parameter space of the Planck and BICEP/Keck Array baseline constraints.

</details>


### [72] [Strong deflection of massive particles via the geodesic deviation equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09946)
*Takahisa Igata,Yohsuke Takamori*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究建立了渐近平坦、静态、球对称时空（asymptotically flat, static, and spherically symmetric spacetimes）中类时测地线（timelike geodesics）粒子散射的强偏转极限（strong deflection limit）公式。当角动量从上方趋近临界值时，粒子无限接近不稳定圆形轨道，偏转角呈对数发散（diverges logarithmically），其系数由临界轨迹的径向不稳定性指数（radial instability exponent）决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在为类时测地线粒子在特定时空背景下的散射行为建立严格的强偏转极限理论框架。这有助于深入理解粒子在接近不稳定圆形轨道时的动力学特性，并为相关物理现象提供几何解释。

Method: 采用测地线偏离方程（geodesic deviation equation）进行协变分析，推导出对数发散系数的表达式。将径向不稳定性指数用不稳定圆形轨道上的局部曲率数据表示，从而建立运动学与几何学的双重解释框架。

Result: 研究发现偏转角在角动量趋近临界值时呈对数发散，其系数由临界轨迹的径向不稳定性指数决定。在广义相对论（general relativity）中，该指数的物质依赖性仅通过由静态参考系能量密度（static-frame energy density）以及径向和切向主压力（principal radial and tangential pressures）构成的单一局部标量组合体现。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了类时测地线散射的强偏转极限理论，为粒子在接近不稳定圆形轨道时的散射行为提供了完整的运动学和几何学描述。所得结果揭示了广义相对论中物质对强偏转行为的简化依赖关系。

Abstract: We develop a formulation of the strong deflection limit for the scattering of particles following timelike geodesics in asymptotically flat, static, and spherically symmetric spacetimes. For fixed specific energy, as the angular momentum approaches its critical value from above, the particle passes arbitrarily close to the associated unstable circular orbit, undergoes many windings around it, and the deflection angle diverges logarithmically. Using the geodesic deviation equation, we show covariantly that the coefficient of this logarithmic divergence is determined by the radial instability exponent of the critical trajectory, defined per unit azimuthal angle. We express this instability exponent in terms of local curvature data on the unstable circular orbit, thereby providing both kinematic and geometric interpretations of the strong deflection limit. In general relativity, its matter dependence enters only through a single local scalar combination constructed from the static-frame energy density and the principal radial and tangential pressures.

### [73] [Interaction of the gravitational Hawking radiation and a static point mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09948)
*João P. B. Brito,Atsushi Higuchi,Luís C. B. Crispino*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究分析了施瓦西黑洞外由弦支撑的静态点质量应力-能量张量与霍金辐射引力子的相互作用。研究发现，在Unruh态中该应力-能量张量对热引力子的总响应率是有限的，且黑洞尺寸起到了自然红外截断的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探讨施瓦西黑洞外由弦支撑的静态点质量应力-能量张量与霍金辐射引力子的相互作用。特别关注对比该体系与Rindler时空中类似体系的响应特性，以理解黑洞如何影响量子引力效应。

Method: 研究方法包括推导Unruh态中应力-能量张量对热引力子总响应率的闭合解析表达式。该Unruh态模拟了引力塌缩形成的球对称黑洞时空中的量子态。同时比较了黑洞视界附近的响应率与Rindler时空中的响应率。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）Unruh态中应力-能量张量对热引力子的总响应率是有限的，与Rindler时空中红外发散的响应率形成对比；2）黑洞尺寸起到了自然红外截断（infrared cutoff）的作用；3）Hartle-Hawking态中来自过去类光无限远的引力子响应率为零；4）Unruh态和Hartle-Hawking态中引力子的总响应率相同。

Conclusion: 结论表明，黑洞尺寸为量子引力效应提供了自然红外截断机制。对于引力子相互作用，Unruh态和Hartle-Hawking态中的总响应率相同，这与电磁场中静态电荷的情况类似，但与无质量标量场中的静态源情况不同。

Abstract: We study the interaction of a stress-energy tensor describing a static point mass supported by a string outside a Schwarzschild black hole with the gravitons of the Hawking radiation. We derive a closed-form analytic expression for the total response rate of this stress-energy tensor to the thermal gravitons in the Unruh state, which models the quantum state in the spacetime of a spherically symmetric black hole formed by gravitational collapse. This response rate is finite in contrast with the infrared divergent response rate for a static point mass supported by a string in Rindler spacetime, i.e., a point mass accelerated uniformly by a string in Minkowski spacetime. By comparing the response rate near the black hole horizon with that in Rindler spacetime, we show that the size of the black hole acts as a natural infrared cutoff. We also find that the response rate of this stress-energy tensor to the thermal gravitons incoming from past null infinity in the Hartle-Hawking state vanishes. As a result, the total response rate of a static point mass (supported by a string) in the Unruh and Hartle-Hawking states for gravitons are identical. This is also the case for a static charge interacting with the electromagnetic field but not for a static source for a massless scalar field.

Method: 方法基于控制复场绝对值的两点映射（two-point map）的存在性，该映射产生相对于格点任意中心化的驻波。首先推导稳态解，然后以此为基础构建非零速度的波。

Abstract: We construct a novel family of exact cnoidal wave and soliton solutions of the focusing and defocusing Ablowitz-Ladik equations. Unlike cnoidal waves that were obtained by earlier authors, the phase variable of the new solutions exhibits a nonlinear dependence on time and site number; the wave ``swings". Our approach hinges on the existence of a two-point map governing the absolute value of the complex field; this map gives rise to standing waves centred arbitrarily relative to the lattice sites. Having derived stationary solutions, we use these as a basis for constructing waves with nonzero velocity. The localised members of the new family comprise dark solitons with the nontrivial asymptotic behaviour. We identify periodic and quasiperiodic patterns and establish an explicit quantisation rule for the velocity of the wave circulating in a closed loop of $N$ sites.

Result: 研究结果显示：在约束参数范围内，黑洞参数显著影响粒子的有效势、角速度、比能量和比角动量；磁荷-PFDM黑洞在给定半径处的局部辐射通量和温度低于史瓦西黑洞，但其整体辐射效率和总光度更高；参数还控制着流体速度、密度分布和黑洞质量吸积率。

Abstract: This paper investigates the dynamical behavior of steady spherical accretion onto a static, magnetically charged black hole embedded in a perfect fluid dark matter (PFDM) background. Using the shadow observations of M87* from the Event Horizon Telescope (EHT), we establish constraints on the parameter space for the magnetic charge and the PFDM parameter. Within this constrained range, we analyze the orbital dynamics of particles in a thin accretion disk surrounding the black hole and find that the black hole parameters significantly influence the effective potential, angular velocity, specific energy, and specific angular momentum of the particles. Subsequently, we calculate the radiative energy flux, temperature profile, and observed spectrum of the disk. Our results show that, while the local radiative flux and temperature at a given radius are lower for the charged-PFDM black hole compared to a Schwarzschild black hole, its overall radiative efficiency and total luminosity are higher. Finally, we explore the spherically symmetric, steady-state accretion process around the black hole, revealing how the parameters govern how the fluid velocity, density profile, and black hole mass accretion rate are influenced.

### [76] [Synchrotron radiation leveling at future circular hadron colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08923)
*Frank Zimmermann*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的同步辐射功率平整（synchrotron radiation power leveling）方法，通过调节束流能量来保持同步辐射功率在限制值以下，从而提高FCC-hh对撞机的峰值和积分亮度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对于未来环形强子对撞机如FCC-hh，同步辐射在70-90 TeV质心能量下变得显著，辐射阻尼时间约为数小时。强烈的同步辐射不仅导致发射度快速收缩，还会在超导磁体中产生显著热负荷，可能限制总束流电流。

Method: 提出同步辐射功率平整方法：在物理运行期间调整束流能量，可以是连续调节或离散步骤，同时束流电流下降，以保持同步辐射功率在或低于特定限制值。文中展示了FCC-hh同步辐射平整的两个示例运行场景。

Result: 与固定束流能量运行相比，该方法提高了FCC-hh的峰值和积分亮度。虽然最高对撞能量下的积分亮度没有大幅减少，但同步辐射平整能显著增加低能量下已发生关键过程的粒子数。例如，双希格斯（di-Higgs）产生事件数增加了60%或更多。

Conclusion: 同步辐射功率平整是一种有前景的运行模式，FCC-hh探测器特别是物理事件分析需要为此新运行模式做好准备。该方法在保持辐射功率限制的同时，优化了对撞机的整体性能。

Abstract: Luminosity leveling to limit the event pile up is a key ingredient of the LHC luminosity upgrade, the High-Luminosity LHC (HL-LHC). For a future circular hadron collider, such as the FCC-hh, operating at a centre-of-mass energy of 70-90 TeV, synchrotron radiation becomes significant, with radiation damping times of the order of one or a few hours. The rapid shrinkage of the emittance may call for a leveling of the beam-beam tune shift or of the event pile up, as previously explored. However, the strong synchrotron radiation emitted inside the cold superconducting magnets also represents a significant heat load and is likely to limit the total beam current. In this article, we discuss a new approach, namely synchrotron radiation power leveling, where the beam energy is adjusted during a physics store, either continually or in a few discrete steps, while the beam current decreases, so as to keep the synchrotron radiation power at or below a certain limiting value. In this way, both peak and integrated luminosity of the FCC-hh are increased, compared with operation at a fixed beam energy. The FCC-hh detectors, and in particular the physics event analysis, need to be prepared for this novel mode of operation. This article presents two example running scenarios for synchrotron radiation leveling at the FCC-hh. While not greatly reducing the integrated luminosity at highest collision energy, synchrotron-radiation leveling can significantly increase the number of events for key processes already occurring at lower energy. As an example, we show that it raises the number of di-Higgs production events by 60% or more.

### [77] [Canonical Criterion for Third-Order Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09124)
*Fangfang Wang,Wei Liu,Kai Qi,Zidong Cui,Ying Tang,Zengru Di*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微正则拐点分析（MIPA）虽然能从微正则熵的导数识别三阶相变，但这些相变是否具有直接的规范表述一直不明确。研究旨在建立基于涨落的规范框架来填补这一理论空白。

Method: 提出基于累积比（cumulant-ratio）的准则，其符号极值定义了规范对应物，在单鞍点区域与微正则分类渐近关联。该方法仅依赖能量累积量，避免了显式的态密度重构，适用于非平衡稳态。

Result: 该框架揭示了依赖性和独立性的三阶相变作为低阶相变周围的涨落重组：无序侧前兆和有序侧重构。在Onsager二维伊辛解、有限尺寸Potts模型和驱动非互易伊辛模型上的基准测试验证了该框架的理论基础和广泛适用性。

Conclusion: 建立的基于涨落的规范框架为三阶相变提供了直接且可操作的规范表述，将微正则分类与规范对应联系起来，适用于平衡和非平衡系统，扩展了相变分析的理论工具。

Abstract: Microcanonical inflection-point analysis (MIPA) identifies third-order transitions from derivatives of the microcanonical entropy, but whether such transitions admit a direct canonical formulation has remained unclear. Here we establish a fluctuation-based canonical framework for third-order transitions through a cumulant-ratio criterion whose signed extrema define their canonical counterparts and, in the single-saddle regime, are asymptotically linked to microcanonical classification. Because the criterion depends only on energy cumulants, it avoids explicit density-of-states reconstruction and remains operational in nonequilibrium steady states. Physically, it reveals dependent and independent third-order transitions as fluctuation reorganizations around low-order transitions, namely disordered-side precursors and ordered-side restructuring. Benchmarks on Onsager's two-dimensional Ising solution, finite size Potts models, and a driven nonreciprocal Ising model show that the framework is theoretically grounded and broadly applicable.

### [78] [Rényi exponent landscape of multipartite entanglement in free-fermion systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08991)
*Aleksandrs Sokolovs*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究自由费米子系统多部分纠缠（multipartite entanglement）的标度行为，特别是Rényi三部分信息$I_3^{(α)}$在低密度极限下的特性。关注α依赖的标度行为与二分熵（bipartite entropy）的差异，以及整数Rényi指数的反常现象。

Method: 采用解析推导与数值验证相结合的方法。推导了系数$c(w_A, w_B, w_D)$的乘积公式，证明了包含-排除矩（inclusion-exclusion moments）的m部分生成函数，并通过高精度数值计算验证了所有结果。

Result: 在秩-1区域（rank-1 regime，$z = k_F w \ll 1$），$I_3^{(α)}$受到两个竞争通道的贡献：分数动量通道$\sim z^α$（对非整数α有效）和来自第一个非零包含-排除矩$σ_m$的多项式通道$\sim z^m$。这导致m个相邻条带的m部分信息的标度指数为$β_m(α) = \min(α, m)$。

Conclusion: 整数Rényi指数$α= 2, 3, \ldots$表现出反常行为：分数通道关闭，指数跃迁至$m$或更高。这导致副本阻碍（replica obstruction）：对于所有整数$n \geq 2$，$I_m^{(n)}/I_m^{(1)} \sim z^{m-1} \to 0$，使得主导冯·诺依曼信号无法从整数Rényi数据中重建。相反，基于负性（negativity-based）的测量（$α= 1/2$）相比冯·诺依曼熵提供了20倍的增强信号。

Abstract: We show that the Rényi tripartite information $I_3^{(α)}$ of free fermions exhibits a qualitatively $α$-dependent scaling at small Fermi momentum, in sharp contrast to bipartite entropy where only the prefactor changes. In the rank-1 regime ($z = k_F w \ll 1$), $I_3^{(α)}$ receives contributions from two competing channels -- a fractional-moment channel $\sim z^α$ (active for non-integer $α$) and a polynomial channel $\sim z^m$ from the first nonvanishing inclusion-exclusion moment $σ_m$ -- yielding the scaling exponent $β_m(α) = \min(α, m)$ for $m$-partite information of $m$ adjacent strips. Integer Rényi indices $α= 2, 3, \ldots$ are anomalous: the fractional channel closes and the exponent jumps to $m$ or higher. A direct consequence is a replica obstruction: $I_m^{(n)}/I_m^{(1)} \sim z^{m-1} \to 0$ for all integer $n \geq 2$, so the leading von Neumann signal cannot be reconstructed from integer Rényi data at the level of leading scaling -- a situation with no bipartite analog. Conversely, negativity-based measures ($α= 1/2$) give a $20\times$ enhanced signal compared to von Neumann. We derive the underlying product formula for the coefficient $c(w_A, w_B, w_D)$, prove an $m$-partite generating function for the inclusion-exclusion moments, and verify all results numerically to high precision.

</details>


### [79] [Asymmetric simple exclusion process with tree-like network branches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09694)
*Yuki Ishiguro,Yasunobu Ando*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于模拟质子传导固体氧化物中沿氧网络的质子传输。传统的非对称简单排他过程（asymmetric simple exclusion process, ASEP）虽然是一维晶格上描述非对称多粒子扩散与硬核相互作用的基本随机模型，但需要扩展以处理更复杂的网络结构。

Method: 方法是将ASEP扩展到具有树状网络分支的一维主干晶格上，推导该网络ASEP的精确稳态分布。通过考虑两种代表性网络几何结构（其物理量可用特定超几何级数表达），分析网络几何对传输特性的影响。

Result: 获得了网络ASEP的精确稳态分布，并阐明了网络几何结构如何影响传输特性。通过两种代表性网络几何的案例分析，展示了物理量可通过超几何级数（hypergeometric series）表达，从而量化几何结构对传输的影响。

Conclusion: 研究成功将ASEP扩展到具有树状分支的网络结构，为质子传输等非平衡输运现象提供了更精确的模型。网络几何结构被证明是影响传输特性的关键因素，该模型为复杂网络中的非平衡输运研究提供了新工具。

Abstract: The asymmetric simple exclusion process (ASEP) is a fundamental stochastic model describing asymmetric many-particle diffusion with hard-core interactions on a one-dimensional lattice, and has been widely applied in the study of nonequilibrium transport phenomena. Motivated by the modeling of proton transport along oxygen networks in proton-conducting solid oxides, we extend the ASEP to a model defined on a one-dimensional backbone lattice with tree-like network branches. We derive the exact stationary distribution of this network ASEP and investigate its transport properties. By considering two representative network geometries for which physical quantities can be expressed in terms of certain hypergeometric series, we elucidate how the network geometry influences transport properties.

### [80] [Diffusive flux into a stochastically gated tube](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09841)
*Sean D Lawley*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文扩展了随机门控（stochastically gated）扩散影响反应的流量估计，使其适用于非窄管和不同扩散系数的场景，并通过理论推导和随机模拟验证了估计公式的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机开闭门控（gates）的扩散影响反应（diffusion-influenced reactions）在生物物理和生化场景中已被研究数十年。先前研究估计了从大体积储层到窄管末端、具有随机门控入口的扩散通量（diffusive flux），但该估计存在局限性。

Method: 本文扩展了门控通量估计，使其适用于两种更具挑战性的情况：一是管子不一定是窄管，这涉及复杂的三维几何；二是管内与体相扩散系数不同，这会引入乘性噪声（multiplicative noise）。

Result: 推导出了显式的通量估计公式，并证明该公式在特定参数范围内是精确的。进一步使用随机模拟（stochastic simulations）表明，该估计在非常广泛的参数范围内保持准确。

Conclusion: 本文结果与先前关于扩展（i）和（ii）的研究不同，成功将门控通量估计推广到更一般的几何和扩散条件，为相关生物物理和生化系统提供了更广泛适用的分析工具。

Abstract: Diffusion-influenced reactions in the presence of gates which randomly open and close have been studied for decades in a variety of biophysical and biochemical scenarios. The diffusive flux from a large bulk reservoir to the end of a narrow tube with a stochastically gated entrance has been previously estimated. In this paper, we extend this gated flux estimate to be valid if (i) the tube is not necessarily narrow and/or (ii) the diffusivity differs in the tube versus the bulk. Extension (i) is challenging because it entails a nontrivial three-dimensional geometry. Extension (ii) is challenging because it introduces multiplicative noise. We derive an explicit flux estimate formula and prove that it is exact in certain parameter regimes. We further use stochastic simulations to show that the estimate remains accurate across a very broad range of parameters. Our results differ from prior work on extensions (i) and (ii).

</details>


### [81] [Non-equilibrium generalized Langevin equation for multi-dimensional observables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09850)
*Benjamin J. A. Héry,Lucas Tepper,Andrea Guljas,Artem Pavlov,Beate Koksch,Cecilia Clementi,Roland R. Netz*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究基于Mori-Zwanzig形式体系推导了非平衡态的多维广义朗之万方程（GLE），特别关注了耦合粗粒化反应坐标在生物复杂系统中的动力学建模，并以人胰岛淀粉样多肽（IAPP）纤维形成过程中的蛋白质折叠为例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立系统性的非马尔可夫框架，用于建模生物复杂系统中耦合粗粒化反应坐标的动力学。特别关注人胰岛淀粉样多肽（IAPP）纤维形成过程中蛋白质内和蛋白质间的耦合折叠过程。

Method: 采用Mori-Zwanzig形式体系，结合时间依赖的多体哈密顿量和多维Mori投影算子，推导了多维可观测量$\vec{A}$的非平衡态Mori广义朗之万方程（GLE）。在三个极限情况下研究了GLE的结构：$\vec{A}$分量不相关、哈密顿量时间独立（平衡态）、以及两个条件同时满足的情况。

Result: 推导出的GLE包含马尔可夫力、非马尔可夫摩擦力的时间积分以及正交力（通常解释为随机力）。研究发现马尔可夫力中存在瞬时摩擦力的贡献，该贡献仅在$\vec{A}$分量不相关时消失。非马尔可夫框架为生物复杂系统中耦合粗粒化反应坐标的系统建模提供了重要基础。

Conclusion: 该非马尔可夫框架是系统建模生物复杂系统中耦合粗粒化反应坐标动力学的重要进展，特别适用于人胰岛淀粉样多肽（IAPP）纤维形成过程中的蛋白质折叠研究，为理解此类复杂生物过程提供了理论工具。

Abstract: The Mori-Zwanzig formalism is a powerful theoretical framework for deriving equations of motion for coarse-grained observables in the form of generalized Langevin equations (GLEs) involving evolution and projection operators. Using a time-dependent many-body Hamiltonian and a multi-dimensional Mori projection operator, we derive a non-equilibrium Mori GLE for a multi-dimensional observable of interest $\vec{A}$ that consists of a Markovian force, a running integral over time of a non-Markovian friction force, and an orthogonal force that is often interpreted as a random force. We study the structure of the derived GLE in three limiting cases: when the components of $\vec{A}$ are uncorrelated, when the Hamiltonian is time-independent and thus the system is at equilibrium, and when both conditions are simultaneously satisfied. We highlight the presence of a contribution to the Markovian force that takes the form of an instantaneous friction force which only vanishes when the components of $\vec{A}$ are uncorrelated. Our non-Markovian framework is an important step towards the systematic modeling of the coupled kinetics of coarse-grained reaction coordinates in biological complex systems, exemplified for the coupled intra- and inter-protein folding during fibril formation of the human islet amyloid polypeptide (IAPP).

### [82] [A new Uncertainty Principle in Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06634)
*V. Dolotin,A. Morozov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了机器学习中多项式搜索问题的本质：海维赛德（Heaviside）和S型（sigmoid）展开的致命退化性导致梯度下降陷入峡谷底部，这可通过一种特殊的"不确定性原理"（uncertainty principle）解释，该原理将傅里叶分析中的概念扩展到S型函数领域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多科学问题在机器学习背景下可简化为寻找适当变量的多项式解。阻碍使用海维赛德（Heaviside）和S型（sigmoid）函数这一简单想法的关键障碍是其展开的致命退化性，导致梯度下降（steepest-descent）演化被困在峡谷底部。

Method: 论文通过分析海维赛德（Heaviside）和S型（sigmoid）展开的数学特性，揭示了这些函数在机器学习应用中的内在限制。该方法将问题表述为一种特殊的不确定性原理（uncertainty principle），类似于傅里叶展开中的相应性质。

Result: 研究发现海维赛德和S型展开的退化问题是不可避免的，可表述为一种特殊的不确定性原理：最小值越尖锐，峡谷就越平滑。这解释了为什么标准机器学习软件需要通过随机分布起始点进行经验性测试来应对此问题。

Conclusion: 机器学习应用于科学时遇到的问题本质上是物理问题而非计算机科学问题。这些现象为已知物理原理提供了新视角，将不确定性原理从傅里叶和小波（wavelet）分析扩展到新的近奇异S型函数类别。

Abstract: Many scientific problems in the context of machine learning can be reduced to the search of polynomial answers in appropriate variables. The Hevisidization of arbitrary polynomial is actually provided by one-and-the same two-layer expression. What prevents the use of this simple idea is the fatal degeneracy of the Heaviside and sigmoid expansions, which traps the steepest-descent evolution at the bottom of canyons, close to the starting point, but far from the desired true minimum. This problem is unavoidable and can be formulated as a peculiar uncertainty principle -- the sharper the minimum, the smoother the canyons. It is a direct analogue of the usual one, which is the pertinent property of the more familiar Fourier expansion. Standard machine learning software fights with this problem empirically, for example, by testing evolutions, originated at randomly distributed starting points and then selecting the best one. Surprisingly or not, phenomena and problems, encountered in ML application to science are pure scientific and belong to physics, not to computer science. On the other hand, they sound slightly different and shed new light on the well-known phenomena -- for example, extend the uncertainty principle from Fourier and, later, wavelet analysis to a new peculiar class of nearly singular sigmoid functions.

</details>


### [83] [Physics-informed neural operator for predictive parametric phase-field modelling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09693)
*Nanxi Chen,Airong Chen,Rujin Ma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种物理信息神经算子框架PF-PINO，用于学习参数化相场偏微分方程，通过嵌入物理约束显著提升了传统傅里叶神经算子在相场模拟中的精度、泛化能力和长期稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相场建模（phase-field modelling）预测材料微观结构和形态演化计算成本高昂，特别是在高通量参数研究中。虽然傅里叶神经算子（Fourier neural operator, FNO）等神经算子有望加速参数化偏微分方程求解，但缺乏显式物理约束可能限制其在复杂相场动力学中的泛化能力和长期精度。

Method: 开发了物理信息神经算子框架PF-PINO，通过将相场控制方程的残差嵌入数据保真度损失函数，在训练过程中有效实施物理约束。该方法针对参数化相场偏微分方程进行学习。

Result: 在电化学腐蚀（electrochemical corrosion）、枝晶凝固（dendritic crystal solidification）和旋节分解（spinodal decomposition）等基准相场问题上验证了PF-PINO。结果表明，PF-PINO在精度、泛化能力和长期稳定性方面显著优于传统FNO。

Conclusion: 该工作为相场建模提供了稳健高效的计算工具，并突显了物理信息神经算子在推进复杂界面演化问题的科学机器学习方面的潜力。

Abstract: Predicting the microstructural and morphological evolution of materials through phase-field modelling is computationally intensive, particularly for high-throughput parametric studies. While neural operators such as the Fourier neural operator (FNO) show promise in accelerating the solution of parametric partial differential equations (PDEs), the lack of explicit physical constraints, may limit generalisation and long-term accuracy for complex phase-field dynamics. Here, we develop a physics-informed neural operator framework to learn parametric phase-field PDEs, namely PF-PINO. By embedding the residuals of phase-field governing equations into the data-fidelity loss function, our framework effectively enforces physical constraints during training. We validate PF-PINO against benchmark phase-field problems, including electrochemical corrosion, dendritic crystal solidification, and spinodal decomposition. Our results demonstrate that PF-PINO significantly outperforms conventional FNO in accuracy, generalisation capability, and long-term stability. This work provides a robust and efficient computational tool for phase-field modelling and highlights the potential of physics-informed neural operators to advance scientific machine learning for complex interfacial evolution problems.

### [84] [A Dynamical Approach to Non-Extensive Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08896)
*Artur O. Lopes,Paulo Varandas*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文为非扩展热力学形式体系（non-extensive thermodynamic formalism）建立理论框架，针对有限字母表上的单边移位（one-sided shift），推广了经典热力学形式体系。该框架基于Tsallis熵（Tsallis entropy）推广，引入q-熵（q-entropy）、q-压（q-pressure）和q-转移算子（q-transfer operators）等概念，并证明了相关的变分原理（variational principles）和平衡态（equilibrium states）的存在唯一性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法包括引入q-熵、q-压和q-转移算子等新概念，并建立它们与经典热力学量之间的关系。核心证明包括Bowen型关系（Bowen-type relation）连接q-压与(2-q)-Ruelle转移算子（Ruelle transfer operator），以及研究Lipschitz势（Lipschitz potentials）下q-平衡态的存在唯一性。

Result: 主要结果包括：证明了q-压与(2-q)-Ruelle转移算子之间的Bowen型关系；建立了Lipschitz势下q-平衡态的存在唯一性；证明了q-压的可微性（differentiability）；获得了q-压及相关渐近压的变分原理；研究了(2-q)-转移算子的上同调方程（cohomological equations）及其解对势的可微依赖性。

Conclusion: 结论表明，本文成功建立了非扩展热力学形式体系的完整数学框架，将Tsallis熵推广应用于符号动力系统。该框架不仅扩展了经典理论，还提供了构造经典Ruelle算子本征函数（eigenfunctions）的替代方法，为研究非扩展统计系统提供了有力工具。

Abstract: We develop a non-extensive thermodynamic formalism for the one-sided shift on a finite alphabet, inspired by Tsallis' generalization of Boltzmann entropy in statistical physics. We introduce notions of $q$-entropy, $q$-pressure, and $q$-transfer operators which extend the classical thermodynamic formalism when $q=1$. We prove a Bowen-type relation linking the $q$-pressure with a $(2-q)$-Ruelle transfer operator and show that $q$-equilibrium states correspond to classical equilibrium states for a related potential. We establish the existence and uniqueness of $q$-equilibrium states for Lipschitz potentials, prove the differentiability of the $q$-pressure, and obtain variational principles for both the $q$-pressure and a related asymptotic pressure. Finally, we study cohomological equations associated with $(2-q)$-transfer operators and prove the differentiable dependence of their solutions on the potential, yielding an alternative construction of eigenfunctions for classical Ruelle operators.

Abstract: This work presents the design and performance characterization of the optical calibration systems produced for the Pacific Ocean Neutrino Experiment (P-ONE). These include novel light-pulse driver circuitry based on gallium nitride field-effect transistor technology and its application to directional and isotropic, self-monitoring optical calibration instruments. A total of 330 directional light pulsers and two isotropic, 17-inch calibration modules (P-CALs) were produced for the first P-ONE line. We present the designs and performance of both the directional and isotropic calibration devices and perform detailed optical characterizations of both full-production batches. In a wavelength range of $365-520\,$nm, our developed driver circuits achieve emission intensities up to $10^{11}\,$photons and pulse widths as small as $1.4\,$ns, respectively. Light-pulse drivers and self-monitoring electronics in the P-CAL were characterized using the same experimental setup, and the instrument's optical-isotropy design was optimized in combination with a dedicated GEANT4-based simulation framework. The optimized P-CAL achieves a simulated isotropy grade of $1.00 \pm 0.01$ across the entire $4 π$ solid angle range. These simulation investigations were explicitly confirmed by dedicated measurements in both air and water using two independent experimental setups, and we report the results. With this, a detailed performance estimate for deployed P-CAL modules in P-ONE was possible.

</details>

# cond-mat.soft [[Back]](#toc)

### [86] [When velocity autocorrelations mirror force autocorrelations: Exact noise-cancellation in interacting Brownian systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08918)
*Anton Lüders,Suvendu Mandal,Thomas Franosch*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究为噪声消除（NC）算法提供了严格的理论基础，证明了在布朗平衡系统中交叉关联项为零，使NC算法成为精确方法；而在非平衡系统中，交叉关联项非零，可作为区分平衡与非平衡状态的判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在软物质系统模拟中，特别是在低密度条件下，解析相互作用布朗粒子的均方位移（MSD）和速度自相关函数（VACF）面临挑战，因为粒子间相互作用稀疏且信号被热噪声主导。噪声消除（NC）算法通过分解粒子轨迹来增强信号清晰度，但其忽略交叉关联项的假设缺乏严格理论依据。

Method: 本研究建立了布朗系统中速度自相关函数（VACF）、表征相互作用贡献的力自相关函数（FACF）以及交叉关联项之间的精确理论关系。通过理论分析，证明了在热平衡条件下交叉关联项为零的数学基础。

Result: 研究结果表明，在热平衡布朗系统中，速度自相关函数（VACF）严格正比于负的力自相关函数（FACF），导致交叉关联项为零，从而确立了噪声消除（NC）算法作为精确方法的理论地位。相反，在布朗非平衡系统中，交叉关联项保持有限值，为区分平衡与非平衡状态提供了直接判据。

Conclusion: 该工作将噪声消除（NC）算法的适用范围扩展到广泛的平衡与非平衡软物质系统，为未来研究中通过模拟获得的速度自相关函数（VACF）数据提供了显著增强分辨率的潜力。对于非平衡系统，需要应用适当的修正来保持NC方法的准确性。

Abstract: Resolving the mean-squared displacement (MSD) and velocity autocorrelation function (VACF) of interacting Brownian particles remains a central challenge in simulations of soft-matter systems, especially at low densities where particle-particle interactions are sparse and signals are dominated by thermal noise. A recently proposed noise-cancellation (NC) algorithm [Mandal et al. Phys. Rev. Lett. 123, 168001 (2019)] addresses this by decomposing particle trajectories into two components: free Brownian motion and interaction-induced displacements. The NC approximation enhances signal clarity by neglecting cross-correlations between the total particle displacements and the extracted interaction-induced contributions of the trajectories - an assumption that has so far lacked rigorous theoretical justification. In this work, we establish an exact theoretical relation between the VACF, the force autocorrelation function (FACF) characterizing the interaction-induced contributions, and these cross-correlations, which is valid for Brownian systems. We show that in thermal equilibrium, the cross-correlations vanish for Brownian systems because the VACF is strictly proportional to the negative FACF, which establishes the NC algorithm as an exact method. In contrast, for Brownian nonequilibrium systems, the cross-correlations remain finite, providing a direct fingerprint of nonequilibrium physics in such systems and a criterion to distinguish equilibrium from nonequilibrium states. Here, suitable corrections must be applied for the NC method to remain accurate. Our results expand the scope of the NC algorithm to a broad range of soft-matter systems in and out of equilibrium, where it has the potential to strongly enhance the resolution of VACF data obtained through simulations in future studies.

</details>


### [87] [Dynamics of viscous liquids and the Random Barrier Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09027)
*Thomas B. Schrøder,Jeppe C. Dyre,Camille Scalliet*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究结合粒子交换蒙特卡洛算法与GPU分子动力学模拟，分析三元Lennard-Jones玻璃形成液体在极高粘度区域的动力学行为，发现随机势垒模型比von Schweidler定律能更好地拟合固有均方位移数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在分析三元Lennard-Jones玻璃形成液体在极高粘度区域的动力学特性，特别关注通过淬火构型到其固有状态获得的固有动力学行为。

Method: 结合粒子交换蒙特卡洛算法（particle-swap Monte Carlo algorithm）与GPU分子动力学模拟，通过淬火构型空间轨迹中的构型到其固有状态获得固有动力学数据。

Result: 随机势垒模型（random barrier model, RBM）在极端无序极限下，尽管没有无量纲自由参数，但比具有一个无量纲自由参数的von Schweidler定律能更好地拟合固有均方位移数据，并能更准确地从短时模拟数据预测扩散系数值。

Conclusion: 随机势垒模型能很好地再现固有动力学数据，尽管该模型假设所有能量极小值相同（这一假设并不现实），这仍是一个未解之谜。

Abstract: This paper combines the particle-swap Monte Carlo algorithm with long GPU molecular dynamics simulations to analyze the dynamics of a ternary Lennard-Jones glass-forming liquid in the extremely viscous regime. The focus is on the inherent dynamics, obtained by quenching configurations along the configuration-space trajectory into their inherent state. We compare how two functional forms, the von Schweidler law and the random barrier model (RBM) prediction in the extreme disorder limit, fit data for the inherent mean-squared displacement as a function of time. We find that the RBM, which has no dimensionless free parameters, generally fits the data better than the von Schweidler law, despite the latters one dimensionless free parameter. In particular, this implies that the RBM predicts the value of the diffusion coefficient from short-time simulation data more accurately than does the von Schweidler expression. It remains an open question why the RBM reproduces well the inherent data despite this models (unrealistic) assumption of identical energy minima.

</details>


### [88] [Effect of Cylindrical Confinement on the Collapse Dynamics of a Polymer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09376)
*Shubham Thwal,Suman Majumder*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过分子动力学模拟探索了圆柱形约束（cylindrical confinement）对均聚物（homopolymer）在溶剂条件从良溶剂（good solvent）突变为不良溶剂（poor solvent）时塌缩动力学的影响。研究发现塌缩过程分为两个阶段：珍珠项链（pearl-necklace）形成阶段和香肠状（sausage-like）中间体向球形球状体（spherical globule）转变阶段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚合物（polymer）在受限条件下的结构和动力学行为会因几何限制而发生显著改变。本研究旨在探索圆柱形约束如何影响均聚物在溶剂条件突变时的塌缩动力学，这对于理解纳米通道（nanochannels）中聚合物的行为具有重要意义。

Method: 采用分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）方法，研究不同圆柱半径（cylinder radius）R下均聚物的塌缩过程。通过分析单个珍珠（pearls）或团簇（clusters）的形状参数（shape parameter）来区分塌缩的两个阶段，并提取相应的弛豫时间（relaxation times）。

Result: 研究发现塌缩过程分为两个阶段：珍珠项链弛豫时间τp与R无关，而香肠弛豫时间τs在特定R值以下呈反比关系，超过该值后趋于饱和。从τp和τs的温度依赖性阿伦尼乌斯图（Arrhenius plots）中提取的活化能（activation energies）显示，珍珠项链阶段的Ea与R无关，而香肠弛豫阶段在强约束条件下的Ea显著高于弱约束条件。平均团簇尺寸的增长在固定温度下遵循普适幂律（universal power law），与R无关。

Conclusion: 圆柱约束显著影响聚合物塌缩动力学，塌缩过程呈现两个不同的阶段。研究提出了在圆柱纳米通道内实现聚合物塌缩实验的可行方案，为理解受限环境中聚合物的动力学行为提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Structure and dynamics of a polymer under confinement gets significantly altered due to the imposed geometric restrictions. Using molecular dynamics simulations, here, we explore the effect of cylindrical confinement on the kinetics of collapse of a homopolymer, when the solvent condition is abruptly changed from good to poor. The observed phenomenology for a range of the cylinder radius $R$, reveals two distinct stages of the collapse. The first stage is highlighted by the formation and growth of local connected clusters resembling a pearl necklace, eventually ending with a single sausage-like cluster. In the second stage, the sausage-like intermediate approaches a spherical globule via surface-energy minimization. These two stages are disentangled using a shape parameter of the individual pearls or clusters, allowing us to also extract the respective relaxation times, and thereby their scaling behaviors with respect to the length of the polymer. We find that the pearl-necklace relaxation time $τ_p$ is independent of $R$. On the other hand, the sausage-relaxation time $τ_s$ varies inversely up to a certain $R$, beyond which it also saturates. From the Arrhenius plots of the temperature dependence of $τ_p$ and $τ_s$, we extract the activation energies $E_{\rm a}$ of the two stages. While the estimated $E_{\rm a}$ for the pearl-necklace stage is independent of $R$, for the sausage relaxation it is significantly higher in the strongly confined case than in the weakly one. Surprisingly, at a fixed temperature, the growth of the average cluster size obeys a universal power law irrespective of $R$. However, for a fixed $R$, the behavior is rather non-universal with respect to temperature. We propose viable scenarios for experimental realization of polymer collapse inside cylindrical nanochannels.

</details>


### [89] [Impact of magnetic fields on polaron dynamics in low-dimensional systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09498)
*Larissa Brizhik,B. M. A. G. Piette*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值方法分析了外磁场对具有电子-晶格相互作用的准一维材料中极化子（polaron）长程输运的影响，揭示了磁场效应不仅取决于场强，还与决定孤子特性的系统参数密切相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解外磁场对多肽、（半）导电聚合物和大分子等准一维材料中长程电子输运的影响，特别关注电子-晶格相互作用下形成的极化子（polaron）动力学行为。

Method: 采用离散非线性方程的数值求解方法，而非连续近似（continuum approximation），研究磁场对极化子动力学的影响，并分析了施主复合物（donor complex）在链上产生的极化子受磁场作用的情况。

Result: 研究发现磁场对极化子动力学的影响不仅取决于磁场强度，还由决定孤子（soliton）特性的系统参数（如能量、振幅和局域化宽度）共同决定，这些参数显著影响极化子对外磁场的响应行为。

Conclusion: 外磁场对极化子输运的影响具有参数依赖性，系统特性参数与磁场强度共同决定了准一维材料中极化子动力学的复杂行为，这为理解磁场调控下的电子输运提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We study the impact of an external magnetic field on the long-range electron transport in quasi-one-dimensional materials, such as polypeptides, (semi-) conducting polymers and macromolecules, taking into account the electron-lattice interaction. At relatively strong electron-lattice interaction extra electrons get self-trapped in the deformation potential well and form stable bound states, called large polarons which in the continuum approximation are known as solitons. Here we do not use the continuum approximation but solve the system of discrete nonlinear equations numerically. We show that the impact of a magnetic field on polaron dynamics depends not only on the field strength, but also on the parameter values of the system which define the properties of solitons such as their energy, amplitude and width of localisation. We also study the impact of a magnetic field on a polaron created by a donor complex on a chain.

### [90] [Tunable shear thickening in active non-Brownian suspensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09620)
*Bhanu Prasad Bhowmik,Christopher Ness*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过颗粒模拟发现，活性自驱动颗粒悬浮液中的粒子自推进（self-propulsion）可在高应力下引发粘度降低的"去增稠（dethickening）"效应，超越传统摩擦介导的剪切增稠（shear thickening）范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索活性（active）非布朗（non-Brownian）、排斥性、摩擦性颗粒悬浮液中的可调剪切增稠行为，特别是活性如何改变传统摩擦介导的剪切增稠机制。

Method: 采用基于颗粒的模拟（particle-based simulation）方法，研究自推进（self-propulsion）颗粒悬浮液，并通过定义无量纲活性应力（dimensionless active stress）来量化活性与流动驱动摩擦接触形成之间的竞争关系。

Result: 增加粒子自推进会在高应力下驱动系统的"去增稠"效应，降低粘度；去增稠程度可通过调节无量纲活性应力进行调控；数据符合近期提出的标度框架（scaling framework），支持对稠密悬浮液可调流变学的普适描述。

Conclusion: 活性自推进通过引入各向同性动力学与流动驱动摩擦接触竞争，实现可调的剪切增稠行为；该发现与其它去增稠途径具有相似性，支持对稠密悬浮液可调流变学的统一描述框架。

Abstract: We study tunable shear thickening in active suspensions of non-Brownian, repulsive, frictional grains using particle-based simulation, finding that activity augments the rheology beyond the friction-mediated shear thickening paradigm. Specifically, increasing particle self-propulsion drives a viscosity-reducing `dethickening' of the system at large stress, where the material would otherwise be in a thickened, highly viscous state. Self-propulsion introduces additional isotropic dynamics to the particles, which compete with the flow-driven formation of frictional contacts. The degree of dethickening can thus be tuned by varying a suitably-defined dimensionless active stress that quantifies this competition. Recognising the parallels between self-propulsion and other contemporary routes to dethickening, we demonstrate that our data obey a recently proposed scaling framework, supporting a universal description of the tunable rheology of dense suspensions.

</details>


### [91] [Three-stage melting of a macroscopic continuous spacetime crystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09649)
*Guoqing Liu,Jimin Bai,Matteo Baggioli,Jie Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究首次实验观测了经典连续时空晶体（spacetime crystal）的熔化过程，使用宏观活性颗粒圆盘在2+1维时空中实现了这一现象，揭示了时空对称性破缺的解耦机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时空晶体（spacetime crystal）已在微观量子多体系统和介观向列相液晶中被实验观测到，但其熔化过程及物理机制尚未有实验报道。本研究旨在填补这一空白，探索时空晶体熔化的物理机制。

Method: 研究采用桌面实验方法，使用宏观活性颗粒圆盘（active granular disks）在2+1维时空中构建系统。通过调节圆盘堆积分数（packing fraction），观测时空晶体的熔化过程。

Result: 实验观测到时空晶体表现出相干刚体旋转的二维三角晶格，持续近一天且对噪声具有鲁棒性。熔化过程包含三个阶段，涉及空间六角相（hexatic phase）和多个共存区域。研究发现空间和时间晶序通过不同机制熔化：空间序被拓扑缺陷增殖破坏，而时间序因多体相互作用减弱导致方向持续性衰减而丧失。

Conclusion: 结果表明空间和时间平移对称性的自发破缺可以解耦，导致奇异非平衡经典物相的出现。这为理解时空晶体熔化机制提供了实验依据，并展示了宏观系统中时空有序性的复杂行为。

Abstract: A spacetime crystal is a phase of matter that spontaneously develops periodic order in both space and time. Spacetime crystals have been experimentally observed in microscopic quantum many-body systems and, very recently, in a mesoscopic nematic liquid crystal. However, the melting process of a spacetime crystal and its underlying physical mechanisms have not yet been experimentally reported. Here, we present a direct observation of a classical continuous spacetime crystal melting in a table-top experiment with macroscopic active granular disks in 2+1 spacetime dimensions. The spacetime crystal is characterized by the spontaneous formation of a coherent, rigid-body rotation of a 2D triangular lattice that persists for almost a day and remains remarkably robust to noise. By tuning the disk packing fraction, we observe a complex three-stage melting process involving a spatially hexatic phase and multiple coexistence regions. Importantly, we show that spatial and temporal crystalline orders melt separately through distinct mechanisms: spatial order is destroyed by the proliferation of topological defects, while temporal order is lost through the decay of directional persistence caused by the progressive weakening of many-body interactions. Our results demonstrate that the spontaneous breaking of spatial and temporal translational symmetries can be decoupled, leading to the emergence of exotic out-of-equilibrium classical phases of matter.

</details>


### [92] [Capillary filling of star polymer melts in nanopores](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09788)
*Jianwei Zhang,Jinyu Lei,Pu Feng,George Floudas,Guangzhao Zhang,Jiajia Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过粗粒化分子动力学模拟，探究星形聚合物拓扑结构对熔体毛细填充动力学的影响，发现臂长、官能度（functionality）和受限程度显著改变浸润行为、构象弛豫及吸附摩擦效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚合物拓扑结构（topology）深刻影响其行为，但其对浸润动力学（imbibition dynamics）的作用尚不明确。本研究旨在探究星形聚合物（star polymer）熔体在毛细填充过程中的动力学行为。

Method: 采用粗粒化模型（coarse-grained model）进行分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations），研究星形聚合物熔体的毛细填充过程（包括浸润期间及完全浸润后）。

Result: 星形聚合物也表现出线性链体系观察到的浸润动力学反转。短臂星形聚合物渗透慢于Lucas-Washburn方程预测，而长臂体系则更快。回转半径（radius of gyration）在受限流动中增加，表明臂的取向和解缠结。官能度越高，保留的缠结点越多，且靠近核心链段的刚性区域越大。臂的构型比例（如环、链轨、尾）随臂长和受限程度剧烈变化，但仅在臂短时受官能度影响。完全浸润后，核心-末端矢量自相关函数（self-correlation function）的不同衰减速率表明，随着官能度、臂长和受限程度增加，臂达到平衡态所需时间更长。

Conclusion: 星形拓扑结构诱导了更强的吸附和摩擦效应，且该效应随官能度增加而更加显著。研究结果与近期实验发现一致，揭示了拓扑结构对聚合物浸润动力学的复杂影响机制。

Abstract: Topology of polymer profoundly influences on its behavior. However, its effect on imbibition dynamics remains poorly understood. In the present work, capillary filling (during imbibition and following full imbibition) of star polymer melts was investigated by molecular dynamics simulations with a coarse-grained model. The reversal of imbibition dynamics observed for linear-chain systems was also present for star polymers. Star polymers with short arms penetrate slower than the prediction of the Lucas-Washburn equation, while systems with long arms penetrate faster. The radius of gyration increases during confined flow, indicating the orientation and disentanglement of arms. In addition, the higher the functionality of the star polymer, the more entanglement points are retained. Besides, a stiff region near the core segments of the stars is observed, which increases in size with functionality. The proportion of different configurations of the arms (e.g. loops, trains, tails) changes dramatically with the arm length and degree of confinement, but is only influenced by the functionality when the arms are short. Following full imbibition, the different decay rates of the self-correlation function of the core-to-end vector illustrate that arms take a longer time to reach the equilibrium state as the functionality, arm length, and degree of confinement increases, in agreement with recent experimental findings. Furthermore, the star topology induces a stronger effect of adsorption and friction, which becomes more pronounced with increasing functionality.

</details>


### [93] [Three phases of odd robotic active matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09897)
*Fan Bo,Shiqi Liu,Zenghong He,Wyatt Joyce,Gregor Leech,Kiet Tran,Keilan Ramirez,Nicholas Boechler,Nicholas Gravish,Hongbo Zhao,Tzer Han Tan*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过可调谐机器人活性物质平台MASBot，首次实验实现了从奇弹性晶体到奇粘性液体再到手性活性气体的相变，建立了非互易活性物质的统一相图，为研究非平衡物理提供了基础实验平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非互易相互作用（nonreciprocal interactions）在活性物质中会产生奇弹性（odd elasticity）和奇粘度（odd viscosity）等奇异力学行为，但这些现象通常被孤立研究。本文旨在探索是否存在一个单一系统能够体现这些不同的奇物质（odd matter）相态，并能在相态间转变，从而建立非互易活性物质的统一相图。

Method: 研究引入了可调谐机器人活性物质平台——磁机械增强旋转机器人集体（Magnetomechanically Augmented Spinning roBotic collective, MASBot）。该系统通过对粒子层面的手性（chirality）、活性和成对相互作用的控制，能够访问奇物质的不同相态。通过连续增加排斥力相对于吸引力和横向力的比例，实验绘制了从奇弹性晶体到奇粘性液体再到手性活性气体的相变。

Result: 实验成功绘制了从奇弹性晶体到奇粘性液体再到手性活性气体的相变图。研究发现手性活性气体相形成了一种非空间填充、非互易的活性气体，由长程流体动力学吸引力稳定，其统计特征与二维自引力点涡气体（two-dimensional self-gravitating point vortex gas）一致。通过调整旋转频率和引入空间图案化活性，可以在这些相态内微调奇力学响应并定制功率谱。进一步的极性和旋转对称性破缺导致了相分离和集体平移等新颖涌现态。

Conclusion: MASBot系统为非平衡物理（nonequilibrium physics）提供了基础实验测试平台，并为将机器人群体视为可编程物质态（programmable states of matter）建立了蓝图。该系统能够实现从弹性结构到自适应群体重构等多种功能，为研究非互易活性物质的统一相图提供了实验基础。

Abstract: Nonreciprocal interactions in active matter are known to generate exotic mechanical behaviors such as odd elasticity and odd viscosity. However, these phenomena have largely been studied in isolation, raising a fundamental question: Is there a single system that embodies these distinct regimes of odd matter and can transition between phases, establishing a unified phase diagram for nonreciprocal active matter? To address this, we introduce a tunable robotic active matter platform, the Magnetomechanically Augmented Spinning roBotic (MASBot) collective, in which particle-level control of chirality, activity, and pairwise interactions enables access to distinct phases of odd matter. By continuously increasing repulsive forces relative to attractive and transverse forces, we experimentally map a transition from an odd elastic crystal to an odd viscous liquid, and then to a chiral active gas. We find that this latter phase forms a non-space-filling, nonreciprocal active gas stabilized by long-range hydrodynamic attractive forces, whose statistical signatures are consistent with those of a two-dimensional self-gravitating point vortex gas. Within these phases, adjusting spinning frequency and introducing spatially patterned activity allows us to fine-tune odd mechanical responses and tailor power spectra. Further polar and rotational symmetry breaking at the particle scale leads to novel emergent states such as phase separation and collective translation. Together, our system provides a fundamental experimental testbed for nonequilibrium physics and establishes a blueprint for treating robotic swarms as programmable states of matter, enabling functions that range from resilient structures to adaptive swarm reconfiguration.

</details>


### [94] [Synthetic design of force-responsive hydrogels with ring-forming catch bonds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09911)
*Wout Laeremans,Wouter G. Ellenbroek*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于可逆成环聚合物（reversible ring-forming polymers）的动态水凝胶最小合成框架，通过粗粒化分子动力学模拟（coarse-grained molecular dynamics simulations）展示了其独特的"捕获键（catch bond）"行为——在机械载荷增加时键寿命反而延长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 捕获键（catch bonds）是一种在机械载荷下寿命反而增加的相互作用，这种反直觉行为在多种生物过程中发挥重要作用。将这种机制应用于合成材料，有望开发出在低应力下柔顺、在受力时硬化的系统，具有从冲击响应材料到动态组织支架的广泛应用潜力。

Method: 本研究提出了基于可逆成环聚合物（reversible ring-forming polymers）的动态水凝胶最小合成框架。通过粗粒化分子动力学模拟（coarse-grained molecular dynamics simulations）来研究这种化学结构的水凝胶行为。

Result: 模拟结果显示，具有这种化学结构的水凝胶在应力增加时发生更少的断键反应，甚至表现出应变率（strain rate）对施加应力的非单调依赖性。这证实了可逆成环机制能够实现类似生物系统中捕获键的力学行为。

Conclusion: 研究结果强调了可逆成环（reversible ring formation）作为设计具有可调耐久性和响应性的力学自适应材料（mechanically adaptive materials）的多功能平台的潜力，为合成材料中实现可调谐、力依赖性相互作用提供了新途径。

Abstract: Catch bonds are interactions whose lifetimes increase under mechanical load, a counterintuitive behaviour that underlies diverse biological processes. Translating this mechanism to synthetic materials offers the potential to create systems that are compliant at low stress but stiffen under applied force, with applications ranging from impact-responsive materials to dynamic tissue scaffolds. However, engineering materials with tunable, force-dependent interactions remains challenging, and existing conceptual designs are limited. Here, we present a minimal synthetic framework for catch bond behaviour in dynamic hydrogels, based on reversible ring-forming polymers. Using coarse-grained molecular dynamics simulations, we show that hydrogels with such a chemistry undergo fewer bond-breaking reactions as the stress increases and can even display a non-monotonic dependence of the strain rate on the applied stress. Our results highlight the potential of reversible ring formation as a versatile platform for designing mechanically adaptive materials with tunable durability and responsiveness.

### [95] [Study of quark and gluon jet identification in photoproduction at EIC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09545)
*Siddharth Narayan Singh,Ritu Aggarwal,Manjit Kaur*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究利用PYTHIA模拟电子-离子对撞机（EIC）中光生（photoproduction）事件产生的喷注（jet），通过喷注形状变量（jet-shape variables）分析夸克和胶子引发喷注的亚结构差异，为区分两者提供基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索电子-离子对撞机（Electron-Ion Collider, EIC）中光生事件产生的喷注亚结构，为区分夸克引发和胶子引发的喷注提供理论基础，支持进一步的量子色动力学（QCD）研究。

Method: 使用PYTHIA生成质心能量（center-of-mass energies）为30-140 GeV的光生事件，分析直接和解析光生（direct and resolved photoproduction）子过程。在FastJet框架内采用纵向不变的$k_T$算法（longitudinally invariant $k_T$ algorithm）重建喷注，并利用喷注形状变量研究选定双喷注样本的亚结构。

Result: 研究提供了胶子引发和夸克引发喷注的子喷注多重数（subjet multiplicities）和积分喷注形状（integrated jet shapes）的预测。结果表明在EIC的光生事件中区分夸克和胶子喷注是可行的。

Conclusion: 该研究证实了在电子-离子对撞机的光生事件中区分夸克和胶子喷注的可行性，为后续量子色动力学研究提供了重要基准（baseline）。

Abstract: We investigate the substructure of jets produced in photoproduction events with center-of-mass energies $\sqrt{s} = 30\text{--}140$ GeV at the proposed Electron-Ion Collider (EIC). Events are generated using PYTHIA and contributions from direct and resolved photoproduction subprocesses are analyzed at different center-of-mass energies. Jets are reconstructed using longitudinally invariant $k_T$ algorithm within the FastJet framework. Substructure of quark- and gluon-initiated jets in the selected di-jet photoproduction sample is studied in detail by using jet-shape variables. Predictions for subjet multiplicities and integrated jet shapes are presented in the gluon-initiated and quark-initiated jets. These results demonstrate the feasibility of distinguishing quark and gluon jets in the photo-production events at the EIC and provide a baseline for further QCD studies.

### [96] [Network modelling of yield-stress fluid flow in randomly disordered porous media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09801)
*Cláudio P. Fonte,Elliott Sutton,Kohei Ohie,Eleanor Doman,Yuji Tasaka,Anne Juel*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一个用于赫歇尔-巴尔克利（Herschel-Bulkley）流体在二维无序多孔介质中流动的孔隙网络模型，包含可选壁面滑移。模型基于收敛-发散喉道的物理压力-流动关系，无需拟合阻力参数即可直接捕捉屈服和屈服后输运行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 屈服应力流体在多孔介质中的流动受到流变学和孔隙尺度几何结构的强耦合影响，导致非线性、非达西输运以及在屈服点附近出现显著的通道化现象。现有模型需要进一步改进以更准确地描述这些复杂行为。

Method: 开发了一个二维无序多孔介质中的孔隙网络模型，用于模拟赫歇尔-巴尔克利流体流动，包含可选壁面滑移条件。模型基于收敛-发散喉道的物理压力-流动关系构建，无需拟合阻力参数，使屈服和屈服后输运直接从孔隙尺度流体力学中产生。

Result: 与直接数值模拟的基准测试表明，该模型能够准确捕捉整体压降以及流动拓扑从空间分布输运到强烈通道化流动的演化过程。模型还能捕捉壁面滑移的主要效应，该效应降低了输运所需的压力梯度并重新激活了无滑移情况下保持阻塞的流动路径。

Conclusion: 屈服点附近的压力损失由收缩统计而非障碍物尺度长度控制。特别地，使用域平均最小喉道宽度进行重新标度，能够在不同孔隙度下统一塑性主导的响应，从而确定了该区域粘塑性输运中与耗散相关的几何尺度。

Abstract: Yield-stress fluid flow through porous media is governed by a strong coupling between rheology and pore-scale geometry, leading to nonlinear, non-Darcy transport and pronounced channelisation near yielding. We develop a pore-network model for Herschel-Bulkley flow in two-dimensional disordered porous media, including optional wall slip. The network is closed by a physics-based pressure-flow relation for a converging-diverging throat, so that yielding and post-yield transport emerge directly from the pore-scale fluid mechanics without fitted resistance parameters. Benchmarking against direct numerical simulations shows that the model captures both the bulk pressure drop and the evolution of the flow topology from spatially distributed transport to strongly channelised flow. The framework also captures the leading effect of wall slip, which lowers the pressure gradient required for transport and reactivates pathways that remain blocked in the no-slip case. Using the model across different porous geometries, we show that near-yield pressure losses are governed by constriction statistics rather than by an obstacle-scale length. In particular, rescaling with the domain-averaged minimum throat width collapses the plastic-dominated response across porosities, identifying the dissipation-relevant geometric scale for viscoplastic transport in this regime.
