### [98] [Hopfield model for patterns with internal structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09317)
*Theodorus Maria Nieuwenhuizen*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究分析了球形Hopfield模型在静态极限下的模式识别能力，通过高斯随机变量建模模式内部结构，发现系统随温度降低会进入自旋玻璃相，并在低负载容量时出现包含模式和关联的玻璃相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究球形Hopfield模型在静态极限下的模式识别特性，特别关注模式内部结构对系统相行为的影响，通过引入高斯随机变量来建模模式内自旋对之间的关联。

Method: 采用复制法（replica method）解析推导系统的自由能，建立重叠分布（overlap distribution）的自洽方程，分析系统从高温到低温的相变行为。

Result: 从高温开始，系统首先进入自旋玻璃相（spin glass phase），随着温度进一步降低，模式和关联开始出现；在足够小的负载容量下，还会出现包含模式和关联的玻璃相。

Conclusion: 球形Hopfield模型在考虑模式内部结构关联时，展现出丰富的相行为，包括自旋玻璃相和包含模式关联的玻璃相，这些相变特性对理解模式识别系统的统计力学性质具有重要意义。

Abstract: The spherical version of the Hopfield model for pattern recognition is considered in the static limit. Structures inside the patterns are modeled by Gaussian random variables that reward correlation between pairs of spins in a given pattern. The free energy is derived analytically with the replica method. The overlap distribution obeys a self-consistent equation. Coming from high temperatures, a spin glass phase is entered, in which patterns and correlations appear at lower temperatures. For small enough loading capacity, also a glass phase with patterns and correlations appears.

### [99] [Dreaming improves memorization in a Hopfield model with bounded synaptic strength](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09384)
*Enzo Marinari,Saverio Rossi,Francesco Zamponi*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在具有突触强度限制（"clipping"）的Hopfield模型中添加"做梦"（dreaming）阶段如何改善记忆容量。研究发现，虽然clipping消除了灾难性遗忘（catastrophic forgetting），但交替进行学习和做梦阶段能提高记忆容量，并使性能优化更符合进化视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Hopfield模型基于Hebbian学习规则，存在灾难性遗忘问题：当尝试存储过多模式时，网络无法检索任何模式。虽然引入突触强度限制（clipping）消除了灾难性遗忘，但记忆容量显著降低。本研究旨在探索添加"做梦"阶段对clipped Hopfield模型容量的影响。

Method: 研究采用Hopfield、Feinstein和Palmer提出的方法，在模型中添加"做梦"阶段。该阶段生成随机模式并进行"反学习"（unlearning）。研究分析了交替进行学习和做梦阶段对模型性能的影响。

Result: 研究显示，clipping确实消除了灾难性遗忘，使模型能够检索最近看到的记忆而消除较旧的记忆。更重要的是，交替进行学习和做梦阶段显著改善了记忆容量，并使寻找最优性能的过程从进化视角看更加现实。

Conclusion: 在clipped Hopfield模型中引入做梦阶段不仅保持了消除灾难性遗忘的优势，还提高了记忆容量。这种学习与做梦交替的机制为理解记忆系统的进化优化提供了更现实的框架。

Abstract: The Hopfield model provides a paradigmatic framework for associative memory. Its classical implementation, based on the Hebbian learning rule, suffers from catastrophic forgetting: when one attempts storing too many patterns, the network fails to retrieve any of them. Yet, the Hebbian rule does not take into account that synaptic strength is bounded. Introducing this biologically plausible modification, known as "clipping", eliminates catastrophic forgetting; the model is now able to retrieve the most recently seen memories, eliminating older ones. Yet, its memorization capacity is much reduced with respect to the unclipped case. Here, we investigate the effects of adding a "dreaming" phase on the capacity of a clipped Hopfield model. Following a proposal by Hopfield, Feinstein and Palmer, we assume that during the dreaming phase, the model generates random patterns that are then "unlearned". We show that while clipping still removes catastrophic forgetting, alternating learning and dreaming phases improves the memorization capacity and makes the search for optimal performance more realistic from an evolutionary perspective.

</details>

### [100] [Compact Dynamical Mean-Field Theory of Oscillator Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09402)
*Kanishka Reddy*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种紧凑型动力学平均场理论（compact DMFT），用于分析具有相干平均场耦合和淬火随机性的大型耦合相位振子网络。该理论框架能够处理任意2π周期耦合函数，并可直接从单神经元相位响应数据预测网络层面的同步阈值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为大型耦合相位振子网络开发一个统一的平均场理论框架，该框架需要同时处理相干平均场耦合和淬火随机性（quenched randomness），并能够适用于任意2π周期耦合函数，包括从生物物理神经元模型导出的无穷小相位响应曲线（iPRCs）。

Method: 方法基于包裹朗之万动力学（wrapped Langevin dynamics），构建了保持相位2π周期性的路径积分表示。在热力学极限下对无序求平均后，理论简化为由确定性平均场和自洽有色高斯噪声驱动的单振子随机方程，其协方差由圆形双时间关联器确定。

Result: 在无序消失极限下，该形式体系重现了Ott-Antonsen约简，并恢复了标准的Kuramoto和theta-神经元神经质量方程。对于自适应指数积分发放神经元，将iPRC拟合的耦合函数插入紧凑DMFT可定量预测同步阈值，提供了从单神经元相位响应数据到网络层面平均场预测的直接途径。

Conclusion: 该紧凑DMFT为任意相位可约简振子提供了一个通用框架，能够直接从单神经元相位响应数据预测网络层面的集体行为，为分析大型耦合振子网络提供了强有力的理论工具。

Abstract: We present a compact dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT) for large networks of coupled phase oscillators whose phases live on the circle $S^1$ and interact with both coherent mean-field coupling and quenched randomness. Starting from wrapped Langevin dynamics, we build a path-integral representation that keeps the $2π$-periodicity of the phases explicit. After averaging over the disorder in the thermodynamic limit, this construction reduces to a single-oscillator stochastic equation driven by a deterministic mean field and a self-consistent colored Gaussian noise, whose covariance is fixed by a circular two-time correlator. In the limit of vanishing disorder, the formalism reproduces the Ott--Antonsen reduction and recovers standard Kuramoto and theta-neuron neural-mass equations. The same framework accommodates arbitrary $2π$-periodic coupling functions, including those obtained from infinitesimal phase response curves (iPRCs) of biophysical neuron models. As an example, we show that for adaptive exponential integrate-and-fire neurons, inserting an iPRC-fitted coupling into the compact DMFT yields quantitative predictions for synchronization thresholds, providing a direct route from single-neuron phase response data to network-level mean-field predictions for arbitrary phase-reducible oscillators.

</details>

### [101] [Quantum algorithm for anisotropic diffusion and convection equations with vector norm scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08799)
*Julien Zylberman,Thibault Fredon,Nuno F. Loureiro,Fabrice Debbasch*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在数字量子计算机上求解偏微分方程（PDEs）的量子数值方案，针对各向异性扩散方程和对流方程，通过量子态制备、对角算子演化和可观测量测量三个步骤，实现了相比先前算子范数分析的指数级加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在解决在数字量子计算机上求解偏微分方程（PDEs）的问题，特别关注两个基本方程：各向异性扩散方程（anisotropic diffusion equation）和各向异性对流方程（anisotropic convection equation）。

Method: 提出了一种包含三个步骤的量子数值方案：量子态制备（quantum state preparation）、对角算子演化（evolution with diagonal operators）和可观测量测量（measurement of observables）。演化步骤基于高阶中心有限差分（high-order centered finite difference）和乘积公式近似（product formula approximation），也称为Trotter分解（Trotterization）。

Result: 通过新颖的向量范数分析（vector-norm analysis）来界定不同误差来源，证明演化所需的时间步数相比先前算子范数分析可实现指数级减少：扩散方程减少因子为Θ(16^n)，对流方程减少因子为Θ(4^n)，其中n是每维度的量子比特数。

Conclusion: 该研究在数字量子计算机上求解偏微分方程方面取得了显著进展，通过量子数值方案和向量范数分析，实现了相比传统方法的指数级加速，为量子计算在科学计算领域的应用提供了重要方法。

Abstract: In this work, we tackle the resolution of partial differential equations (PDEs) on digital quantum computers. Two fundamental PDEs are addressed: the anisotropic diffusion equation and the anisotropic convection equation. We present a quantum numerical scheme consisting of three steps: quantum state preparation, evolution with diagonal operators, and measurement of observables of interest. The evolution step relies on a high-order centered finite difference and a product formula approximation, also known as Trotterization. We provide novel vector-norm analysis to bound the different sources of error. We prove that the number of time-steps required in the evolution can be reduced by a factor $Θ(16^n)$ for the diffusion equation, and $Θ(4^n)$ for the convection equation, where $n$ is the number of qubits per dimension, an exponential reduction compared to the previously established operator-norm analysis.

</details>


### [102] [The Structure of Circle Graph States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08847)
*Frederik Hahn,Rose McCarty,Hendrik Poulsen Nautrup,Nathan Claudet*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了圆图态（circle graph states）的局域等价性，证明了圆图在r-局域补变换下封闭，建立了二部圆图态与平面码态（planar code states）的一一对应关系，并证明了计算给定图态局域幺正等价图态数量是#P-难问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 圆图态是结构上重要的图态家族，其纠缠特性理论上足以支持基于测量的通用量子计算（MBQC），但实际上基于圆图态的MBQC可被经典计算机高效模拟。本文旨在详细描绘圆图态的局域等价性图景。

Method: 采用图论方法分析圆图态的局域幺正（LU）等价性，研究r-局域补变换下的封闭性；建立二部圆图态与平面码态的一一对应关系；利用这一对应关系提供简洁证明；最后分析计算等价图态数量的计算复杂性。

Result: 证明圆图在r-局域补变换下封闭，即只有圆图态自身与圆图态局域幺正等价；建立了二部圆图态与平面码态的一一对应；提供了平面码态与稳定子态等价性的简洁证明；证明了计算给定图态局域幺正等价图态数量是#P-难问题。

Conclusion: 圆图态在局域幺正变换下具有独特的封闭性，其与平面码态的对应关系解释了为何基于圆图态的MBQC可被经典高效模拟，同时揭示了计算等价图态数量的计算复杂性本质。

Abstract: Circle graph states are a structurally important family of graph states. The family's entanglement is a priori high enough to allow for universal measurement-based quantum computation (MBQC); however, MBQC on circle graph states is actually efficiently classically simulable. In this work, we paint a detailed picture of the local equivalence of circle graph states. First, we consider the class of all graph states that are local unitary (LU)-equivalent to circle graph states. In graph-theoretical terms, this LU-equivalence class is the set of all graphs reachable from the family of circle graphs by applying $r$-local complementations. We prove that the only graph states that are LU-equivalent to circle graph states are circle graph states themselves: circle graphs are closed under $r$-local complementation. Second, we show that bipartite circle graph states, i.e., 2-colorable circle graph states, are in one-to-one correspondence with planar code states, on which MBQC is known to be efficiently classically simulable. Leveraging this correspondence, we present alternative, simple proofs that (1) if a planar code state is LU-equivalent to a stabilizer state, they are in fact local Clifford (LC)-equivalent to it and that (2) MBQC on all circle graph states is efficiently classically simulable. Third and finally, we demonstrate that the problem of counting the number of graph states LU-equivalent to a given graph state is $\#\mathsf{P}$-hard.

### [103] [Optimal Universal Bounds for Quantum Divergences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09885)
*Gilad Gour*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发现经典散度平滑化的一个普适结构原理：优化器是截断概率向量，与具体散度无关。基于此结构洞察，推导出平滑量子散度的最优普适界，包括任意阶量子Rényi散度和假设检验散度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究经典散度平滑化背后的统一结构原理，揭示看似不同量之间的共同几何结构。这一结构洞察为推导量子散度的最优普适界提供理论基础。

Method: 识别经典散度平滑化问题的优化器为截断概率向量（clipped probability vector），这一特性与具体散度无关。基于此结构原理，推导平滑量子散度（smoothed quantum divergences）的最优普适界。

Result: 获得形式为 $D_β^{\varepsilon} \le D_α+ \mathrm{correction}$ 和 $D_β^{\varepsilon} \ge D_α+ \mathrm{correction}$ 的最优不等式，证明修正项在所有此类普适、状态无关的不等式中是最优的。结果严格改进了先前次优的界，并在早期界与本文界一致时确立了其最优性。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了经典散度平滑化的普适结构原理，并基于此推导出平滑量子散度的最优普适界，特别是获得了假设检验散度（hypothesis testing divergence）的最优普适界，为量子信息理论提供了严格的理论工具。

Abstract: We identify a universal structural principle underlying the smoothing of classical divergences: the optimizer of the smoothing problem is a clipped probability vector, independently of the specific divergence. This yields a divergence-independent characterization of all smoothed classical divergences and reveals a common geometric structure behind seemingly different quantities. Building on this structural insight, we derive optimal universal bounds for smoothed quantum divergences, including quantum R'enyi divergences of arbitrary order and the hypothesis testing divergence. Our inequalities relate divergences of different orders through bounds of the form $D_β^{\varepsilon} \le D_α+ \mathrm{correction}$ and $D_β^{\varepsilon} \ge D_α+ \mathrm{correction}$, and we prove that the correction terms are optimal among all universal, state-independent inequalities of this type. Consequently, our results strictly improve previously known bounds whenever those were suboptimal, and in cases where earlier bounds coincide with ours, our analysis establishes their optimality. In particular, we obtain optimal universal bounds for the hypothesis testing divergence.

### [104] [Hysteretic squashed entanglement in many-body quantum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09907)
*Siddhartha Das,Alexander Yosifov,Jinzhao Sun*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的条件纠缠单调度——滞后压缩纠缠（hysteretic squashed entanglement）$T_{sq}$，用于量化多体量子系统中两个子区域在第三个区域条件下的真实量子关联。该度量能有效压缩经典贡献，检测相邻和长程子系统间的量子关联，并为混合态的拓扑纠缠熵提供鲁棒量化工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体量子系统中的纠缠分布在空间区域中，其结构通常决定了态的信息处理能力。然而，表征纠缠结构，特别是对于混合态（mixed states），仍然是一个挑战。

Method: 本文提出滞后压缩纠缠（hysteretic squashed entanglement）$T_{sq}$，这是一种条件纠缠单调度（conditional entanglement monotone），用于测量多体量子态中两个子区域在第三个区域条件下的真实量子关联。$T_{sq}$ 上界于量子条件互信息（quantum conditional mutual information）的凸顶延拓（convex-roof extension）。

Result: $T_{sq}$ 展现出多种理想特性：单调性（monogamy）、凸性（convexity）、渐近连续性（asymptotic continuity）、忠实性（faithfulness）以及张量积态（tensor-product states）的可加性（additivity）。在一维横场伊辛模型（one-dimensional transverse-field Ising model）的淬火（quench）下研究条件纠缠生成，表明$T_{sq}$能有效压缩经典贡献，检测相邻和长程子系统的真实量子关联。

Conclusion: 该度量可作为混合态拓扑纠缠熵（topological entanglement entropy）的鲁棒量化工具，为探测拓扑序（topological order）和临界性（criticality）开辟了新的操作资源理论途径（operational resource-theoretic avenues）。

Abstract: Entanglement in many-body quantum systems is distributed across spatial regions, where its structure often dictates the information-processing capabilities of the state. Yet, characterizing the entanglement structure, especially for mixed states, remains a challenge. In this work, we propose hysteretic squashed entanglement $T_{sq}$, a conditional entanglement monotone that measures the genuine quantum correlations between two subregions, conditioned on a third region, in a many-body quantum state. $T_{sq}$ is upper bounded by the convex-roof extension of quantum conditional mutual information and exhibits several desirable properties like monogamy, convexity, asymptotic continuity, faithfulness, and additivity for tensor-product states. We study the conditional entanglement generation in a one-dimensional transverse-field Ising model under quench, where we show that $T_{sq}$ effectively squashes classical contributions and can detect genuine quantum correlations across both adjacent and long-range subsystems. We elucidate the utility of this measure as a robust quantifier of topological entanglement entropy for mixed states. This opens new operational resource-theoretic avenues for probing topological order and criticality.

Abstract: We conjecture analytic expressions for the non-local magic of bipartite pure qudit states of prime local dimension. Our main focus is the investigation of the quantum dynamics of differently prepared wave packets that scatter from the multi-well potential landscape. *Adrian Paul Misselwitz,Jacquelin Luneau,Peter Rabl*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了波导量子电动力学（waveguide QED）系统中光子与原子杂质相互作用及光子间非线性排斥的竞争机制，揭示了丰富的多体相图，包括类莫特绝缘态和具有长程关联的超流相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于理解纳米光子晶体、电路QED晶格和超冷原子系统中普遍存在的相互作用波导QED系统，其中光子局域化与光子-光子排斥的竞争机制尚未得到充分探索。

Method: 采用大规模数值模拟和近似解析模型相结合的方法，分析周期性杂质阵列中局域化少光子束缚态的形成机制，并确定不同填充因子下的多体基态。

Result: 研究发现丰富的相图特征，包括类莫特绝缘态（Mott-like insulating states）以及具有长程关联的超流相，这些相由未束缚但强相互作用的光子流体介导。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了Jaynes-Cummings介导的束缚与固有光子-光子排斥之间的竞争如何影响局域化束缚态的形成，并决定了相互作用波导QED系统的多体基态性质。

Abstract: We consider a generic model for interacting waveguide QED systems, where photons in a coupled-cavity array localize around atomic impurities while simultaneously interacting through local Kerr nonlinearities. This scenario appears naturally in nanophotonic crystals, circuit QED lattices, and ultracold atomic systems and is governed by the competition between attractive Jaynes-Cummings-mediated binding and intrinsic photon-photon repulsion. We analyze how this interplay affects the formation of localized few-photon bound states and determine the resulting many-body ground states for large periodic arrays of impurities and different filling factors. With the help of large-scale numerical simulations and approximate analytical models, we identify a rich phase diagram featuring Mott-like insulating states as well as superfluid phases with long-range correlations, which are mediated by an unbound, but strongly interacting photonic fluid.

</details>


### [111] [An elementary proof of symmetrization postulate in quantum mechanics for a system of particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09560)
*Diganta Parai,Nikhilesh Maity*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文从数学角度论证了全同粒子系统的波函数必须完全对称或完全反对称，基于波函数连续性、概率密度交换不变性、位形空间连通性及哈密顿量交换对称性等条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为全同粒子系统的对称化假设（symmetrization postulate）提供数学证明，忽略三维空间中的自旋部分，从纯数学角度验证波函数的对称性要求。

Method: 方法基于对N个全同粒子系统的薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）解的分析，设定四个关键条件：概率密度在粒子位置交换下保持时间不变性；波函数及其梯度连续；3N维位形空间（configuration space）连通；哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）中的势能项在粒子交换下不变。

Result: 研究结果表明，当满足上述所有条件时，波函数随时间演化必须保持完全对称（totally symmetric）或完全反对称（totally antisymmetric）的特性，从而为对称化假设提供了数学依据。

Conclusion: 结论证实了全同粒子系统的波函数对称性要求可以通过严格的数学条件推导得出，为量子力学中的对称化假设提供了理论支持，特别是在忽略自旋自由度的三维系统中。

Abstract: According to symmetrization postulate for a system of identical particles, wave function has to be completely symmetric or completely anti-symmetric. In this paper we want to mathematically justify this postulate ignoring the spin part of wave function in three dimension. For a system of N identical particles, if the solution to the governing Schrodinger equation meets these criteria: a) the probability density remains invariant when any two particle positions are exchanged over time, b) the wave function is continuous and has a continuous gradient, and the system exhibits the following characteristics: c) the configuration space, which is 3N dimensional, is connected, and d) the potential term in the Hamiltonian is invariant under the exchange of any two particle positions, then the wave function must be either totally symmetric or totally antisymmetric over time.

</details>


### [112] [System-bath model for quantum chemistry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09631)
*Dmitry S. Golubev,Reza G. Shirazi,Vladimir V. Rybkin,Benedikt M. Schoenauer,Peter Schmitteckert,Michael Marthaler*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将分子哈密顿量近似映射到量子比特哈密顿量的方法，用于计算分子的垂直激发能（vertical excitation energies）。该方法基于将仅含两个轨道的小活性空间分离，并通过量子比特或振荡器模拟剩余轨道中的电子激发。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在开发适用于近期量子计算机（near term quantum computers）计算分子激发能的新方法。传统量子化学计算面临计算复杂度挑战，而量子计算为高精度计算提供了潜在解决方案。

Method: 方法基于随机相位近似（Random Phase Approximation, RPA）思想，将分子哈密顿量约化为系统-浴（system-bath）模型。系统部分描述最高占据分子轨道（HOMO）和最低未占据分子轨道（LUMO），仅需两个量子比特编码；浴部分由振荡器或等效的两能级系统组成，对应费米能级（Fermi level）以下的电子激发。

Result: 该方法实现了分子哈密顿量到量子比特哈密顿量的近似映射，能够进行高精度量子化学计算。通过分离小活性空间并模拟剩余轨道激发，显著降低了量子资源需求。

Conclusion: 该映射方法有望启发新的计算方法和算法，用于在近期量子计算机上计算分子激发能。通过系统-浴模型简化，为量子化学计算提供了可行的量子实现路径。

Abstract: We propose an approximate mapping of a molecular Hamiltonian to a Hamiltonian of qubits, which allows for high accuracy quantum chemistry calculations of vertical excitation energies of some molecules. The mapping is based on separating of a very small active space of only two orbitals and on modeling the electronic excitations in the remaining orbitals by a set of qubits or, equivalently, by a set of oscillators. This approach is inspired by the Random Phase Approximation (RPA), in which the excitations of electron gas are described by bosonic degrees of freedom. As a result, the Hamiltonian of the molecule is reduced to that of a system-bath model. The "system" part of the Hamiltonian describes the two molecular orbitals -- the highest occupied molecular orbital (HOMO) and the lowest unoccupied molecular orbital (LUMO) -- which are populated by two electrons. Two qubits are sufficient to encode the Hamiltonian of such a system. The "bath" consists of oscillators or, equivalently, of two level systems with each of them corresponding to an electron excitation from a doubly occupied orbital below the Fermi level to an empty orbital above the Fermi level. We hope that this mapping can inspire new approaches and algorithms aimed at calculating excitation energies of molecules on near term quantum computers.

</details>


### [113] [Self-consistent mean-field quantum approximate optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09838)
*Maxime Dupont,Bhuvanesh Sundar,Meenambika Gowrishankar*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种自洽平均场量子优化算法，用于近似经典伊辛哈密顿量的基态。该算法将问题分解为独立子问题，并通过变分量子电路构建自洽环境来处理子问题间的相互作用，从而避免完整问题的计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在开发一种能够处理超出当前量子硬件比特数和门数限制的优化问题的量子算法。通过分解问题并自洽处理相互作用，使算法能够解决原本无法在现有硬件上实现的大规模优化问题。

Method: 算法采用自洽平均场方法，将经典伊辛哈密顿量（classical Ising Hamiltonians）分解为独立子问题。通过变分量子电路（variational quantum circuit）构建自洽环境，该环境以平均场方式捕获子问题间的相互作用，同时保持子问题的计算独立性。

Result: 通过谢林顿-柯克帕特里克自旋玻璃（Sherrington-Kirkpatrick spin glasses）的广泛数值模拟评估了算法性能，并实验应用于分子对接中的加权最大团问题（weighted maximum clique problem）。算法框架能够解决超出当前量子硬件能力的问题。

Conclusion: 该自洽平均场量子优化算法提供了一种有效近似经典伊辛哈密顿量基态的方法，通过问题分解和自洽环境构建，使算法能够处理超出当前量子硬件限制的大规模优化问题。

Abstract: We introduce a self-consistent mean-field quantum optimization algorithm that approximates the ground state of classical Ising Hamiltonians. The algorithm decomposes the problem into independent subproblems and treats the interactions between them in a mean-field manner. These interactions are captured by a common environment, constructed self-consistently through a variational quantum circuit, and which modifies the subproblems to account for mutual influence while maintaining computational independence. Consequently, subproblems can be solved individually, avoiding the computational cost of the full problem. We explore the properties of the generated environment and assess the algorithm's performance through extensive numerical simulations on Sherrington-Kirkpatrick spin glasses. Furthermore, we apply it experimentally to a weighted maximum clique problem applied to molecular docking. This framework enables the solution of problems that would otherwise exceed the qubit and gate counts of current quantum hardware.

</details>


### [114] [Quantum control of the environment in open quantum systems enables rapid qubit reset](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09913)
*Carlos Ortega-Taberner,Eoin O'Neill,Paul Eastham*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过精确张量网络模拟和时间依赖变分方法，分析了transmon量子比特在时间依赖系统-环境耦合下的重置过程，揭示了极化子态形成对重置的限制，并设计了能够实现10纳秒内激发态布居降至10^-6的高效重置协议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子比特重置（qubit reset）在量子技术中至关重要，通常通过将量子比特耦合到耗散环境实现。然而，量子比特-环境纠缠限制了可达到的速度和保真度，需要研究这些效应并设计更有效的重置方案。

Method: 采用精确张量网络模拟（exact tensor-network simulations）和时间依赖变分方法（time-dependent variational approach），研究具有时间依赖系统-环境耦合的transmon量子比特的重置过程。

Result: 研究揭示了重置限制源于极化子态（polaron state）的形成，并展示了如何通过时间依赖耦合逆转这一效应。确定了能够在10纳秒内实现激发态布居降至10^-6的耦合协议，证明了在非马尔可夫系统中通过控制环境动力学设计有效量子过程的可行性。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了如何通过控制开放量子系统的环境动力学，在非马尔可夫系统中设计有效的量子过程，为量子比特重置提供了新的理论框架和实用方案。

Abstract: Qubit reset is crucial in quantum technology and is typically achieved by coupling the qubit to a dissipative environment. However, the achievable speed and fidelity are limited by qubit-environment entanglement. We use exact tensor-network simulations and a time-dependent variational approach to investigate these effects for transmon qubits with a time-dependent system-environment coupling. We show that they are due to the formation of a polaron state and how this can be reversed using a time-dependent coupling. Coupling protocols are identified which achieve reset with an excited-state population of $10^{-6}$ in $10$ ns. A related paper [C. Ortega-Taberner, E. O'Neill and P. R. Eastham, arXiv:XXXX.XXXX] addresses the complementary case of control via a time-dependent Hamiltonian. Our work shows how the dynamics of the environment of an open quantum system can be controlled to design effective quantum processes in non-Markovian systems.

</details>


### [115] [Qubit reset beyond the Born-Markov approximation: optimal driving to overcome polaron formation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09914)
*Carlos Ortega-Taberner,Eoin O'Neill,Paul Eastham*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了超越玻恩-马尔可夫近似（Born-Markov approximation）的量子比特（qubit）重置问题，通过数值精确的张量网络方法（tensor network methods）和时间依赖变分原理（time-dependent variational principle），发现系统-环境关联（system-environment correlations）的建立会限制重置保真度（reset fidelity）。研究采用数值最优控制（numerical optimal control）设计时间依赖的量子比特哈密顿量（time-dependent qubit Hamiltonians），以克服这一限制并逆转极化子（polaron）形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子比特通常通过与低温环境耦合重置到已知状态，在玻恩-马尔可夫近似下这种耦合产生指数弛豫，仅受温度限制而获得高重置保真度。本研究旨在探索超越该近似的量子比特重置问题，特别是系统-环境关联的建立如何限制重置性能。

Method: 采用数值精确的张量网络方法和时间依赖变分原理，研究描述transmon量子比特与电阻耦合的自旋-玻色子模型（spin-boson model）。通过数值最优控制寻找时间依赖的量子比特哈密顿量，以引导相关系统-环境状态的动力学过程。

Result: 超越玻恩-马尔可夫近似时，重置保真度受系统-环境关联建立限制，这对应于极化子的形成。最优控制策略能够克服这一限制，当环境被滤波以覆盖更小频谱范围时控制效果更佳，且在考虑transmon的多能级特性时仍保持有效。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明如何克服重置速度和保真度的限制，以及时间依赖驱动如何引导系统-环境关联并逆转极化子形成。相关论文[C. Ortega-Taberner, E. O'Neill and P. R. Eastham, arXiv:XXXX.XXXX]则通过时间依赖的系统-环境耦合控制处理了互补情况。

Abstract: Qubits are typically reset into a known state by coupling them to a low-temperature environment. When treated in the Born-Markov approximation such couplings produce exponential relaxation to equilibrium, giving high reset fidelities limited only by temperature. We investigate qubit reset beyond this approximation, using numerically exact tensor network methods and the time-dependent variational principle, focussing on a spin-boson model describing a transmon qubit coupled to a resistor. Beyond the Born-Markov approximation the reset fidelity becomes limited by the buildup of system-environment correlations which corresponds to the formation of a polaron. We implement numerical optimal control to find time-dependent qubit Hamiltonians which overcome this limitation by steering the dynamics of the correlated system-environment state. The optimal controls becomes more effective when the environment is filtered to span a smaller spectral range, and remain effective when the multilevel nature of the transmon is considered. A related paper [C. Ortega-Taberner, E. O'Neill and P. R. Eastham, arXiv:XXXX.XXXX] addresses the complementary case of control via a time-dependent system-environment coupling. Our results show how limitations on reset speed and fidelity can be overcome, and how time-dependent driving can steer system-environment correlations and reverse polaron formation.

</details>

### [116] [Thermal Hall conductivity from semiclassical spin dynamics simulations: implementation and applications to chiral ferromagnets and Kitaev magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08777)
*Ignacio Salgado-Linares,Alexander Mook,Léo Mangeolle,Johannes Knolle*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究采用半经典自旋动力学模拟方法研究磁性系统中的热霍尔输运，通过线性响应框架计算热霍尔电导率，并将其应用于两种模型：具有面内Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用的方形晶格手性磁体和场中的反铁磁Kitaev模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究磁性系统中的热霍尔输运现象，特别是在非线性效应（如磁振子-磁振子相互作用和强热涨落）起关键作用的区域，需要超越简单本征非相互作用近似的计算方法。

Method: 采用半经典自旋动力学（semiclassical spin dynamics）模拟方法，基于线性响应（linear response）框架，通过实时能量流关联（real-time energy current correlations）和能量磁化（energy magnetization）计算热霍尔电导率（thermal Hall conductivity）。

Result: 该方法成功应用于两种模型：具有面内Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（in-plane Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction）的方形晶格手性磁体（square-lattice chiral magnet）和场中的反铁磁Kitaev模型（antiferromagnetic Kitaev model in a field），展示了半经典自旋动力学在捕捉超越简单本征非相互作用近似的定量效应方面的效率。

Conclusion: 半经典自旋动力学方法为研究热霍尔输运提供了有效的计算框架，特别是在需要考虑磁振子-磁振子相互作用（magnon-magnon interactions）和强热涨落（strong thermal fluctuations）的非线性区域，可作为与实验比较的基准。

Abstract: We investigate thermal Hall transport in magnetic systems, using semiclassical spin dynamics simulations. Building on a linear response framework, we discuss the intricacies of computing the thermal Hall conductivity from real-time energy current correlations and the energy magnetization. We then apply this methodology to two models: a square-lattice chiral magnet with in-plane Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction, and the antiferromagnetic Kitaev model in a field. Our results demonstrate the efficiency of semiclassical spin dynamics to study thermal Hall transport capturing quantitative effects beyond the simple intrinsic non-interacting approximation. They can serve as a benchmark for comparison with experiments in regimes where non-linearities from magnon-magnon interactions and strong thermal fluctuations play a crucial role.

### [117] [Proximate Spin Liquid Ground State Arising from Competing Stripy and 120$^{\circ}$ Spin Correlations in the Triangular Quantum Antiferromagnet ErMgGaO$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08934)
*S. H. -Y. Huang,S. Petit,Bo Yuan,Z. W. Cronkwright,C. Pinvidic,Y. Wang,E. M. Smith,S. Bhattacharya,C. Yang,J. -M. Zanotti,Q. Berrod,M. B. Stone,A. I. Kolesnikov,R. J. Cava,E. Kermarrec,B. D. Gaulin*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: ErMgGaO₄是一种量子反铁磁体，在约2.5K处显示自旋玻璃（spin glass）转变，约为其居里-外斯（Curie-Weiss）温度的1/6。通过非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering）测量，观察到二维条纹（stripy）相关性和120°型相关性共存，低能连续谱带宽约0.8 meV。采用J₁-J₂-Δ模型拟合，参数表明该体系接近自旋液体（spin liquid）与条纹有序相（stripy ordered phases）的量子相边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究ErMgGaO₄作为量子反铁磁体的磁性质，特别是与其姐妹化合物YbMgGaO₄的区别。该材料在约2.5K处显示明确的自旋玻璃转变，需要探究其磁激发谱和交换耦合机制，以理解其低能物理行为。

Method: 采用非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering）测量粉末ErMgGaO₄样品。使用Warren线形分析二维相关性的弹性散射，通过线性自旋波理论（linear spin wave theory）建模非弹性散射，并采用三角晶格上的J₁-J₂-Δ模型估计自旋哈密顿量参数。

Result: 观察到晶体电场（crystalline electric field, CEF）跃迁，第一激发能级约3 meV，可能影响交换耦合。在T_g以下，主导的二维条纹（stripy）相关性与持续的120°型相关性共存。低能非弹性散射显示带宽约0.8 meV的连续谱，可用阻尼谐振子（damped harmonic oscillators, DHO）模型描述。J₁-J₂-Δ模型拟合得到J₁/J₂=0.13±0.03和Δ=0.4±0.1。

Conclusion: ErMgGaO₄位于理论J₁-J₂-Δ相图中接近自旋液体（spin liquid）与条纹有序相（stripy ordered phases）量子相边界的位置。其低能磁激发谱可用线性自旋波理论良好描述，表明该体系具有丰富的磁相关性和量子临界行为。

Abstract: ErMgGaO$_4$ is a quantum antiferromagnet wherein the pseudospin-1/2 degrees of freedom of Er$^{3+}$ decorate two-dimensional triangular planes separated by disordered non-magnetic bilayers of Mg$^{2+}$ and Ga$^{3+}$. Unlike its sister compound, YbMgGaO$_4$, our powder ErMgGaO$_4$ sample shows a clear spin glass transition near $T_g \sim 2.5$~K, about 1/6 of its Curie-Weiss temperature. We have carried out new inelastic neutron scattering measurements on these powder ErMgGaO$_4$ samples. At high energies, we observed crystalline electric field (CEF) transitions within the $J=15/2$ multiplet of Er$^{3+}$, but with the first excited CEF level sufficiently low in energy ($\sim$ 3~meV) so as to allow the possibility that virtual CEF transitions influence the exchange couplings. At E=0, we observe diffuse elastic scattering which is analysed using Warren lineshapes appropriate for two dimensional correlations. This reveals dominant 2D stripy correlations below $T_g$, coexisting with 2D 120$^\circ$-type correlations that persist above $T_g$. At low temperatures, the low energy inelastic component of the scattering shows a continuum with bandwidth of $\sim$ 0.8~meV. This dynamic magnetic spectral weight can be modeled at all $Q$, energies, and temperatures as the sum of high energy and low energy damped harmonic oscillators (DHO), with the high energy DHO defining the bandwidth of $\sim$ 0.8~meV. We use linear spin wave theory to model this inelastic scattering and to estimate its spin Hamiltonian parameters in terms of a $J_1-J_2-Δ$ model on the triangular lattice. This gives a good description of the low lying spectral weight for ErMgGaO4, and allows us to place it on the theoretical $J_1-J_2-Δ$ phase diagram with $\frac{J_1}{J_2}=0.13 \pm 0.03$ and $Δ=0.4 \pm 0.1$, which is close to the expected quantum phase boundary between the spin liquid and the stripy ordered phases.

</details>


### [118] [Interplay of Rashba spin-orbit coupling and Coulomb interaction in topological spin-triplet excitonic condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09362)
*Quoc-Huy Ninh,Huu-Nha Nguyen,Van-Nham Phan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了Rashba自旋轨道耦合（SOC）与库仑吸引在二维电子-空穴系统中协同稳定拓扑自旋三重态激子凝聚（ECs）的效应，揭示了从拓扑半金属到拓扑激子凝聚的转变机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Rashba自旋轨道耦合（SOC）与库仑吸引在外部磁场中协同稳定二维电子-空穴系统拓扑自旋三重态激子凝聚（ECs）的微观机制，为在非中心对称Janus过渡金属二硫化物和扭曲范德华异质结中实现此类凝聚提供理论指导。

Method: 采用无限制Hartree-Fock方法结合随机相位近似（random-phase approximation），研究二维电子-空穴系统中Rashba SOC与库仑相互作用的协同效应。

Result: 弱电子-空穴库仑相互作用时，带内Rashba SOC诱导自旋-动量锁定和拓扑半金属行为；强相互作用稳定自旋三重态ECs。增加价带SOC驱动从拓扑平庸ECs到拓扑自旋向上ECs的转变，后者具有量子化陈数C=2。动力学激子磁化率揭示了作为凝聚前兆的软自旋向上三重态模式。

Abstract: The cooperative effect of Rashba spin-orbit coupling (SOC) and Coulomb attraction in stabilizing topological spin-triplet excitonic condensates (ECs) in two-dimensional electron-hole systems in external magnetic field is investigated by using an unrestricted Hartree-Fock approach combined with the random-phase approximation. At weak electron-hole Coulomb interaction, the intraband Rashba SOC induces spin-momentum locking and topological semimetal behavior, while stronger interaction stabilizes spin-triplet ECs. Increasing the valence-band SOC drives a transition from a topologically trivial EC with coexisting spin-up and spin-down components to a topological spin-up EC only with quantized Chern number $C=2$. The dynamical excitonic susceptibility reveals a soft spin-up triplet mode acting as the precursor of the condensate. These results establish a microscopic mechanism for Rashba SOC-induced topological ECs and suggest realistic situations for their realization in noncentrosymmetric Janus transition-metal dichalcogenides and twisted van der Waals heterostructures.

These experiments are complemented by density-functional-theory calculations combined with the construction of maximally localized Wannier functions and an analysis of the relevant superexchange pathways. Quantum Monte Carlo simulations are employed to model thermodynamic properties and to quantitatively determine the magnetic exchange parameters. Our combined approach identifies Bi$_2$CuO$_3$(SO$_4$) as a two-leg spin-ladder system with ferromagnetic rungs ($J'$ $\approx -208$ K) and antiferromagnetic legs ($J$ $\approx 258$ K). Abstract: We determine the finite-temperature phase diagram and critical behavior of the classical square-lattice Heisenberg-compass model using large-scale Monte Carlo simulations and finite-size scaling.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 主要方法包括：扩展Feynman变分法到紧束缚晶格；重新审视并推广传统分析近似，如正则变换（canonical transformations）和自洽Wigner-Brillouin型近似；将方法扩展到具有Rashba型自旋轨道耦合的极化子。

Result: 改进的Wigner-Brillouin方案产生了无共振的动量依赖极化子自能（polaron self-energy），在整个布里渊区内与数值精确结果吻合良好。修正的Feynman变分法在基态能量和色散方面表现出与其他成熟分析方法相当甚至更优的精度。

Abstract: We develop and compare several analytical approximations for the polaron problem in finite-width, non-parabolic conduction bands. The main focus of the work is an extension of the Feynman variational method to a tight-binding lattice, where the effective-mass approximation is no longer applicable. The resulting variational formulation is not restricted to a specific phonon dispersion or electron-phonon interaction and provides a uniform description across weak-, intermediate-, and strong-coupling regimes. We revisit and generalize other analytical approaches traditionally formulated for continuum polarons, including canonical transformations and self-consistent Wigner-Brillouin-type approximations. For lattice polarons, these methods exhibit qualitative features absent in the continuum case, such as a nontrivial connection between weak- and strong-coupling limits. We show that an improved Wigner-Brillouin scheme yields a momentum-dependent polaron self-energy free of resonances and in good agreement with numerically exact results over the whole range of momenta within the Brillouin zone. All methods are applied to the Holstein model and are benchmarked against numerically exact calculations, including Diagrammatic Monte Carlo (both our calculations and preceding works), exact diagonalization, and density-matrix renormalization-group results. The analytical approaches are extended to polarons with Rashba-type spin-orbit coupling, providing a stringent test of their applicability in systems with nontrivial band structure. Our results demonstrate that the modified Feynman variational method yields ground-state energies and dispersions with accuracy comparable to, and in many cases exceeding, that of other established analytical approaches. The developed framework offers a versatile and reliable analytical description of lattice polarons beyond the continuum approximation.

These results establish MnSb$_2$ as a pressure-stabilized marcasite magnet with a highly tunable, complex magnetic ground state and a compelling stoichiometric platform for exploring unconventional magnetic behavior, including potential altermagnetism.

### [124] [Evidence of universal spectral collapse at a marginal dynamical regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09665)

TL;DR: 该研究提出强关联材料中的非相干电子谱源于自生动态无序与竞争涨落，而非传统认为的静态无序或材料特定机制。通过推导普适标度函数ρ(z)=exp(-z²/4)Dν(z)并应用于多种材料体系，发现非相干谱在标度变换后坍缩至单一普适曲线，揭示低能下微观细节无关的固定点行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究推导了电子动力学耦合时变散射产生的谱函数形式ρ(z)=exp(-z²/4)Dν(z)，其中z为标度能量，Dν表示抛物柱面函数。将该标度函数应用于多种材料的角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）能量分布曲线，包括铜酸盐Nd₂₋ₓCeₓCuO₄和Bi₂Sr₂CaCu₂O₈₊δ、Kagome金属CsCr₃Sb₅以及双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了跨越多种强关联材料的连续谱主导ARPES谱的统一定量框架，证明非相干谱源于自生动态无序与竞争涨落导致的边际动力学机制，而非静态无序或材料特异性因素。

Abstract: Incoherent electronic states in strongly correlated materials are commonly attributed to disorder or material specific mechanisms. Here we show that incoherent spectra instead arise from self-generated dynamical disorder associated with competing fluctuations. In this regime, electron dynamics coupled to time-dependent scattering naturally produce a spectral function of the form rho (z) = exp(-z^2/4) Dnu (z), where z is a scaled energy and Dnu denotes the parabolic cylinder function. This form reflects a marginal dynamical regime characterized by non-Markovian temporal correlations. Applying this scaling function to angle resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES) energy distribution curves from the cuprates Nd2-xCexCuO4 and Bi2Sr2CaCu2O8+delta, the Kagome metal CsCr3Sb5, and the double-layer nickelate La3Ni2O7, we find that incoherent spectra are quantitatively described by rho (z), differing only in non-universal amplitude and energy scales. After rescaling, the datasets collapse onto a single universal curve characterized by a fixed parabolic-cylinder order nu = -1/2. The observed spectral collapse indicates a fixed-point-like regime in which microscopic details such as lattice geometry, band structure, and chemical composition become irrelevant at low energies. These results establish a unified and quantitative framework for continuum-dominated ARPES spectra across diverse strongly correlated materials.

### [125] [Entanglement Measure Response to Modular Flow and Chiral Topological Phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09717)
*Yunlong Zang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了量子态纠缠哈密顿量驱动的实时动力学过程中两种纠缠度量的响应，提出了统一的生成函数框架，并证明其响应由手征拓扑不变量唯一确定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来基于纠缠的量子物相表征取得重要进展，纠缠哈密顿量（entanglement Hamiltonian）作为量子态的内禀性质理论上决定了所有实验可观测的局域可观测量。本文旨在研究两种纠缠度量在纠缠哈密顿量驱动的实时动力学过程中的响应。

Method: 通过提出统一的生成函数 $\langleρ_{AB}^α\mathrm{e}^{λ{Q}_{AB}}\mathrm{e}^{μ{Q}_{BC}}ρ_{BC}^β\rangle$，该函数推广了最近提出的Rényi模交换子（Rényi modular commutator）。采用两种独立方法验证：自由费米子系统使用实空间陈数公式，以及通过手征共形场论正则化纠缠切割的有效场论处理。

Result: 在适当极限下，生成函数给出Rényi熵及其带电版本的响应，这些响应被证明由手征拓扑不变量唯一确定，特别是手征中心荷（chiral central charge）和霍尔电导（Hall conductance）。两种验证方法得到一致结果。

Conclusion: 研究建立了纠缠度量在模流（modular flow）过程中的响应与手征拓扑不变量之间的直接联系，提出的生成函数框架为纠缠哈密顿量动力学研究提供了统一的理论工具，并通过自由费米子和有效场论两种方法验证了结果的普适性。

Abstract: Recent years have witnessed significant progress in the entanglement-based characterization of quantum phases of matter. The primary objects of interest are the reduced density matrix and its associated entanglement Hamiltonian. As intrinsic properties of a quantum state, these quantities theoretically determine all experimentally accessible local observables. In this work, we investigate the response of two entanglement measures to the real-time dynamics driven by the entanglement Hamiltonian--a process known as modular flow. We demonstrate that our results can be unified into a single generating function, $\langleρ_{AB}^α\mathrm{e}^{λ{Q}_{AB}}\mathrm{e}^{μ{Q}_{BC}}ρ_{BC}^β\rangle$. This function is of independent interest as it represents a generalization of the recently proposed Rényi modular commutator. In appropriate limits, this function yields the response of Rényi entropy and its charged version, which we find to be uniquely determined by chiral topological invariants, specifically the chiral central charge and the Hall conductance. Our analytical findings are validated through two independent approaches: (i) free fermion systems using the real-space Chern number formula, and (ii) an effective field theory treatment that regularizes the entanglement cut via chiral conformal field theory. Both methods yield consistent results.

*Shang-Jie Liou,Herbert F. Fotso*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究探讨无序（disorder）如何影响相互作用量子系统中的绝热性（adiabaticity），发现无序强度和脉冲持续时间均能抑制相互作用调制后系统的总能量变化，促进更绝热的响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究无序对相互作用量子系统中绝热性的影响，通过分析系统在相互作用调制（或"脉冲"）后的状态变化，探讨无序如何改变系统的能量和热响应。

Method: 通过改变相互作用强度（从零到最大值再回零）的时间调制，采用矩形（rectangular）、三角形（triangular）和高斯（Gaussian）三种脉冲形状，在不同无序强度下分析系统总能量和有效温度的变化。

Result: 发现脉冲持续时间与总能量变化呈负相关，无序强度与总能量变化也呈现稳健的负相关，表明增强无序能抑制相互作用脉冲后系统的残余能量，促进更绝热的响应；三角形脉冲在可比条件下产生最小的总能量变化。

Conclusion: 无序是影响相互作用时间调制过程中能量和温度变化的关键因素，无序诱导和持续时间诱导的绝热性在所有脉冲形状中均一致观察到，为理解无序量子系统的热响应提供了定量关系。

Abstract: We investigate how disorder affects adiabaticity in an interacting quantum system by assessing its effect on the state of the system after an interaction modulation, or interaction ``pulse" ,whereby the interaction is changed from zero to a maximum value and then back to zero following a given time profile. We find that, independently of the disorder strength and pulse shapes (rectangular, triangular, and Gaussian), the pulse duration is negatively correlated with the change in total energy in the system. That is, the longer duration reduces the change in total energy for each protocol. Most importantly, across different considered pulse shapes, we find a robust negative correlation between the disorder strength and the change in total energy across the interaction pulse. Namely, increasing the disorder strength systematically suppresses the residual energy added to the system after the interaction pulse, indicating a more adiabatic response. These two effects, disorder-induced and duration-induced adiabaticity, are consistently observed across all three pulse shapes. Among the protocols, the triangular pulse yields the smallest change in total energy in the system over comparable conditions, demonstrating the most adiabatic response. In addition to the energy analysis, we also examine how disorder modifies the effective temperature change across the interaction pulse, to further establish a quantitative relation between disorder and the thermal response. Altogether, our results identify disorder as a key factor in both the energy and the temperature variation over the time-modulation of the interaction.

</details>

### [127] [Testing Screened Modified Gravity with Strongly Lensed Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09340)
*Chengsheng Mu,Shuo Cao,Shuxun Tian,Xinyue Jiang,Chenfa Zheng,Dadian Cheng*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文研究了利用强引力透镜化的引力波（gravitational waves）测试屏蔽修正引力理论（screened modified gravity theories）的可能性，开发了理论框架来测量存在屏蔽效应时的后牛顿参数γ_PN，发现下一代引力波探测器能对PPN参数提供严格约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 屏蔽机制（screening mechanisms）是许多修正引力理论的关键组成部分，它们满足广义相对论（General Relativity）的局部测试，同时解释宇宙尺度的加速膨胀。强引力透镜化的引力波为研究宇宙学和基础物理提供了独特的观测手段。

Method: 开发了精细的理论和统计框架，以测量存在屏蔽效应时的后牛顿参数γ_PN。引入质量截断幂律（mass-truncated power-law）和Navarro-Frenk-White（NFW）模型来量化修正的透镜势（lensing potential）。通过结合强透镜引力波系统的绝对放大率和时间延迟测量，解决了质量片简并（mass-sheet degeneracy）问题。

Result: 研究发现，下一代引力波探测器探测到的单个透镜引力波系统能够在不同屏蔽尺度（screening scales）Λ上对PPN参数γ_PN提供严格约束。强透镜引力波的未来测量有望在kpc-Mpc尺度上探测与广义相对论的偏离。

Conclusion: 强透镜引力波的测量具有巨大潜力，能够利用透镜引力波信号提供的更精确时间延迟，在kpc-Mpc尺度上寻找与广义相对论的偏离，从而测试屏蔽修正引力理论。

Abstract: Screening mechanisms are essential components in many modified gravity theories, which satisfy local tests of General Relativity (GR) and address cosmic acceleration on cosmological scales. The strong gravitational lensing of gravitational waves (GWs) offers a unique observational probe into cosmology and fundamental physics. In this paper, we investigate the possibility of testing screened modified gravity theories with strongly lensed gravitational waves. Specially, we develop the refined theoretical and statistical framework, in order to measure the post-Newtonian parameter $γ_{\text{PN}}$ in the presence of screening effects. Specially, the mass-truncated power-law and Navarro-Frenk-White (NFW) models are introduced to quantify the modified lensing potential. Our analysis also addresses the mass-sheet degeneracy (MSD) problem, by incorporating the absolute magnification and time delay measurements accessible through strongly lensed GW systems. We find that individual lensed GW system detected by next-generation GW detectors can provide stringent constraints on the PPN parameter ($γ_{\text{PN}}$) across different screening scales ($Λ$). Therefore, future measurements of strongly lensed GWs have great promise to seek departures from GR on kpc-Mpc scales, due to more precise time delay from lensed GW signals.

### [128] [Verifying Good Regulator Conditions for Hypergraph Observers: Natural Gradient Learning from Causal Invariance via Established Theorems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09067)
*Max Zhuravlev*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 该研究验证了因果不变超图基底中的持久观测者满足Conant-Ashby良好调节器定理条件，连接了Wolfram的超图物理与Vanchurin的神经网络宇宙学框架，推导出量子-经典阈值κ(F)=2，并表明单个观测者可在Fisher度规的不同特征方向上同时占据不同Vanchurin体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在验证因果不变超图基底中的持久观测者是否满足Conant-Ashby良好调节器定理（Good Regulator Theorem）条件，从而连接Wolfram的超图物理（hypergraph physics）框架与Vanchurin的神经网络宇宙学（neural network cosmology）理论。

Method: 基于Wolfram的超图物理和Vanchurin的神经网络宇宙学，将持久观测者形式化为最小化其与环境边界预测误差的实体。应用Conant-Ashby定理的现代重述，证明超图观测者满足良好调节器条件。通过信息几何（information geometry）推导Fisher信息度规（Fisher information metric），并应用Amari的重参数化不变梯度唯一性定理（uniqueness theorem for reparameterization-invariant gradients）。

Result: 超图观测者满足良好调节器条件，需要维持内部模型。一旦存在带损失函数的内部模型，Fisher信息度规自然涌现。自然梯度下降（natural gradient descent）是唯一可接受的学习规则。在指数族观测者的M=F^2假设和特定收敛时间泛函下，推导出Vanchurin Type II框架中体系参数α的闭式解，量子-经典阈值位于κ(F)=2。引入方向性体系参数α_{v_k}和无迹偏差张量，表明单个观测者可沿Fisher度规的不同特征方向同时占据不同Vanchurin体系。

Conclusion: 通过已建立的定理连接了Wolfram和Vanchurin框架，提供了约25-30%的新贡献。研究显示量子-经典阈值κ(F)=2的预测高度依赖于模型，因为三种替代收敛模型未能重现该结果。该工作为理解观测者在超图基底中的信息处理特性提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We verify that persistent observers in causally invariant hypergraph substrates satisfy the conditions of the Conant-Ashby Good Regulator Theorem. Building on Wolfram's hypergraph physics and Vanchurin's neural network cosmology, we formalize persistent observers as entities that minimize prediction error at their boundary with the environment. Applying a modern reformulation of the Conant-Ashby theorem, we demonstrate that hypergraph observers satisfy Good Regulator conditions, requiring them to maintain internal models. Once an internal model with loss function exists, the emergence of a Fisher information metric follows from standard information geometry. Invoking Amari's uniqueness theorem for reparameterization-invariant gradients, we show that natural gradient descent is the unique admissible learning rule. Under the ansatz M=F^2 for exponential family observers and one specific convergence time functional, we derive a closed-form formula for the regime parameter alpha in Vanchurin's Type II framework, with a quantum-classical threshold at kappa(F)=2. However, three alternative convergence models do not reproduce this result, so this prediction is strongly model-dependent. We further introduce the directional regime parameter alpha_{v_k} and the trace-free deviation tensor, showing that a single observer can simultaneously occupy different Vanchurin regimes along different eigendirections of the Fisher metric. This connects Wolfram and Vanchurin frameworks through established theorems, providing approximately 25-30% novel contribution.

### [129] [How to formulate the $\mathbb{Z}_8$ topological invariant of Majorana fermion on the lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09354)
*Sho Araki,Hidenori Fukaya,Tetsuya Onogi,Satoshi Yamaguchi*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种Arf-Brown-Kervaire (ABK) 拓扑不变量在格点规范理论中的实现方法，该不变量取值为ℤ₈，并通过Wilson Dirac算子的Pfaffian提取，在多种二维非定向流形上进行了数值验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑不变量及其相关反常在理解量子场论低能现象中至关重要。在格点规范理论中，标准的ℤ值Atiyah-Singer指标通过重叠Dirac算子和Ginsparg-Wilson关系表述，但更一般拓扑不变量的扩展仍然有限。

Method: 通过仔细处理边界条件（包含或不包含畴壁质量项），证明了ABK不变量可以从Wilson Dirac算子的Pfaffian中提取。在二维格点上提供了数值验证。

Result: 在二维格点上获得的ℤ₈值结果在环面（torus）、克莱因瓶（Klein bottle）、实射影平面（real projective plane）和莫比乌斯带（Möbius strip）上与连续理论的结果一致。

Conclusion: 本研究成功实现了Arf-Brown-Kervaire (ABK) 拓扑不变量在格点规范理论中的表述，为更一般拓扑不变量在格点上的研究提供了有效方法。

Abstract: Topological invariants and their associated anomalies have played a crucial role in understanding low-energy phenomena in quantum field theories. In lattice gauge theory, the standard $\mathbb{Z}$-valued Atiyah-Singer index is formulated via the overlap Dirac operator through the Ginsparg-Wilson relation, but extensions to more general topological invariants have remained limited. In this work, we propose a lattice formulation of the Arf-Brown-Kervaire (ABK) invariant, which takes values in $\mathbb{Z}_8$. The ABK invariant arises in Majorana fermion partition functions with reflection symmetry on two-dimensional non-oriented manifolds, and its definition involves an infinite sum over Dirac eigenvalues that must be properly regularized. By carefully treating the boundary conditions, with and without a domain-wall mass term, we demonstrate that the ABK invariant can be extracted from Pfaffians of the Wilson Dirac operator. We further provide numerical verification on two-dimensional lattices, showing that the $\mathbb{Z}_8$-valued results on the torus, Klein bottle, real projective plane, and Möbius strip agree with those in the continuum theory.

### [130] [Pfaffian-based topological invariants for one dimensional semiconductor-superconductor heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08786)
*Binayyak B. Roy,William B. Cason,Nimish Sharma,Sumanta Tewari*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文综述了一维半导体-超导体纳米线异质结构中基于Pfaffian的ℤ₂拓扑不变量，阐明了它们在有限系统和无序系统中的有效性。通过引入超晶格描述，证明了实空间Pfaffian不变量在缺乏微观平移对称性时仍然保持良好定义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在澄清一维半导体-超导体纳米线异质结构中基于Pfaffian的ℤ₂拓扑不变量在有限和无序系统中的有效性。研究动机源于需要建立适用于实际非理想系统的拓扑不变量的明确定义。

Method: 采用Pfaffian方法分析拓扑相变，通过粒子-空穴对称动量点k=0,π处哈密顿量Pfaffian乘积的符号变化定义ℤ₂基塔耶夫不变量。引入超晶格描述周期性重复无序，建立实空间构造与动量空间不变量之间的等价性。

Result: 证明了动量空间不变量与基于扭曲边界条件的实空间构造等价。在无序系统中，实空间Pfaffian不变量保持良好定义，且等价于最近定义的周期性无序不变量。建立了Pfaffian符号与基态费米子宇称的直接物理联系。

Conclusion: 该研究为有限和无序一维拓扑超导系统提供了统一的拓扑不变量框架。数值结果证实了Pfaffian符号反转、通量诱导能级交叉和基态宇称切换之间的对应关系，为实验探测提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We review the Pfaffian-based $\mathbb{Z}_2$ topological invariants in one dimensional semiconductor-superconductor (SM-SC) nanowire heterostructures and clarify their validity in finite and disordered systems. For the clean nanowire, the product of the Pfaffians of the Hamiltonian at particle-hole symmetric momenta $k=0,π$ changes sign at the topological phase transition defined by the bulk gap closing, leading to the definition of $\mathbb{Z}_2$ Kitaev invariant also known as Majorana number. We show that this momentum-space invariant is equivalent to a real space construction based on twisted boundary conditions, in which the sign of the product of the Pfaffians of the Hamiltonian under periodic and anti-periodic boundary conditions defines the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ index. By introducing a superlattice description of periodically repeated disorder, we demonstrate that the real space Pfaffian invariant defined as the sign of the Pfaffians of the Hamiltonian with periodic and anti-periodic boundary conditions, remains a well defined invariant even in the absence of microscopic translational symmetry. Within this framework, it is also equivalent to the recently defined periodic disorder invariant (PDI), which constitutes an integer valued ($\mathbb{Z}$) topological invariant in the presence of chiral symmetry. Finally, we prove that the sign of the Pfaffian of a quadratic Hamiltonian equals the fermion parity of its ground state, establishing a direct physical interpretation of the invariant, in terms of sign of the product of the ground state fermion parity with periodic and anti-periodic boundary conditions. Numerical results confirm the correspondence between sign of the Pfaffian reversals, flux-induced level crossings, and ground-state parity switching in clean and disordered nanowires.

</details>


### [131] [Structural and electronic signatures of strain-tunable marginally twisted bilayer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09295)
*Pei Ouyang,Jiawei Yu,Qian Li,Guihao Jia,Yuyang Wang,Kebin Xiao,Hongyun Zhang,Zhiqiang Hu,Pierre A. Pantaleón,Zhen Zhan,Shuyun Zhou,Francisco Guinea,Qi-Kun Xue,Wei Li*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微小扭转角（marginally twisted）双层石墨烯被预测具有独特的结构和电子性质，但实验表征仍然有限。本研究旨在通过扫描隧道显微镜（STM）对这些系统进行实验表征，以阐明其电子结构。

Method: 使用扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）研究扭转角为0.06°-0.35°的双层石墨烯系统。通过紧束缚计算（tight-binding calculations）验证应变驱动的畴壁转变。

Result: AA堆叠区显示出显著的隧穿谱峰，表明高度局域化的电子态；AB区域显示均匀的多重谱峰，表明强晶格重构和增强的电子均匀性。识别出两种不同的应变诱导畴壁：一种显示尖锐的-120 meV谱峰（剪切型），另一种显示不同的光谱特征（混合剪切-拉伸型）。

Conclusion: 这些结果阐明了微小扭转角双层石墨烯的电子结构，并确立了应变作为畴壁态的控制参数。紧束缚计算验证了两种畴壁类型的应变驱动转变，并确认了应变介导的畴壁转变的直接观测。

Abstract: Marginally twisted bilayer graphene having small twist angles is predicted to exhibit unique structural and electronic properties, though experimental characterization remains limited. Using scanning tunneling microscopy, we investigate such systems with twist angles of 0.06^{\circ}-0.35^{\circ}. AA-stacked regions reveal a pronounced tunneling spectral peak signifying highly localized electronic states. Conversely, AB domains display uniform multiple spectral peaks, indicative of strong lattice reconstruction and enhanced electronic homogeneity. We identify two distinct strain-induced domain walls: one exhibits a sharp -120 meV spectral peak (shear type), while the other shows distinct spectral characteristics (mixed shear-tensile type). Tight-binding calculations verify strain-driven transformations of both domain wall types and confirm direct observation of strain-mediated domain wall transitions. These results elucidate the electronic structure of marginally twisted bilayer graphene and establish strain as a control parameter for domain wall states.

### [132] [Orbital-Zeeman cross correlation in $p$- and $d$-wave altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09325)
*Tomonari Mizoguchi,Soshun Ozaki*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了交变磁体（altermagnets）中的轨道-塞曼（orbital-Zeeman, OZ）交叉项，分析了其在Rashba金属和三维拓扑绝缘体（TIs）表面狄拉克锥中的行为特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体是一类新型磁体，具有大的自旋劈裂但总磁矩为零。这种非常规的自旋劈裂导致了各种特征现象，如自旋电流产生。本文旨在研究交变磁体中的轨道-塞曼交叉项，以理解其独特性质。

Method: 研究考虑了存在交变磁序参数情况下的两种系统：Rashba金属和三维拓扑绝缘体（TIs）表面狄拉克锥。分别分析了p波和d波序参数对轨道-塞曼交叉项的影响。

Result: 对于Rashba金属，p波序参数对OZ项影响有限，而d波序参数在序参数足够大时会导致OZ项符号改变。对于TI表面，p波序参数保留了OZ项随化学势（μ）的阶跃函数型依赖关系，但幅度减小；d波情况下μ=0处的跳跃幅度保持不变，但OZ项随|μ|增大而减小。

Conclusion: 交变磁体中的轨道-塞曼交叉项表现出对序参数波对称性的敏感依赖性，p波和d波序参数在Rashba金属和拓扑绝缘体表面产生不同的调制效应，揭示了交变磁序与轨道自由度的复杂相互作用。

Abstract: Altermagnets are a novel class of magnets that exhibit a large spin splitting but the total magnetic moment is vanishing. This unconventional spin splitting gives rise to various characteristic phenomena, such as spin current generation. In this paper, we study the orbital-Zeeman (OZ) cross term in altermagnets. Specifically, we consider the Rashba metal and the surface Dirac cones of three-dimensional topological insulators (TIs) in the presence of the altermagnetic order parameters. For the Rashba metals, the $p$-wave order parameter exerts only a limited influence on the OZ term, whereas the $d$-wave one causes the sign change of it when the order parameter becomes sufficiently large. For the TI surface, the $p$-wave order parameter retains the step-function-type dependence of the OZ term as a function of the chemical potential ($μ$) associated with the jump at $μ=0$, observed in the TI surface without magnetism, but its magnitude is reduced. For the $d$-wave case, the magnitude of jump at $μ=0$ is preserved but the OZ term decreases as increasing $|μ|$.

### [133] [Magneto-optical Response of 5-SL MnBi$_2$Te$_4$ in Spin-Flip States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09578)
*Shahid Sattar,Roman Stepanov,A. H. MacDonald,C. M. Canali*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究通过第一性原理计算和简化耦合狄拉克锥模型，揭示了五层MnBi2Te4薄膜中自旋构型、拓扑序和磁光响应之间的相互作用，发现尽管具有非零面外磁化，系统可呈现拓扑绝缘体或拓扑平庸绝缘体状态，取决于顶层与底层自旋相对取向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于近期对MnBi2Te4薄膜中自旋翻转/翻转转变的实验研究，旨在探究层间自旋构型、拓扑序与磁光响应之间的相互作用，特别是在五层薄膜中的表现。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算和简化耦合狄拉克锥模型，通过从第一性原理计算导出的紧束缚模型评估法拉第和克尔旋转角，并与简化模型结果进行比较以阐明磁光响应的宏观机制。

Result: 研究发现五层MnBi2Te4薄膜尽管具有非零面外磁化，但根据顶层与底层七重层的相对自旋取向，可呈现拓扑陈数（Chern number）为+1的拓扑绝缘体或拓扑平庸绝缘体状态。通过比较第一性原理与简化模型结果，阐明了自旋翻转态磁光响应的宏观机制。

Conclusion: 这些理论发现突显了MnBi2Te4薄膜中拓扑和磁光性质的可调性，为层状反铁磁材料中复杂拓扑序的出现提供了微观见解。

Abstract: Magneto-optical effects like Kerr and Faraday rotations provide a direct probe of topological order in thin films of the magnetic topological insulator MnBi$_2$Te$_4$ (MBT). Motivated by recent experimental studies of spin-flip/flop transitions in MBT thin films, we investigate the interplay between interlayer spin configurations, topological order, and magneto-optical response in five septuple-layer (5-SL) MBT using first-principles calculations and a simplified coupled-Dirac-cone model. Our results reveal that, despite possessing a non-zero out-of-plane magnetization, 5-SL MBT thin films can be either ${\cal C}=+1$ topological insulators or ${\cal C}=0$ topologically trivial insulators depending on the relative spin orientations of the top and bottom SLs. We evaluate the Faraday and Kerr rotation angles using tight-binding models derived from \textit{ab-initio} calculations and by comparing our results with those of a simplified coupled Dirac-cone model clarify the macroscopic mechanisms underlying the magneto-optical response of spin-flip states. These theoretical findings highlight the tunability of topological and magneto-optical properties in MBT thin films and provide microscopic insight into the emergence of complex topological order in layered antiferromagnetic materials.

</details>


### [134] [Gate-tunable anisotropic Josephson diode effect in topological Dirac semimetal Cd$_3$As$_2$ nanowires](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09676)

Result: 观察到显著的门电压可调且高度各向异性的二极管响应，其角度依赖性可通过唯象模型准确描述。温度依赖测量成功区分了体态（bulk states）与拓扑表面态（topological surface states）对二极管效率的各自贡献。二极管效率温度依赖中的异常揭示了多个输运通道的共存。

Conclusion: 约瑟夫森二极管效应可作为探测隐藏拓扑超导态（hidden topological superconducting states）的灵敏探针。Cd₃As₂纳米线约瑟夫森结中观察到的多通道输运特性突显了该效应在揭示复杂材料系统中对称性破缺机制方面的独特价值。

Abstract: The intrinsic Josephson diode effect (JDE) has recently attracted considerable attention due to its sensitivity to broken symmetries in Josephson junctions, offering a powerful probe for uncovering hidden symmetry-breaking mechanisms in materials. The presence of higher-harmonic components in the current-phase relation, together with spin-orbital coupling, makes topological materials ideal platforms to explore this effect. In this work, we present a systematic study of the JDE in type-I topological Dirac semimetal Cd$_3$As$_2$ nanowire-based Josephson junctions. We observe a pronounced gate-tunable and highly anisotropic diode response under different magnetic-field orientations. By developing a comprehensive phenomenological model, we capture the angular dependence of the diode effect and, through temperature-dependent measurements, disentangle the respective contributions from bulk and topological surface states. Notably, anomalies in the temperature dependence of the diode efficiency reveal the coexistence of multiple transport channels, highlighting the Josephson diode effect as a sensitive probe of hidden topological superconducting states.

### [135] [Microscopic origin of $p$-wave magnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09736)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解释$P$-, $f$-, 或$h$-波反交错磁体中观察到的非相对论性大自旋劈裂现象，这种劈裂在动量空间中产生面外自旋极化，且垂直于共面非共线局域磁矩。需要从微观层面阐明这种非常规自旋极化的物理起源。

Method: 通过模型推导证明面外动量空间自旋极化与共面非共线自旋序的实空间叉积成正比，同时采用第一性原理计算（ab initio calculations）在候选材料CeNiAsO中进行验证。建立了所有自旋双位点紧束缚哈密顿量（spinful two-site tight-binding Hamiltonians）自旋极化的通用分类和解析表达式。

Result: 揭示了动量分辨自旋极化可作为自旋-位点耦合（spin-site coupling）产生的布洛赫态几何结构的探针。该方法能够几何区分铁磁体、交错磁体和反交错磁体，为量子化面外动量空间自旋极化和大自旋劈裂提供了定量指导。

Conclusion: 研究提供了反交错磁体的构造原理，将非常规自旋极化与先前被忽视的位点补偿自旋密度联系起来，该密度在投影到相反动量时呈反平行排列。这一发现深化了对非共线磁序系统中自旋极化机制的理解。

Abstract: $P$-, $f$-, or $h$-wave antialtermagnets yield large non-relativistic spin splitting with out-of-plane spin polarization in momentum space perpendicular to the coplanar non-collinear local magnetic moments. We provide a microscopic explanation of this unconventional spin polarization by linking it to a previously overlooked site-compensated spin density that orders antiparallel when projected onto opposite momenta. We verify this result both by model derivation of the out-of-plane momentum-space spin polarization being proportional to the direct-space cross product of the coplanar non-collinear spin order, as well as by ab initio calculations in the material candidate CeNiAsO. By providing a general classification and analytic expression for the spin polarization of all spinful two-site tight-binding Hamiltonians, we reveal the momentum-resolved spin polarization as a probe of the Bloch-state geometry arising from spin-site coupling. Furthermore, our approach allows for geometric distinction between ferro-, alter-, and antialtermagnets. Our results provide a quantitative guidance for quantized out-of-plane momentum-space spin polarization and large spin splitting, and construction principles for antialtermagnets.

### [136] [Magnetic field tuning of modulated magnetic orders in CrOCl at the two-dimensional limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09836)
*T. Riccardi,A. Pawbake,S. Badola,F. Petot,B. Grémaud,A. Saul,K. Singh,N. R. Nair,R. S. Chemban,Z. Sofer,J. Coraux,C. Faugeras*

Method: 采用磁拉曼散射光谱（magneto-Raman scattering spectroscopy）技术对CrOCl薄层进行表征，通过分析声子模式（phonon modes）的软化或硬化来探测自旋与晶格自由度（spin and atomic degrees of freedom）的耦合。

Result: 识别出与原子晶格匹配（commensurate with the atomic lattice）的磁有序相，并观察到强烈的磁致伸缩（magneto-striction）特征，推测源于交换相互作用（exchange origin）。在单层极限下，声子模式因相互作用竞争而以复杂方式显著软化或硬化，不同磁相的稳定区域（existence domains）随层数变化。

Conclusion: CrOCl薄层中自旋与晶格自由度存在强耦合，这种耦合在单层极限下依然显著，且磁相行为对层数敏感，揭示了范德华磁体中竞争相互作用对磁相稳定性的重要影响。

Abstract: Chromium oxychloride is a van der Waals magnet with intrinsic competing exchange interactions, including a strong antiferromagnetic one, source of a very rich magnetic phase diagram, with ferrimagnetic, antiferromagnetic, and canted states, up to high magnetic fields. We investigate the sequence of these magnetic phases in thin layers of CrOCl using magneto-Raman scattering spectroscopy. We identify phases whose magnetic order is commensurate with the atomic lattice, and find signatures of strong magneto-striction, presumably of exchange origin. The coupling of the spin and atomic degrees of freedom in the crystal is observed down to the single-layer limit -- phonon modes significantly soften or stiffen, in a complex way due to the competition of interactions. The existence domains of the different phases change with the number of layers.

### [137] [Higher-harmonic acoustic driving of quantum-dot optical transitions beyond Rabi-frequency resonance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09849)
*Mateusz Kuniej,Paweł Machnikowski,Michał Gawełczyk*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用高阶谐波辅助过程实现量子点声学控制的新方法，通过应变诱导的光学跃迁能量调制，在可实现的声学频率下实现高保真度量子态制备。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 声子（phonons）对量子系统的声学控制和耦合能够实现小型化量子技术器件的片上集成。光学活性量子点（quantum dots, QDs）在此类平台中至关重要，但长期以来缺乏电荷态之间的直接声学跃迁。最近提出的混合声光摆动方案引入了这种高保真度跃迁，但仅限于亚太赫兹声子频率，限制了实际应用。

Method: 通过利用应变诱导的光学跃迁能量调制产生的高阶谐波辅助过程，当机械调制的谐波与广义拉比频率（generalized Rabi frequency）匹配时，光学修饰分裂的参量调制会产生多声子类共振。该方法结合了数值模拟、有效模型和几何解释，并在非马尔可夫框架内评估了声子诱导的退相干效应。

Result: 预测了在声学频率仅为分裂频率一小部分时（例如，对于0.341 THz的分裂，使用42 GHz声学频率）能够实现高保真度量子态制备，从而将可实现的声学频率控制与太赫兹能量尺度联系起来。声子诱导退相干评估表明，该方案具有与单声子和全光学方案相当的高态制备保真度。

Conclusion: 该方法建立了将光学能量传递与相干声学控制分离的控制原理。由于相同的相互作用结构也适用于量子化声场，该结果为量子点与声子谐振器耦合中的多声子过程奠定了基础，包括量子点-声子纠缠、态转移以及量子化声学模式中非经典多声子态的光学制备，这些对于未来片上量子技术都至关重要。

Abstract: Acoustic control and coupling of quantum systems via phonons can enable miniaturized quantum technology devices for on-chip integration. Optically active quantum dots (QDs) are essential for such platforms, yet they have long lacked direct acoustic transitions between charge states. The recently proposed hybrid acousto-optical swing-up scheme introduces such high-fidelity transitions but has been proposed for sub-THz phonon frequencies, limiting practical implementations. Here, we overcome this limitation by exploiting higher-harmonic-assisted processes arising from strain-induced modulation of the optical transition energy. This parametric modulation of the optically dressed splitting produces multi-phonon-like resonances when a harmonic of the mechanical modulation matches the generalized Rabi frequency. We predict faithful state preparation with an acoustic frequency that is only a fraction of this splitting, specifically 42 GHz for a 0.341 THz splitting, thereby bridging control at accessible acoustic frequencies with the THz energy scales. In doing so, we establish control principles that separate optical energy delivery from coherent acoustic control. We complement numerical simulations with an effective model and a geometric interpretation. Evaluation of phonon-induced decoherence within a non-Markovian framework indicates high state-preparation fidelities, comparable to one-phonon and all-optical schemes. Potential applications extend beyond QD charge state preparation. Since the same interaction structure arises for a quantized acoustic field, our results provide a foundation for multi-phonon processes in QDs coupled to phononic resonators, including QD-phonon entanglement, state transfer, and the optical preparation of nonclassical multi-phonon states in quantized acoustic modes, all essential for future on-chip quantum technologies.

</details>

### [138] [Weyl-Transition-Driven Giant Reversible Orbital Hall Conductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08851)
*Bo Zhao,Hao Wang,Wei Ren,Hongbin Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文发现倾斜外尔交叉点（tilted Weyl crossings）通过产生不对称的轨道贝里曲率（orbital Berry curvature）分布，能够在布里渊区积分后形成显著的非平衡，从而产生巨大的轨道霍尔电导率（orbital Hall conductivity）。在PtBi₂单层材料中，通过双轴拉伸应变可实现外尔点类型转变，进而可逆地调控轨道霍尔电导率的符号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轨道霍尔电导率（orbital Hall conductivity）是轨道电子学（orbitronics）的核心要素，但其微观调控机制尚未得到充分探索。论文旨在发现一种通用机制，能够生成并可逆控制轨道霍尔电导率。

Method: 论文通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）研究了PtBi₂单层材料。采用双轴拉伸应变（biaxial tensile strain）驱动外尔点从type-II到type-I再到type-II的转变，分析轨道贝里曲率（orbital Berry curvature）分布的不对称性及其演化。

Result: PtBi₂单层材料实现了所提出的机制，其巨大的轨道霍尔电导率主要由type-II外尔点（type-II Weyl point）主导。应变驱动的外尔转变（Weyl transition）导致轨道贝里曲率不平衡的演化，进而引起轨道霍尔电导率的可逆符号变化。这一过程受交叉能带的手性轨道纹理（chiral orbital texture）控制，并得到应变诱导的一级结构相变（first-order structural phase transition）的辅助。

Conclusion: 研究确立了外尔工程（Weyl engineering）作为在极性多轨道材料（polar multi-orbital materials）中生成并可逆控制轨道霍尔电导率的有效途径。通过调控轨道量子几何（orbital quantum geometry），可以实现对轨道霍尔效应的精细控制。

Abstract: Orbital Hall conductivity (OHC) is a central ingredient of orbitronics, yet how to control it microscopically remains largely unexplored. Here we identify a general mechanism in which tilted Weyl crossings formed by orbitally distinct bands generate a strongly asymmetric orbital Berry curvature (OBC) distribution, whose imbalance survives Brillouin-zone integration and yields a sizable OHC already at zeroth order. Using first-principles calculations, we show that monolayer PtBi2 realizes this mechanism and hosts a giant OHC dominated by a type-II Weyl point. A small biaxial tensile strain drives a type-II $\rightarrow$ type-I $\rightarrow$ type-II Weyl transition, leading to a reversible sign change of the OHC through the evolution of the OBC imbalance. This process is governed by the chiral orbital texture of the crossing bands and is further assisted by a strain-induced first-order structural phase transition through bonding reconstruction and polarization change. Our results establish Weyl engineering of orbital quantum geometry as a powerful route to generating and reversibly controlling OHC in polar multi-orbital materials.

</details>


### [139] [Ground-State Structure Search of Defective High-Entropy Alloys Using Machine-Learning Potentials and Monte Carlo Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08855)
*Siya Zhu,Raymundo Arroyave*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了PAIPAI框架，这是一个结合机器学习原子间势（MLIPs）的蒙特卡洛方法，用于高效搜索含缺陷和间隙原子的高熵合金（HEAs）的基态原子构型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于巨大的构型空间和现有方法的局限性，解析含有间隙原子的缺陷高熵合金（HEAs）的原子尺度结构仍然是一个主要的计算挑战。

Method: PAIPAI框架采用蒙特卡洛方法与机器学习原子间势（MLIPs）相结合，并设计了双工作者架构——快速工作者用于快速构型筛选，慢速工作者用于高精度优化，通过共享等待池协调实现高效并行采样。

Result: 通过三个案例研究验证了PAIPAI的有效性：Ti-V-Cr-Re板表面偏析、BCC Nb-Ti-Ta-Hf块体中氧和硼间隙原子聚集、以及Nb-Ti-Ta-Hf晶界处的金属和间隙原子耦合偏析。在所有案例中，蒙特卡洛优化的结构能量显著低于随机采样获得的任何构型，且MLIP能量排序与密度泛函理论（DFT）计算结果一致。

Conclusion: PAIPAI为预测复杂缺陷高熵合金系统中的原子有序化、偏析和间隙原子行为提供了一个通用且高效的框架。

Abstract: Resolving the atomic-scale structure of defective high-entropy alloys (HEAs) containing interstitial species remains a major computational challenge due to the vast configurational space and the limitations of existing methods. Here we introduce PAIPAI (Package for Alloy Interstitial Predictions using Artificial Intelligence), a Monte Carlo framework coupled with machine-learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) that searches for ground-state atomic configurations in HEAs with defects and interstitials. PAIPAI employs a dual-worker architecture-fast workers for rapid configurational screening and slow workers for high-accuracy refinement-coordinated through a shared waiting pool, enabling efficient parallel sampling. We demonstrate PAIPAI through three case studies: (i) surface segregation in a Ti-V-Cr-Re slab; (ii) interstitial oxygen and boron aggregation in bulk BCC Nb-Ti-Ta-Hf; and (iii) coupled metallic and interstitial segregation at grain boundaries in Nb-Ti-Ta-Hf. In all cases, Monte Carlo-optimized structures are significantly lower in energy than any configuration obtained by random sampling, and MLIP energy rankings are validated against density functional theory calculations. PAIPAI provides a general and efficient framework for predicting atomic ordering, segregation, and interstitial behavior in complex, defective HEA systems.

</details>


### [140] [Uncovering the properties of homo-epitaxial GaN devices through cross-sectional infrared nanoscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08858)

Conclusion: 散射型扫描近场光学显微镜（s-SNOM）能够满足表征同质外延GaN器件的严苛性能要求，通过结合中红外和太赫兹光谱范围可区分载流子和晶格变化，在半导体器件表征中展现出优越的分辨率和灵敏度。

This work demonstrates that scattering-type scanning near-field optical microscopy (s-SNOM) can meet the demanding performance requirements for characterizing homoepitaxial GaN devices. Specifically, we show that combining s-SNOM results in the mid-IR and terahertz (THz) spectral ranges can disentangle carrier and lattice changes in a GaN p-i-n diode, which is not possible using one spectral range alone. We observe strong, resonant near-field signals near the LO phonon mode of GaN that correlate well with point-dipole models. This data shows great sensitivity to the local carrier density, with changes on the order of 1018 cm-3 easily resolved experimentally. Further, we demonstrate high sensitivity to sub-surface defects, which remain a significant challenge for other non-destructive techniques. To validate the power of s-SNOM imaging, our results are compared to traditional metrologies, including micro-Raman mapping and Kelvin Probe Force Microscopy (KPFM). Our results show that s-SNOM shows superior resolution and sensitivity to perturbations, highlighting the power of this technique in semiconductor device characterization.

### [141] [Aligning van der Waals heterostructures using electron backscatter diffraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08872)

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究展示了电子背散射衍射（EBSD）作为精确测定范德华材料晶体取向的通用工具，精度优于0.2°，并成功应用于精确控制扭转角的α-MoO₃异质结构工程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确测定晶体学取向对于范德华异质结构工程至关重要，因为层间扭转角控制着新奇的电子和光学性质。虽然电子背散射衍射（EBSD）已广泛用于块体材料，但其在范德华材料中的应用尚未充分探索。

Method: 本研究将EBSD作为精确测定范德华材料晶体取向的通用工具，通过晶粒参考取向分布（GROD）和核平均取向差（KAM）分析实现优于0.2°的精度。该方法扩展应用于多种低对称性材料，包括单斜α-As₂Te₃、单斜GaTe和三斜ReSe₂。

Result: 研究展示了EBSD测定的取向与硅衬底上正交α-MoO₃薄片晶面取向之间的定量一致性。作为概念验证应用，利用EBSD测定的取向工程化制备了具有精确控制扭转角的扭转α-MoO₃异质结构，实现了最近报道的沟道化声子极化激元观测。

Conclusion: 本研究确立了EBSD作为范德华材料表征的强大方法，为实现扭转电子学（twistronics）和扭转光学（twist-optics）所需的精确取向控制提供了关键工具。

Abstract: Precise and accurate determination of crystallographic orientation is crucial for engineering van der Waals heterostructures, where the twist angle between layers controls emergent electronic and optical properties. While Electron Backscatter Diffraction (EBSD) has been extensively used for bulk materials, its application to van der Waals materials remains largely unexplored. In this work, we demonstrate EBSD as a robust and versatile tool for determining crystallographic orientations of van der Waals materials with high precision. We show quantitative agreement between EBSD-determined orientations and facet orientations in orthorhombic α-MoO3 flakes on silicon substrates. We use Grain Reference Orientation Distribution (GROD) and Kernel Average Misorientation (KAM) across the flakes to demonstrate precision better than 0.2°. We extend this technique to other low-symmetry materials, specifically, monoclinic α-As2Te3, monoclinic GaTe and triclinic ReSe2, demonstrating broad applicability across van der Waals materials with different crystal structures. Finally, as a proof-of-concept application, we leverage EBSD-determined orientations to engineer twisted α-MoO3 heterostructure with precisely controlled twist angle, enabling observation of recently reported canalized phonon polaritons. Our results establish EBSD as a powerful characterization method for van der Waals materials, enabling precise orientation control essential for twistronics and twist-optics.

We compare a corpus-trained Word2Vec baseline with transformer-based embeddings, where compositions are encoded either by linear element-wise mixing or by short composition prompts. Similarities to `concept directions', the terms conductivity and dielectric, define a 2-dimensional descriptor space, and a symmetric Pareto-front selection is used to filter candidate subsets without using electrochemical labels. Performance is assessed on 15 materials libraries including noble metal alloys and multicomponent oxides. However, the microscopic mechanisms governing such hydrogenation reactions remain poorly understood. Here, we show that machine-learning potential molecular dynamics (MLP-MD) simulations can reproduce and distinguish competing reaction pathways leading to metastable and stable hydrides. By simulating hydrogenation reactions at CaH$_2$/H$_2$ and CaH$_4$/H$_2$ interfaces, we identify two distinct pathways that produce clathrate-type CaH$_6$ and A15-type CaH$_{5.75}$, respectively. CaH$_{5.75}$ lies on the convex hull but requires extensive Ca sublattice rearrangement and therefore forms only at elevated temperatures. In contrast, CaH$_6$ becomes kinetically accessible when CaH$_2$ is used as the precursor. The crystallographic compatibility between the Ca sublattice of CaH$_2$ and the bcc framework of CaH$_6$ enables a martensitic-like topotactic transformation that bypasses the reconstructive pathway leading to CaH$_{5.75}$. These results reveal how precursor structure and thermodynamic stability compete to determine superhydride formation pathways and demonstrate that machine-learning molecular dynamics can directly capture the kinetic selection of metastable phases in reactive materials systems.

They behave as particle-like entities while retaining a fully reconfigurable optical response. Here it is shown experimentally that individual torons can be created, steered and parked on demand using tailored alternating-current electric fields in planar cells, enabling deterministic control of both position and trajectory. By tuning the ratio of cell thickness to cholesteric pitch and systematically adjusting waveform parameters, including amplitude, modulation frequency, duty-cycle asymmetry and small DC offsets, robust toron nucleation is achieved and programmable translation is realised along arbitrary in-plane directions with submicrometre placement accuracy. Directional transport is controlled within a defined frequency and temperature window and can be reversed by changing modulation conditions even at zero offset. A dedicated graphical interface enables real-time switching between waveform presets so that torons follow scripted paths and draw user-defined shapes. Quantitative Landau-de Gennes Q-tensor simulations reproduce toron nucleation and the ensuing translational dynamics, supporting an interpretation in which waveform-controlled director reorientation, reorientation-driven flow and rectified polarity-sensitive coupling jointly bias the drift. Finally, three proof-of-concept functions are demonstrated: a software-defined liquid-crystal racetrack memory analogue with optical readout, deterministic path writing for reconfigurable patterning, and toron-mediated pick-and-place transport of microparticles for micromanipulation.

Conclusion: XMLD和XMCD可作为元素特异性探针，用于探测交变磁体中的磁弹性多极子序。该研究提供了基于对称性的通用途径，以识别超越传统铁磁性的隐藏铁性多极子和应变可控自旋现象。

Abstract: Recent developments in the multipole reformulation of X-ray absorption spectroscopy (XAS) have provided a unified framework to describe magnetic and orbital responses in terms of ferroic multipole order parameters. X-ray magnetic circular dichroism (XMCD) is known to probe spin, orbital, and anisotropic magnetic dipole (AMD) moments. Its applications to altermagnets and noncollinear antiferromagnets have revealed that the XMCD response is often governed by the ferroic states of the AMD in the photo-excited states rather than by conventional magnetic dipoles in the ground states. In this work, we extend the multipole-based analysis to X-ray magnetic linear dichroism (XMLD) and demonstrate that XMLD in altermagnets can be understood as a manifestation of piezomagnetic effects: linear couplings between magnetic dipole and electric quadrupole moments. Using symmetry analysis combined with exact diagonalization calculations of $L_{2,3}$-edge XAS, we systematically investigate representative altermagnets, including $α$-MnTe, MnF$_2$, and CrSb. We show that the ferroic ordering of higher-rank magnetic multipoles, particularly spinful magnetic octupoles, gives rise to characteristic field-odd XMLD signals that directly reflect the underlying piezomagnetic response tensors allowed by magnetic point-group symmetry. Furthermore, we discuss XMCD signals induced by piezomagnetic effects, in which strain generates magnetic dipole moments. Our results establish XMLD and XMCD as element-specific probes of magnetoelastic multipole order in altermagnets and provide a general symmetry-based pathway to identify hidden ferroic multipoles and strain-controllable spin phenomena beyond conventional ferromagnetism.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用π矩阵方法（π-matrix method）计算材料特定的朗道能级（Landau levels），并评估包含完整带间效应的磁化强度。引入自由-塞曼-狄拉克模型（free-Zeeman-Dirac, fZD model）拟合计算得到的朗道能级参数。

Result: 系统在x=0和x=0.35时均表现出抗磁性（diamagnetism），后者由于带隙更小而响应更强。抗磁性大小随SOC强度单调增加，在强磁场中尤为显著。分析表明SOC增强了狄拉克型带间贡献（Dirac-type interband contribution）相对于塞曼项（Zeeman term）的比例。
